<sup>31:21</sup>&nbsp;He turned, kissed him again, and hugged him. He was very happy that he had seen the sons of his true son Jacob. <sup>31:22</sup>&nbsp;He moved out from between his feet, fell down, and bowed to him. He then blessed them. He rested there near his father Isaac that night. They ate and drank happily. <sup>31:23</sup>&nbsp;He made Jacob's two sons sleep, one on his right, one on his left; and it was credited to him as something righteous.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>31:24</sup>&nbsp;ወነገረ ያዕቆብ ኵሎ ለአቡሁ በሌሊት ዘከመ ገብረ እግዚአብሔር ምስሌሁ ሣህለ ዐቢይ። ወከመ ሠርሐ ኵሎ ፍናዊሁ ወተማኅፀኖ እምኵሉ እኩይ <sup>31:25</sup>&nbsp;ወባረከ ይስሐቅ አምላከ አቡሁ አብርሃም ዘኢኀደገ ምሕረቶ ወጽድቆ እምወልደ ገብሩ ይስሐቅ። <sup>31:26</sup>&nbsp;ወበነግህ ነገረ ያዕቆብ ለአቡሁ ይስሐቅ ጸሎተ ዘጸለየ ለእግዚአብሔር ወራእየ ዘርእየ ወከመ ሐነጸ ምሥዋዐ ወኵሉ ድልው ለመሥዋዕት ለገቢር ቅድመ እግዚአብሔር በከመ ጸለየ ወከመ መጽአ ይጽዐኖ ዲበ አድግ። <sup>31:27</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤ ይስሐቅ ለያዕቆብ ወልዱ ኢይክል መጺአ ምስሌከ እስመ ረሣእኩ ወኢይክል ተዐግሦ በፍኖት ሖር ወልድየ በሰላም እስመ ወልደ ምእት ወስሳ ወኀምስቱ ዓመት አነ። ዮም ኢይክል እንከ ነጊደ ጸዐና ለእምከ ወትሖር ምስሌከ <sup>31:28</sup>&nbsp;ወአአምር አነ ወልድየ ከመሰ በእንቲአየ መጻእከ። ወዛቲ ዕለት ትኩን ቡርክተ እንተ ባቲ ርኢከኒ ሕያውየ ወርኢኩከ አነሂ ወልድየ <sup>31:29</sup>&nbsp;ወተሰራሕ ወግበር ጸሎተ እንተ ጸለይከ ወኢታጐንዲ ጸሎተከ እስመ ትትኃሠሥ ጸሎተ። ወይእዜኒ ጐጕእ ትግበራ ወይሥመር ዘገብረ ኵሎ ለዘ ጸለይከ ጸሎተ። <sup>31:30</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤላ ለርብቃ ሖሪ ምስለ ያዕቆብ ወልድኪ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>31:24</sup>&nbsp;That night Jacob told his father everything — how the Lord had shown him great kindness, that he had directed all his ways favorably and had protected him from every evil one. <sup>31:25</sup>&nbsp;Isaac blessed the God of his father Abraham who had not put an end to his mercy and faithfulness for the son of his servant Isaac. <sup>31:26</sup>&nbsp;In the morning Jacob told his father Isaac the vow that he had made to the Lord, the vision that he had seen, that he had built an altar and everything was ready for offering the sacrifice before the Lord as he had vowed, and that he had come to put him on a donkey. <sup>31:27</sup>&nbsp;But Isaac said to his son Jacob: 'I am unable to come with you because I am old and unable to put up with the trip. Go safely, my son, because I am 165 years of age today. I am no longer able to travel. Put your mother on an animal and let her go with you. <sup>31:28</sup>&nbsp;I know, my son, that it was on my account that you came. Blessed be this day on which you have seen me alive and I, too, have seen you, my son. <sup>31:29</sup>&nbsp;Be successful and carry out the vow that you made. Do not delay (in carrying out) your vow because you will be held accountable regarding the vow. Now hurry to perform it. May the one who has made everything, to whom you made the vow, be pleased (with it)'. <sup>31:30</sup>&nbsp;He said to Rebecca: 'Go with your son Jacob'.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
ወሖረት ርብቃ ምስለ ያዕቆብ ወልዳ ወዲቦራ ምስሌሃ ወበጽሑ ውስተ ቤቴል። <sup>31:31</sup>&nbsp;ወተዘከረ ያዕቆብ ጸሎተ እንተ ባረኮ አቡሁ ወክልኤተ ውሉዶ ሌዊሃ ወይሁዳሃ ወተፈሥሐ ወባረኮ ለአምላከ አበዊሁ አብርሃም ወይስሐቅ። <sup>31:32</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤ ይእዜ አእመርኩ ከመ ብየ ተስፋ ዘለዓለም ወለውሉድየሂ በቅድመ አምላከ ኵሉ ወከመዝ ሥሩዕ በእንተ ክልኤሆሙ ወያዐርጉ ሎሙ በስምዕ ዘለዓለም ውስተ ጽላተ ሰማይ በከመ ባረኮሙ ይስሐቅ።
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
So Rebecca went with her son Jacob and Deborah with her. They arrived at Bethel. <sup>31:31</sup>&nbsp;When Jacob recalled the prayer with which his father had blessed him and his two sons — Levi and Judah — he was very happy and blessed the God of his fathers Abraham and Isaac. <sup>31:32</sup>&nbsp;He said: 'Now I know that I and my sons, too, have an eternal hope before the God of all'. This is the way it is ordained regarding the two of them, and it is entered for them as an eternal testimony on the heavenly tablets just as Isaac blessed them.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>32:1</sup>&nbsp;ወኀደረ በይእቲ ሌሊት ውስተ ቤቴል ወሐለመ ሌዊ ከመ ሤምዎ ወረሰይዎ ለክህነት ለአምላክ ልዑል ኪያሁ ወውሉዶ እስከ ለዓለም። ወነቅሀ እምንዋሙ ወባረኮ ለእግዚአብሔር። <sup>32:2</sup>&nbsp;ወጌሰ ያዕቆብ በነግህ አመ ዐሡሩ ወረቡዑ ለዝ ወርኅ። ወዐሠረ እምኵሉ ዘመጽአ ምስሌሁ እምሰብእ እስከ እንስሳ እምወርቅ እስከ ኵሉ ንዋይ ወልብስ ወዐሠረ እምኵሉ። <sup>32:3</sup>&nbsp;ወበውእቶን መዋዕል ፀንሰት ይእቲ ራሔል ብንያምሃ ወልዳ ወኆለቈ እምኔሁ ያዕቆብ ወልዶ። ወዐርገ ወወረደ ላዕሌሁ ለሌዊ በመክፈልተ እግዚአብሔር ወአልበሶ አቡሁ አልባሰ ክህነት ወመልአ እደዊሁ። <sup>32:4</sup>&nbsp;ወአመ ወሡሩ ወኀሙሱ ለዝ ወርኅ አብአ ውስተ ምሥዋዕ አስዋረ እምአልህምት ዐሠርተ ወአርባዕተ ወአብሐኰ ዕሥራ ወሰማኒተ ወአባግዐ አርብዓ ወተስዐተ ወመሓስአ ስሳ ወመሓስአ ጠሊ ዕሥራ ወተስዐተ ጽንሐሐ ውስተ ምሥዋዕ ወቍርባነ ሥሙረ ለመዓዛ ሠናይ ቅድመ አምላክ። <sup>32:5</sup>&nbsp;ዝውእቱ መባኡ እምጸሎት እንተ ጸለየ ከመ የዐሥር ምስለ መሥዋዕቶሙ ወለሞጻሕቶሙ። <sup>32:6</sup>&nbsp;ወሶበ በልዖ እሳት የዐጥን ስኂነ ዲቤሁ ለእሳት መልዕልቶ። ወለመሥዋዕተ መድኃኒት አስዋረ ክልኤተ ወአብሐኰ አርባዕተ ወአባግዐ አርባዕተ ዳቤላተ አርባዕተ አባግዐ ዘዘ ዓመት ክልኤተ ወመሓስአ ጠሊ ክልኤተ። ከመዝ ይገብር እንተ ጸብሐት ሰቡዐ መዋዕለ <sup>32:7</sup>&nbsp;ወሀሎ እንዘ ይበልዕ ውእቱ ወኵሎሙ ውሉዱ ወሰብኡ በፍሥሓ በህየ ሰቡዐ መዋዕለ ወይባርኮ ወያአኵቶ ለእግዚአብሔር ለዘ ባልሖ እምኵሉ ምንዳቤሁ ወለዘ ወሀቦ ጸሎቶ። <sup>32:8</sup>&nbsp;ወዐሠረ ኵሎ እንስሳ ንጹሐ ወገብሮ ጽንሐሐ ወእንስሳ ርኩሰ ወሀቦ ለሌዊ ወልዱ ወነፍሳተ ሰብእ ኵሎ ወሀቦ። <sup>32:9</sup>&nbsp;ወተክህነ ሌዊ በቤቴል ቅድመ ያዕቆብ አቡሁ እምዐሠርቱ አኃዊሁ ወሀሎ ህየ ካህነ። ወያዕቆብ ወሀበ ጸሎቶ ከመዝ ዐሠረ ዳግመ ዓሥራተ ለእግዚአብሔር ወቀደሶ ወኮነ ቅዱሰ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>32:1</sup>&nbsp;That night he stayed at Bethel. Levi dreamed that he — he and his sons — had been appointed and made into the priesthood of the most high God forever. When he awakened, he blessed the Lord. <sup>32:2</sup>&nbsp;Jacob got up early in the morning on the fourteenth day of this month and gave a tithe of everything which had come with him — from people to animals, from money to all utensils and clothing. He gave a tithe of everything. <sup>32:3</sup>&nbsp;At that time that Rachel became pregnant with her son Benjamin. Jacob counted his sons from him. He went up (the hst), and it came down on Levi in the Lord's share. His father put priestly clothes on him and ordained him. <sup>32:4</sup>&nbsp;On the fifteenth of this month he brought to the altar 14 young bulls from the cattle, 28 rams, 49 sheep, 7 kids, and 21 goats — as a burnt offering on the altar and as a pleasing offering for a pleasant aroma before God. <sup>32:5</sup>&nbsp;This was his gift because of the vow which he had made that he would give a tithe along with their sacrifices and their libations. <sup>32:6</sup>&nbsp;When the fire had consumed it, he would burn incense on the fire above it; and as a peace offering two young bulls, four rams, four sheep, four he-goats, two year-old sheep, and two goats. This is what he would do daily for the seven days. <sup>32:7</sup>&nbsp;He was eating happily there — he, all his sons, and his men — for the seven days. He was blessing and praising the Lord who had freed him from all his difficulties and who had granted him his vow. <sup>32:8</sup>&nbsp;He tithed all the clean animals and made an offering of them. He gave his son Levi the unclean animals and gave him all the persons of the men. <sup>32:9</sup>&nbsp;Levi rather than his ten brothers served as priest in Bethel before his father Jacob. There he was a priest, and Jacob gave what he had vowed. In this way he again gave a tithe to the Lord. He sanctified it, and it became holy.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>32:10</sup>&nbsp;ወበእንተዝ ሥሩዕ ውስተ ጽላተ ሰማይ ሕግ ለዐሥሮ ዓሥራት ካዕበ ለበሊዖቱ በቅድመ እግዚአብሔር በመካን በኀበ ተኀርየ ይኅድር ስሙ ላዕሌሁ ዓም እምዓም። ወአልቦ ለዝ ሕግ ዐቅመ መዋዕል ለዓለም <sup>32:11</sup>&nbsp;ውእቱ ሥርዐት ጽሑፍ ለገቢሮቱ ዓመት እምዓመት ለበሊዐ ዓሥራት ዳግመ ቅድመ እግዚአብሔር በመካን በኀበ ተኀርየ። ወአልቦ ለአትርፎ እምኔሁ እምዝ ዓመት ለዓመት ለዘ ይመጽእ <sup>32:12</sup>&nbsp;እስመ በዓመቲሁ ይትበላዕ ዘርእ እስከ አመ መዋዕለ ሐሪፍ ዘርአ ዓመት ወወይን እስከ አመ መዋዕለ ወይን ወለዘይት እስከ አመ መዋዕለ ጊዜ መዋዕሊሁ። <sup>32:13</sup>&nbsp;ኵሉ ዘይተርፍ እምኔሁ ወዘይበሊ ይኩን ስኡበ በእሳት የዐይ እስመ ኮነ ርኩሰ <sup>32:14</sup>&nbsp;ወከማሁ ይብልዕዎ ኅቡረ በቤት ቅዱስ ወኢያብልይዎ <sup>32:15</sup>&nbsp;ወኵሉ ዓሥራተ ላህም ወአባግዕ ቅዱስ ለእግዚአብሔር ወለካህናቲሁ ይኩን ዘይበልዑ በቅድሜሁ ዓመት እምዓመት። እስመ ከማሁ ሥሩዕ ወቍሩጽ በእንተ ዓሥራት ውስተ ጽላተ ሰማይ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>32:10</sup>&nbsp;For this reason it is ordained as a law on the heavenly tablets to tithe a second time, to eat it before the Lord — year by year — in the place which has been chosen (as the site) where his name will reside. This law has no temporal limits forever. <sup>32:11</sup>&nbsp;That statute has been written down so that it should be carried out year by year — to eat the tithe a second time before the Lord in the place that has been chosen. One is not to leave any of it over from this year to the next year. <sup>32:12</sup>&nbsp;For the seed is to be eaten in its year until the time for harvesting the seed of the year; the wine (will be drunk) until the time for wine; and the olive (will be used) until the proper time of its season. <sup>32:13</sup>&nbsp;Any of it that is left over and grows old is to be (considered) contaminated; it is to be burned up because it has become impure, <sup>32:14</sup>&nbsp;In this way they are to eat it at the same time in the sanctuary; they are not to let it grow old. <sup>32:15</sup>&nbsp;The entire tithe of cattle and sheep is holy to the Lord, and is to belong to his priests who will eat (it) before him year by year, because this is the way it is ordained and inscribed on the heavenly tablets regarding the tithe.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>32:16</sup>&nbsp;ወበሌሊት ካልእት አመ ዕሥራ ወሰኑዩ ለመዋዕለ ዝወርኅ መከረ ያዕቆብ ከመ ይሕንጽ ውእተ መካነ ወከመ ይጥቅም ዐጸደ ወይቀድሶ ወከመ ይግበሮ ቅዱሰ ዘለዓለም ሎቱ ወለውሉዱ እስከ ለዓለም እምድኅሬሁ። <sup>32:17</sup>&nbsp;ወአስተርአዮ እግዚአብሔር በሌሊት ወባረኮ ወይቤሎ ኢይጸዋዕ ስምከ ያዕቆብሃ ባሕቲቶ አላ እስራኤልሃ ይሰምዩ ስምከ። <sup>32:18</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤሎ ካዕበ አነ ውእቱ እግዚአብሔር ዘፈጠርኩ ሰማየ ወምድረ ወአልህቀከ ወአበዝኀከ ፈድፋደ ጥቀ ወነገሥት እምኔከ ይከውኑ ወይኴንኑ በኵለሄ ወእደ ኬደ አሰረ ውሉደ ሰብእ። <sup>32:19</sup>&nbsp;ወእሁብ ለዘርእከ ኵላ ምድረ ዘመትሕተ ሰማይ ወይኴንኑ ውስተ ኵሉ አሕዛብ በከመ ፈቀዱ ወእምድኅረዝ ያስተጋብኡ ኵላ ምድረ ወይወርስዋ ለዓለም <sup>32:20</sup>&nbsp;ወፈጸመ ተናገሮ ምስሌሁ ወዐርገ እምኀቤሁ ወይሬኢ ያዕቆብ እስከ ሶበ ዐርገ ውስተ ሰማይ። <sup>32:21</sup>&nbsp;ወርእየ በራእየ ሌሊት ወናሁ መልአክ ይወርድ እምሰማይ ወሰብዑ ሰሌዳት ውስተ እደዊሁ ወወሀቦ ለያዕቆብ ወአንበቦን ወአንበበ ኵሎ ዘጽሑፍ ውስቴቶን ዘይከውን ሎቱ ወለውሉዱ በኩሉ ዓለማት። <sup>32:22</sup>&nbsp;ወአርአዮ ኵሎ ዘጽሑፍ ውስተ ሰሌዳት ወይቤሎ ኢትሕንጽ ዘንተ መካነ ወኢትግበሮ መቅደሰ ዘለዓለም ወኢትኅድር ዝየ እስመ አኮ ዝመካን። ሖር ቤተ አብርሃም አቡከ ወኅድር ኀበ ይስሐቅ አቡከ ህየ እስከ አመ ዕለተ ሞቱ ለአቡከ። <sup>32:23</sup>&nbsp;እስመ በግብጽ ትመውት በሰላም ወበዛ ምድር ትትቀበር በክብር ውስተ መቃብረ አበዊከ ምስለ አብርሃም ወይስሐቅ። <sup>32:24</sup>&nbsp;ኢትፍራህ እስመ በከመ ርኢከ ወአንበብከ ከማሁ ይከውን ኵሉ ወአንተሂ ጸሐፍ ኵሎ ዘከመ ርኢከ ወአንበብከ <sup>32:25</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤ ያዕቆብ እግዚኦ እፎ እዜከር ዘከመ አንበብኩ ወርኢኩ ኵሎ። ወይቤሎ አነ አዜክረከ ኵሎ። <sup>32:26</sup>&nbsp;ወዐርገ እምኀቤሁ። ወነቅሀ እምንዋሙ ወተዘከረ ኵሎ ዘአንበበ ወዘርእየ ወጸሐፈ ኵሎ ነገረ ዘአንበበ ወዘርእየ <sup>32:27</sup>&nbsp;ወገብረ በህየ ዓዲ ዕለተ አሐተ ወሦዐ ባቲ በከመ ኵሉ ዘይሠውዕ በመዋዕለ ቀዳሚያት ወጸውዐ ስማ ቶሳከ እስመ ተወሰከት ይእቲ ዕለት ወለቀዳሚያት ጸውዖን በዓለ። <sup>32:28</sup>&nbsp;ወከመዝ ያስተርኢ ውእቱ ከመ ትኩን ወጽሑፍ ውስተ ጽላተ ሰማይ። በእንተዝ ተከሥተ ሎቱ ከመ ይግበራ ወከመ ይወስክ ዲበ ሰብዑ መዋዕለ በዓል ኪያሃ <sup>32:29</sup>&nbsp;ወተጸውዐ ስማ ቶሳከ እስመ እንተ ያዐርጉ ይእቲ በስምዐ መዋዕለ በዓል በከመ ኆልቈ መዋዕል ዘዓመት 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>32:16</sup>&nbsp;During the next night, on the twenty-second day of this month, Jacob decided to build up that place and to surround the courtyard with a wall, to sanctify it, and make it eternally holy for himself and for his children after him forever. <sup>32:17</sup>&nbsp;The Lord appeared to him during the night. He blessed him and said to him: 'You are not to be called Jacob only but you will (also) be named Israel'. <sup>32:18</sup>&nbsp;He said to him a second time: 'I am the Lord who created heaven and earth. I will increase your numbers and multiply you very much. Kings will come from you, and they will rule wherever mankind has set foot. <sup>32:19</sup>&nbsp;I will give your descendants all of the land that is beneath the sky. They will rule over all the nations just as they wish. Afterwards, they will gain the entire earth, and they will possess it forever'. <sup>32:20</sup>&nbsp;When he had finished speaking with him, he went up from him, and Jacob kept watching until he had gone up into heaven. <sup>32:21</sup>&nbsp;In a night vision he saw an angel coming down from heaven with seven tablets in his hands. He gave (them) to Jacob, and he read them. He read everything that was written in them — what would happen to him and his sons throughout all ages. <sup>32:22</sup>&nbsp;After he had shown him everything that was written on the tablets, he said to him: 'Do not build up this place, and do not make it an eternal temple. Do not live here because this is not the place. Go to the house of your father Abraham and live where your father Isaac is until the day of your father's death. <sup>32:23</sup>&nbsp;For you will die peacefully in Egypt and be buried honorably in this land in the grave of your fathers — with Abraham and Isaac. <sup>32:24</sup>&nbsp;Do not be afraid because everything will happen just as you have seen and read. Now you write down everything just as you have seen and read'. <sup>32:25</sup>&nbsp;Then Jacob said: 'Lord, how shall I remember everything just as I have read and seen'? He said to him: 'I will remind you of everything'. <sup>32:26</sup>&nbsp;When he had gone from him, he awakened and remembered everything that he had read and seen. He wrote down all the things that he had read and seen. <sup>32:27</sup>&nbsp;He celebrated one more day there. On it he sacrificed exactly as he had been sacrificing on the previous days. He named it Addition because that day was added. He named the previous ones the Festival. <sup>32:28</sup>&nbsp;This is the way it was revealed that it should be, and it is written on the heavenly tablets. For this reason it was revealed to him that he should celebrate it and add it to the seven days of the festival. <sup>32:29</sup>&nbsp;It was called Addition because of the fact that it is entered in the testimony of the festal days in accord with the number of days in the year.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>32:30</sup>&nbsp;ወበሌሊት አመ ዕሥራ ወሠሉሱ ለዝ ወርኅ ሞተት ዲቦራ ሐፃኒተ ርብቃ ወቀበርዋ መትሕተ ሀገር ታሕተ ባላን ዘፈለግ ወጸውዐ ስሞ ለውእቱ መካን ፈለገ ዲቦራ ወበላኖንሃ በላኖን ለሐ ዲቦራ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>32:30</sup>&nbsp;That night, on the twenty-third of this month, Deborah, Rebecca's nurse, died. They buried her below the city, beneath the oak (near) the stream. He named that place the Stream of Deborah and the oak the Oak of Mourning for Deborah.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>32:31</sup>&nbsp;ወሖረት ርብቃ ወገብአት ውስተ ቤት ኀበ አቡሁ ይስሐቅ። ወፈነወ ያዕቆብ በእዴሃ አብሐኰ ወደቤላተ ወአባግዐ ከመ ትግበር ለአቡሁ መብልዐ ዘከመ ይፈቅድ። <sup>32:32</sup>&nbsp;ወሖረ እምድኅሬሃ ለእሙ እስከ ቀርበ ምድረ ከብራታን ወኀደረ ህየ። <sup>32:33</sup>&nbsp;ወወለደት ራሔል በሌሊት ወልደ ወጸውዐት ስሞ ወልደ ሕማምየ እስመ ዐጸበት ሶበ ትወልዶ ወአቡሁሰ ጸውዐ ስሞ ብንያምሃ። አመ ዐሡሩ ወአሚሩ ለወርኅ ሳምን። በዓመት አሐዱ ዘሱባዔ ሳድስ ዘዝንቱ ኢዮቤልውን። <sup>32:34</sup>&nbsp;ወሞተት በህየ ራሔል ወተቀብረት ውስተ ምድረ ኤፍራታ እንተ ይእቲ ቤተ ልሔም። ወሐነጸ ያዕቆብ ውስተ መቃብረ ራሔል ሐውልተ ውስተ ፍኖት ላዕለ መቃብሪሃ።
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>32:31</sup>&nbsp;Then Rebecca set out and returned home to his father Isaac. Through her Jacob sent rams, he-goats, and sheep to make his father a meal as he would wish. <sup>32:32</sup>&nbsp;He followed his mother until he reached the country of Kabratan, and he remained there. <sup>32:33</sup>&nbsp;During the night Rachel gave birth to a son. She named him Son of my Pain because she had difficulty when she was giving birth to him. But his father named him Benjamin on the eleventh of the eighth month, during the first year of the sixth week of this jubilee [2143]. <sup>32:34</sup>&nbsp;Rachel died there and was buried in the country of Ephrathah, that is, Bethlehem. Jacob built a pillar at Rachel's grave — on the road above her grave.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>33:1</sup>&nbsp;ወሖረ ያዕቆብ ወኀደረ መንገለ ደቡበ መግደለድራኤፍ ወሖረ ኀበ አቡሁ ይስሐቅ ውእቱ ወልያ ብእሲቱ አመ ሠርቁ ለወርኅ ዓሥር። <sup>33:2</sup>&nbsp;ወርእዮ ሮቤል ባላንሃ ለአኪተ ራሔል ዕቅብተ አቡሁ እንዘ ትትሐፀብ በማይ በኅቡእ አፍቀራ <sup>33:3</sup>&nbsp;ወተኀብአ በሌሊት ወቦአ ቤተ ባላን ሌሊተ ወረከባ እንዘ ትሰክብ ውስተ ዐራታ ባሕቲታ ወትነውም ውስተ ቤታ <sup>33:4</sup>&nbsp;ወሰከበ ምስሌሃ ወነቅሀት ወርእየት ወናሁ ሮቤል ይሰክብ ምስሌሃ ውስተ ምስካብ። ወከሠተት ክንፋ ወአኀዘቶ ወአውየወት ወአእመረት ከመ ሮቤል ውእቱ <sup>33:5</sup>&nbsp;ወተኀፈረት እምኔሁ ወኀደገት እዴሃ እምላዕሌሁ ወጐየ። <sup>33:6</sup>&nbsp;ወትላሑ በእንተዝ ነገር ፈድፋደ ወኢነገረት ወኢለመኑሂ ሰብእ። <sup>33:7</sup>&nbsp;ወሶበ መጽአ ያዕቆብ ወኀሠሣ ትቤሎ ኢኮንኩ ንጽሕተ ለከ እስመ ተገመንኩ እምኔከ እስመ አርኰሰኒ ሮቤል ወሰከበ ምስሌየ ሌሊተ ወአንሰ እነውም ወኢያእመርኩ እስከ ሶበ ከሠተ ክነፍየ ወሰከበ ምስሌየ። <sup>33:8</sup>&nbsp;ወተምዐ ያዕቆብ ጥቀ ላዕለ ሮቤል እስመ ሰከበ ምስለ ባላን እስመ ከሠተ ክድነተ አቡሁ <sup>33:9</sup>&nbsp;ወኢቀርባ እንከ ያዕቆብ እስመ አርኰሳ ሮቤል። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>33:1</sup>&nbsp;Jacob went and lived to the south of the Tower of Eder Ephrathah. He went to his father Isaac — he and his wife Leah — on the first of the tenth month. <sup>33:2</sup>&nbsp;When Reuben saw Bilhah, Rachel's maid — his father's concubine — bathing in water in a private place, he loved her. <sup>33:3</sup>&nbsp;At night he hid. He entered Bilhah's house at night and found her lying alone in her bed and sleeping in her tent. <sup>33:4</sup>&nbsp;After he had lain with her, she awakened and saw that Reuben was lying with her in the bed. She uncovered the edge of her (clothing), took hold of him, shouted out, and realized that it was Reuben. <sup>33:5</sup>&nbsp;She was ashamed because of him. Once she had released her grip on him, he ran away. <sup>33:6</sup>&nbsp;She grieved terribly about this matter and told no one at all. <sup>33:7</sup>&nbsp;When Jacob came and looked for her, she said to him: 'I am not pure for you because I am too contaminated for you, since Reuben defiled me and lay with me at night. I was sleeping and did not realize (it) until he uncovered the edge of my (garment) and lay with me'. <sup>33:8</sup>&nbsp;Jacob was very angry at Reuben because he had lain with Bilhah, since he had uncovered the covering of his father. <sup>33:9</sup>&nbsp;Jacob did not approach her again because Reuben had defiled her.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
ወኵሉ ሰብእ ዘከሠተ ክድነተ አቡሁ እስመ እኩይ ነገሩ ጥቀ ወእስመ ምኑን ውእቱ በቅድመ እግዚአብሔር። <sup>33:10</sup>&nbsp;በእንተዝ ጽሑፍ ወሥሩዕ ውስተ ጽላተ ሰማይ ከመ ኢይስክብ ብእሲ ምስለ ብእሲተ አቡሁ ወከመ ኢይክሥት ክድነተ አቡሁ እስመ ርኩሰ ውእቱ ሞተ ይሙት ኅቡረ ብእሲ ዘይሰክብ ምስለ ብእሲተ አቡሁ ወብእሲትኒ እስመ ርኩሰ ነገሩ ውስተ ምድር <sup>33:11</sup>&nbsp;ወኢይኩን ርኵሰ ቅድመ አምላክነ በውስተ ሕዝብ ዘኀረየ ሎቱ ለምልካን። <sup>33:12</sup>&nbsp;ወካዕበ ጽሑፍ ዳግመ ርጉመ ይከን ዘይሰክብ ምስለ ብእሲተ አቡሁ እስመ ከሠተ ኀፍረተ አቡሁ ወይቤሉ ኵሎሙ ቅዱሳኒሁ ለእግዚአብሔር ለይኩን ለይኩን። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
As for any man who uncovers the covering of his father — his act is indeed very bad and it is indeed despicable before the Lord. <sup>33:10</sup>&nbsp;For this reason it is written and ordained on the heavenly tablets that a man is not to lie with his father's wife and that he is not to uncover the covering of his father because it is impure. They are certainly to die together — the man who lies with his father's wife and the woman, too — because they have done something impure on the earth. <sup>33:11</sup>&nbsp;There is to be nothing impure before our God within the nation that he has chosen as his own possession. <sup>33:12</sup>&nbsp;Again it is written a second time: 'Let the one who lies with his father's wife be cursed because he has uncovered his father's shame'. All of the Lord's holy ones said: 'So be it, so be it'.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>33:13</sup>&nbsp;ወአንተኒ ሙሴ አዝዞሙ ለውሉደ እስራኤል ይዕቀቡ ዘንተ ቃለ እስመ ኵነኔ ሞት ውእቱ ወርኵስ ውእቱ ወአልቦ ስርየተ ለአስተስርዮ በእንተ ብእሲ ዘገብረ ዘንተ ለዓለም ዘእንበለ ለአምቶቱ ወለቀቲሎቱ ወለተወግሮቱ በእብን ወለተሠርዎቱ እማእከለ ሕዝበ አምላክነ <sup>33:14</sup>&nbsp;እስመ ኢይከውኖ ሐይወ አሐተ ዕለተ ውስተ ምድር ኵሉ ሰብእ ዘይገብሮ በውስተ እስራኤል እስመ ምኑን ወርኩስ ውእቱ። <sup>33:15</sup>&nbsp;ወኢይበሉ ለሮቤል ኮነ ሐዩው ወስርየተ እምዘ ሰከበ ምስለ ዕቅብተ ብእሲተ አቡሁ ወይእቲኒ እንዘ ባቲ ምተ ወእንዘ ምታ ሕያው ያዕቆብ አቡሁ። <sup>33:16</sup>&nbsp;እስመ ኢተከሥተ ሥርዓት ወኵነኔ ወሕግ እስከ አሜሃ ፍጹመ ለኵሉ። እስመ በመዋዕሊከ ከመ ሕገ ጊዜ በመዋዕሉ ወሕግ ዘለዓለም ለትውልድ ዘለዓለም <sup>33:17</sup>&nbsp;ወአልቦ ለዝ ሕግ ተውዳአ መዋዕል ወምንተኒ ስርየተ ሎቱ ዘእንበለ ከመ ይሠረዉ ክልኤሆሙ በማእከለ ሕዝብ በዕለት እንተ ባቲ ገብርዋ ይቅትልዎሙ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>33:13</sup>&nbsp;Now you, Moses, order the Israelites to observe this command because it is a capital offence and it is an impure thing. To eternity there is no expiation to atone for the man who has done this; but he is to be put to death, to be killed, and to be stoned and uprooted from among the people of our God. <sup>33:14</sup>&nbsp;For any man who commits it in Israel will not be allowed to live a single day on the earth because he is despicable and impure. <sup>33:15</sup>&nbsp;They are not to say: 'Reuben was allowed to live and (have) forgiveness after he had lain with the concubine-wife of his father while she had a husband and her husband — his father Jacob — was alive'. <sup>33:16</sup>&nbsp;For the statute, the punishment, and the law had not been completely revealed to all but (only) in your time as a law of its particular time and as an eternal law for the history of eternity. <sup>33:17</sup>&nbsp;There is no time when this law will be at an end, nor is there any forgiveness for it; rather both of them are to be uprooted among the people. On the day on which they have done this they are to kill them.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>33:18</sup>&nbsp;ወአነተኒ ሙሴ ጸሐፍ ለእስራኤል ወይዕቀብዋ ወኢይግበሩ ዘከመ ዝንቱ ነገር ወኢይስሐቱ ለአበሳ ሞት እስመ መኵንን እግዚአብሔር አምላክነ ዘውእቱ ኢይነሥእ ገጸ ወኢይነሥእ ሕልያነ። <sup>33:19</sup>&nbsp;ወንግሮሙ ዘንተ ነገረ ሥርዓት ሎሙ ይስምዑ ወይትዐቀቡ ወይትናጸሩ እምኔሆሙ ወኢይትሐጐሉ ወኢይሠረዉ እምድር። እስመ ርኩስ ወሰቆራር ወንክፈት ወግማኔ ኵሎሙ እለ ይገብርዋ በምድር በቅድመ አምላክነ። <sup>33:20</sup>&nbsp;ወአልቦ ኀጢአተ ዐባየ እምዝሙና ዘይዜምዉ ዲበ ምድር እስመ ሕዝብ ቅዱስ እስራኤል ለእግዚአብሔር አምላኩ። ወሕዝበ ርስት ውእቱ ወሕዝበ ክህነት ውእቱ ወመንግሥተ ክህነት ውእቱ ወጥሪት ውእቱ ወአኮ ዘያስተርኢ ዘከመዝ ርኵስ በማእከለ ሕዝብ ቅዱስ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>33:18</sup>&nbsp;Now you, Moses, write for Israel so that they keep it and do not act hke this and do not stray into a capital offence; because the Lord our God, who shows no partiahty and accepts no bribes, is the judge. <sup>33:19</sup>&nbsp;Tell them these words of the testament so that they may listen, guard themselves, be careful about them, and not be destroyed or uprooted from the earth. For all who commit it on the earth before the Lord are impure, something detestable, a blemish, and something contaminated. <sup>33:20</sup>&nbsp;No sin is greater than the sexual impurity which they commit on the earth because Israel is a holy people for the Lord its God. It is the nation which he possesses; it is a priestly nation; it is a priestly kingdom; it is what he owns. No such impurity will be seen among the holy people.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>33:21</sup>&nbsp;ወበሣልስ ዓመት ዘሱባዔ ሳድስ ሀሎ እንዘ የሐውር ያዕቆብ ወኵሉ ውሉዱ ወኀደሩ ቤተ አብርሃም ቅሩበ ይስሐቅ አቡሁ ወእሙ ርብቃ። <sup>33:22</sup>&nbsp;ወዝንቱ አስማቲሆሙ ለውሉደ ያዕቆብ በኵሩ ሮቤል። ስምዖን ሌዊ። ይሁዳ። ይሳኮር። ዛብሎን። ውሉዳ ለልያ። ወውሉዳ ለራሔል ዮሴፍ ወብንያም። ወውሉደ ባላን ዳን ወንፍታሌም። ወውሉደ ዘለፋን ጋድ ወአሴር። ወዲና ወለተ ልያ ባሕቲታ ወለተ ያዕቆብ። <sup>33:23</sup>&nbsp;ወሐዊሮሙ ሰገዱ ለይስሐቅ ወለርብቃ። ወሶበ ርእይዎሙ ባረክዎ ለያዕቆብ ወለኵሎሙ ውሉዱ። ወተፈሥሐ ይስሐቅ ፈድፋደ እስመ ርእየ ውሉደ ያዕቆብ ወልዱ ዘይንእስ ወባረኮሙ።
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>33:21</sup>&nbsp;During the third year of the sixth week [2145] Jacob and all his sons went and took up residence at the house of Abraham near his father Isaac and his mother Rebecca. <sup>33:22</sup>&nbsp;These are the names of Jacob's sons: Reuben, his first-born, Simeon, Levi, Judah, Issachar, Zebulun were Leah's sons. Rachel's sons were Joseph and Benjamin. Bilhah's sons were Dan and Naphtali. And Zilpah's sons were Gad and Asher. Leah's daughter Dinah was Jacob's only daughter. <sup>33:23</sup>&nbsp;After they had come, they bowed to Isaac and Rebecca. When they saw them, they blessed Jacob and all his children. Isaac was extremely happy that he had seen the children of his younger son Jacob, and he blessed them.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>34:1</sup>&nbsp;ወበሳድስ ዓመቱ ለዝ ሱባዔ እምዝንቱ ዘአርብዓ ወአርባዕቱ ኢዮቤልዉ። ፈነዎሙ ያዕቆብ ለውሉዱ ይርዐዩ አባግዒሆሙ ወአግብርቲሁኒ ምስሌሆሙ ውስተ ጺኦተ ሰቂሞን። <sup>32:2</sup>&nbsp;ወተጋብኡ ላዕሌሆሙ ሰብዐቲሆሙ ነገሥተ አሞሬዎን ከመ ይቅትልዎሙ ተኀቢኦሙ ታሕተ ኦም ወከመ ይማህርኩ እንስሳሆሙ። <sup>34:3</sup>&nbsp;ወያዕቆብ ወሌዊ ወይሁዳ ወዮሴፍ ሀለዉ ውስተ ቤት ኀበ ይስሐቅ አቡሆሙ እስመ የሐዝኖ መንፈሱ ወስእኑ ኀዲጎቶ ወብንያም ውእቱ ዘይንእስ ወበእንተዝ ነበረ ኀቤሁ። <sup>34:4</sup>&nbsp;ወመጽኡ ነገሥተ ታፉ ወነገሥተ አሬስ ወነገሥተ ሴራጋን ወነገሥተ ሴሎ ወንጉሥ ጋአዝ ወንጉሠ ቤቶሮን ወንጉሠ ማአኒሳኪር ወኵሎሙ እለ ይነብሩ ውስተዝ ደብር እለ ይነብሩ ውስተ ኦመ ምድረ ከናአን። <sup>34:5</sup>&nbsp;ወዜነውዎ ለያዕቆብ እንዘ ይብሉ ከመ ናሁ ነገሥቶ አሞሬዎን ዐገትዎሙ ለውሉድከ ወመራዕዮሙሂ ተማሠጡ። <sup>34:6</sup>&nbsp;ወተንሥአ እምነ ቤቱ ውእቱ ወሠለስቲሆሙ ውሉዱ ወኵሎሙ ደቀ አቡሁ ወደቁ ወሖረ ላዕሌሆሙ በስሳ ምእት ዕድ እለ ይጸውሩ አስይፍተ <sup>34:7</sup>&nbsp;ወቀተሎሙ በውስተ ጺኦት ዘሰቂሞን ወዴገኑ እለ ጐዩ ወቀተሎሙ በአፈ ሰይፍ። ወቀተሎ ለአሬስ ወለታፉ ወለሰሬጋን ወለሲሎ ወለአማኒሰኪር ወለጋጋአስ <sup>34:8</sup>&nbsp;ወአስተጋብአ መራዕዪሁ። ወዐብየ ላዕሌሆሙ ወሠርዐ ጸባሕተ ላዕሌሆሙ ከመ የሀብዎ ጸባሕተ ኃምስተ ፍሬ ምድሮሙ። ወሐነጸ ሮቤልሃ ወተምናታሬስሃ <sup>34:9</sup>&nbsp;ወተመይጠ በሰላም። ወገብረ ምስሌሆሙ ሰላመ ወኮንዎ አግብርተ እስከ አመ ዕለተ ወረዱ ውእቱ ወውሉዱ ውስተ ግብጽ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>34:1</sup>&nbsp;During the sixth year of this week of this forty-fourth jubilee [2148], Jacob sent his sons to tend their sheep — his servants were also with them — to the field of Shechem. <sup>34:2</sup>&nbsp;Seven Amorite kings assembled against them to kill them from their hiding place beneath the trees and to take their animals as booty. <sup>34:3</sup>&nbsp;But Jacob, Levi, Judah, and Joseph remained at home with their father Isaac because he was distressed and they were unable to leave him. Benjamin was the youngest, and for this reason he stayed with him. <sup>34:4</sup>&nbsp;Then came the kings of Tafu, the king of Ares, the king of Seragan, the king of Selo, the king of Gaaz, the king of Betoron, the king of Maanisakir, and all who were living on this mountain, who were living in the forest of the land of Canaan. <sup>34:5</sup>&nbsp;It was reported to Jacob: 'The Amorite kings have just surrounded your sons and have carried off their flocks by force'. <sup>34:6</sup>&nbsp;He set out from his house — he, his three sons, all his father's servants, and his servants — and went against them with 6000 men who carried swords. <sup>34:7</sup>&nbsp;He killed them in the field of Shechem, and they pursued the ones who ran away. He killed them with the blade of the sword. He killed Ares, Tafu, Saregan, Silo, Amanisakir, and Gagaas <sup>34:8</sup>&nbsp;and collected his flocks. He got control of them and imposed tribute on them so that they should give him as tribute five of their land's products. He built Robel and Tamnatares <sup>34:9</sup>&nbsp;and returned safely. He made peace with them, and they became his servants until the day that he and his sons went down to Egypt.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>34:10</sup>&nbsp;ወበሳብዕ ዓመት ዘዝ ሱባዔ ፈነወ ዮሴፍሃ። ከመ ያእምር ሰላሞሙ ለአኀዊሁ እምቤቱ ውስተ ምድረ ሰቂሞን ወረከቦሙ በምድረ ዶታኢም። <sup>34:11</sup>&nbsp;ወሐብለይዎ ወገብሩ ላዕሌሁ ምክረ ከመ ይቅትልዎ። ወተመይጦሙ ሤጥዎ ለነጋዲተ እስማኤላዊያን ወአውረድዎ ግብጽ ወሤጥዎ ለፉጢፋራን ለኅፅወ ፈርዖን ሊቀ መብስላን ሣውዕ ዘሀገረ ኤሌው። <sup>34:12</sup>&nbsp;ወውሉደ ያዕቆብ ዘብሑ ደቤላ ጠሊ ወጸንቀቁ ልብሶ ለዮሴፍ በደሙ ወፈነዉ ኀበ ያዕቆብ አቡሆሙ አመ ዐሡሩ ለወርኅ ሳብዕ። <sup>34:13</sup>&nbsp;ወለሐወ ኵላ ይእተ ሌሊተ እስመ ሰርከ አምጽኡ ሎቱ ኪያሁ ወፈፀነ በላሐ ሞቱ ወይቤ ከመ አርዌ ፀዋግ በልዖ ለዮሴፍ ወላሐዉ ምስሌሁ ኵሉ ሰብአ ቤቱ በዛቲ ዕለት ወሀለዉ እንዘ የሐምሙ ወይላሕዉ ምስሌሁ ኵላ ይእተ ዕለተ። <sup>34:14</sup>&nbsp;ወተንሥኡ ውሉዱ ወወለቱ ከመ ይናዝዝዎ ወኢተናዘዘ በእንተ ወልዱ። <sup>34:15</sup>&nbsp;ወበውእቱ ዕለት ሰምዐት ባላን ከመ ተሐጕለ ዮሴፍ ወእንዘ ትላሕዎ ሞተት ወይእቲ ሀለወት ትነብር ውስተ ቀፍራቴፋ ወዲናኒ ወለቱ ሞተት እምድኅረ ተሐጕለ ዮሴፍ ወበጽሖሙ ለእስራኤል ዝንቱ ሠለስቱ ላሕ በወርኅ አሐዱ <sup>34:16</sup>&nbsp;ወቀበርዋ ለባላን አንጸረ መቃብራ ለራሔል ወዲናሃኒ ወለቶ ቀበሩ ህየ። <sup>34:17</sup>&nbsp;ወሀሎ እንዘ ይላሑ ድኅሬሁ ለዮሴፍ ዓመተ አሐደ ወኢነገፈ እስመ ይቤ እረድ ውስተ መቃብር እንዘ እላሑ በእንተ ወልድየ። <sup>34:18</sup>&nbsp;በእንተዝ ተሠርዐ ዲበ ውሉደ እስራኤል ከመ ይሕመሙ በዐሡር ወርኅ በሳብዕ አመ ዕለተ በጽሐ ዘያበኪ ዮሴፍሃ ኀበ ያዕቆብ አቡሁ ከመ ያስተስሪ ባቲ ሎቱ በእጕለ አጣሊ። አመ ዐሡሩ ለወርኅ ሳብዕ ምዕረ ለዓመት በእንተ ኀጢአቶሙ እስመ አሕዘኑ ምሕረተ አቡሆሙ በእንተ ዮሴፍ ወልዱ። <sup>34:19</sup>&nbsp;ወተሠርዐት ዛቲ ዕለት ከመ ይሕዘኑ ባቲ በእንተ ኀጢአቶሙ ወበእንተ ኵሉ አበሳሆሙ ወበእንተ ኵሉ ስሕተቶሙ ከመ ያንጽሑ ርእሶሙ በዛቲ ዕለት ምዕረ ለዓመት። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>34:10</sup>&nbsp;During the seventh year of this week [2149] he sent Joseph from his house to the land of Shechem to find out about his brothers' welfare. He found them in the land of Dothan. <sup>34:11</sup>&nbsp;They acted in a treacherous way and made a plan against him to kill him; but, after changing their minds, they sold him to a traveling band of Ishmaelites. They brought him down to Egypt and sold him to Potiphar, the pharaoh's eunuch, the chief cook, and the priest of the city Elew. <sup>34:12</sup>&nbsp;Jacob's sons slaughtered a he-goat, stained Joseph's clothing by dipping it in its blood, and sent (it) to their father Jacob on the tenth of the seventh month. <sup>34:13</sup>&nbsp;He mourned all that night because they had brought it to him in the evening. He became feverish through mourning his death and said that a wild animal had eaten Joseph. That day all the people of his household mourned with him. They continued to be distressed and to mourn with him all that day. <sup>34:14</sup>&nbsp;His sons and daughter set about consoling him, but he was inconsolable for his son. <sup>34:15</sup>&nbsp;That day Bilhah heard that Joseph had perished. While she was mourning for him, she died. She had been hving in Qafratefa. His daughter Dinah, too, died after Joseph had perished. These three (reasons for) mourning came to Israel in one month. <sup>34:16</sup>&nbsp;They buried Bilhah opposite Rachel's grave, and they buried his daughter Dinah there as well. <sup>34:17</sup>&nbsp;He continued mourning Joseph for one year and was not comforted but said: 'May I go down to the grave mourning for my son'. <sup>34:18</sup>&nbsp;For this reason, it has been ordained regarding the Israelites that they should be distressed on the tenth of the seventh month — on the day when (the news) which made (him) lament Joseph reached his father Jacob — in order to make atonement for themselves on it with a kid — on the tenth of the seventh month, once a year — for their sins. For they had saddened their father's (feelings of) affection for his son Joseph. <sup>34:19</sup>&nbsp;This day has been ordained so that they may be saddened on it for their sins, all their transgressions, and all their errors; so that they may purify themselves on this day once a year.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>34:20</sup>&nbsp;ወእምድኅረ ተሐጕለ ዮሴፍ ነሥኡ ለርእሶሙ ውሉደ ያዕቆብ አንስቲያ። ስማ ለብእሲተ ሮቤል ኦዳ። ወስማ ለብእሲተ ስምዖን አዴባአ ከነናዊት። ወስማ ለብእሲተ ሌዊ ሜልካ እምአዋልደ አራም እምዘርአ ውሉደ ታራን። ወስማ ለብእሲተ ይሁዳ ቤተሱኤል ከነናዊት። ወስማ ለብእሲተ ይሳኮር ሔዘቃ። ወስማ ለብእሲተ ዛብሎን። [ኔኤማን ?] ወስማ ለብእሲተ ዳን ኤግላ ወስማ ለብእሲተ ንፍታሌም ራሱኡ እንተ መስጴጦምያ። ወስማ ለብእሲተ ጋድ ማከ። ወስማ ለብእሲተ አሴር ኢዮና። ወስማ ለብእሲተ ዮሴፍ አስኔት ግብጻዊት። ወስማ ለብእሲተ ብንያም ኢያስከ <sup>34:21</sup>&nbsp;ወተመይጦ ስምዖን ነሥአ ብእሲተ እምነ መስጴጦምያ ካልእተ ከመ አኀዊሁ።
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>34:20</sup>&nbsp;After Joseph had perished, Jacob's sons took wives for themselves. The name of Reuben's wife was Oda; the name of Simeon's wife was Adebaa, the Canaanitess; the name of Levi's wife was Melcha, one of the daughters of Aram — one of the descendants of Terah's sons; the name of Judah's wife was Betasuel, the Canaanitess; the name of Issachar's wife was Hezaqa; the name of Zebulun's wife was [Neeman]; the name of Dan's wife was Egla; the name of Naphtali's wife was Rasu'u of Mesopotamia; the name of Gad's wife was Maka; the name of Asher's wife was Iyona; the name of Joseph's wife was Asenath, the Egyptian, and the name of Benjamin's wife was Iyaska. <sup>34:21</sup>&nbsp;Simeon, after changing his mind, married another woman from Mesopotamia like his brothers.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>35:1</sup>&nbsp;ወበቀዳሚ ዓመት ዘሱባዔ ቀዳሚ በዘ አርብዓ ወኃምስቱ ኢዮቤልዉ ጸውዐቶ ርብቃ ለያዕቆብ ወልዳ ወአዘዘቶ በእንተ አቡሁ ወበእንተ እኁሁ ከመ ያክብሮሙ ኵሎ መዋዕለ ሕይወቱ ለያዕቆብ። <sup>35:2</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤ ያዕቆብ አነ እገብር ኵሎ ዘከመ አዘዝክኒ እስመ ክብር ወዕበይ ሊተ ዝንቱ ነገር ወጽድቅ ሊተ በቅድመ እግዚአብሔር ከመ አክብሮሙ። <sup>35:3</sup>&nbsp;ወአንቲኒ እሞ ታአሞሪ እምዕለተ ተወለድኩ እስከ ዛቲ ዕለት ኵሎ ምግባርየ ወኵሎ ዘውስተ ልብየ ከመ ኵሎ መዋዕለ እኄሊ ሠናየ ለኵሉ። <sup>35:4</sup>&nbsp;ወእፎ ኢይግብር ነገረ ዘአዘዝክኒ ከመ አክብር አባየ ወእኅዋየ <sup>35:5</sup>&nbsp;ንግርኒ እሞ ምንተ ርኢኪ በላዕሌየ ጥውየተ ወተግሕሦ እትገሐሥ እምኔሁ ወይከውን ላዕሌየ ሣህል። <sup>35:6</sup>&nbsp;ወትቤሎ ወልድየ ኵሎን መዋዕልየ አልቦ ዘርኢኩ በላዕሌከ ምንተኒ ግብረ ጠዋየ አላ ርቱዐ ወባሕቱ ጽድቀ እነግረከ ወልድየ አነ በዛቲ ዓመት እመውት ወኢይትዐደው ዛተ ዓመተ በሕይወት። እስመ ርኢኩ በሕልም ዕለተ ሞትየ ከመ ኢየሐዩ ፈድፋደ እምእት ወኀምሳ ወኀምስ ዓመት ወናሁ አነ ፈጸምኩ ኵሎ መዋዕለ ሕይወትየ ዘሀሎኩ እሕየው <sup>35:7</sup>&nbsp;ወሠሐቀ ያዕቆብ በእንተ ነገረ እሙ እስመ ትቤሎ እሙ ከመ ትመውት ወይእቲሰ ትነብር አንጻሪሁ ወኀይላ ላዕሌሃ ወኢደክመት እምኀይላ እስመ ትበውእ ወትወፅእ ወትሬኢ ወአስናኒሃኒ ጽኑዕ ወምንተኒ ሕማም ኢለከፋ ኵሎ መዋዕለ ሕይወታ። <sup>35:8</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤላ ያዕቆብ ብፁዕ አነ እሞ እመ ቀርበ መዋዕልየ ለመዋዕለ ሕይወትኪ ወይሄሉ ኀይልየ ላዕሌየ ከመዝ በከመ ኀይልኪ ወኢትመውቲ እስመ በከ በጸው ትትናገሪ ምስሌየ በእንተ ሞትኪ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>35:1</sup>&nbsp;During the first year of the first week in the forty-fifth jubilee [2157], Rebecca summoned her son Jacob and ordered him regarding his father and brother that he was to honor them throughout Jacob's entire lifetime. <sup>35:2</sup>&nbsp;Jacob said: 'I will do everything just as you ordered me because this matter will be something honorable and great for me; it will be a righteous act for me before the Lord that I should honor them. <sup>35:3</sup>&nbsp;You, mother, know everything I have done and all my thoughts from the day I was born until today — that at all times I think of what is good for all. <sup>35:4</sup>&nbsp;How shall I not do what you have ordered me — that I should honor my father and brother? <sup>35:5</sup>&nbsp;Tell me, mother, what impropriety you have noticed in me and I will certainly turn away from it and will experience mercy'. <sup>35:6</sup>&nbsp;She said to him: 'My son, throughout my entire lifetime I have noticed no improper act in you but only proper one(s). However, I will tell you the truth, my son: I will die during this year and will not make it alive through this year because I have seen the day of my death in a dream — that I will not live more than 155 years. Now I have completed my entire lifetime that I am to live'. <sup>35:7</sup>&nbsp;Jacob laughed at what his mother was saying because his mother said to him that she would die, but she was sitting in front of him in possession of her strength. She had lost none of her strength because she could come and go; she could see and her teeth were strong. No sickness had touched her throughout her entire lifetime. <sup>35:8</sup>&nbsp;Jacob said to her: 'Mother, I would be fortunate if my lifetime approached your lifetime and (if) my strength would remain with me in the way your strength has. You are not going to die but rather have jokingly spoken idle nonsense with me about your death'.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>35:9</sup>&nbsp;ወቦአት ኀበ ይስሐቅ ወትቤሎ አሐተ ስእለተ አስተበቍዕ በኀቤከ እምሕሎ ለዔሳው ከመ ኢያሕስም ላዕለ ያዕቆብ ወኢይስድዶ በጸልእ። እስመ አንተ ታአምር ኅሊናሁ ለዔሳው ከመ ፀዋግ ውእቱ እምንእሱ ወአልቦ ላዕሌሁ ኂሩተ እስመ ይፈቅድ ውእቱ እምድኅረ ሞትከ ይቅትሎ <sup>35:10</sup>&nbsp;ወአንተ ታአምር መጠነ ገብረ ኵሎ እምአመ ዕለተ ሖረ ያዕቆብ እኁሁ ውስተ ካራን እስከ ዛቲ ዕለት ከመ በኵሉ ልቡ ኀደገነ። ወገብረ ምስሌነ እኩየ መራዕየከ አስተጋብአ ወኵሎ ጥሪተከ ሄደከ እምቅድመ ገጽከ <sup>35:11</sup>&nbsp;ወእንዘ ናስተበቍዕ ንስእሎ ዘእምዚአነ ወውእቱ ይሬሲ ከመ ዘብእሲ ዘይምሕረነ። <sup>35:12</sup>&nbsp;ወያመርር ላዕሌከ በእንተ ዘባረከ ያዕቆብሃ ወልደከ ፍጹማዊ ወራትዐ እስመ አልቦ እከየ ዘእንበለ ኂሩት። ወእምአመ መጽአ ምእካራን እስከ ዛቲ ዕለት ኢያኅፀፀ ለነ ወኢምንተኒ እስመ ኵሎ ያመጽእ ለነ በበ ጊዜሁ ኵሎ ዕለተ ወይትሬሣሕ በኵሉ ለቡ ሶበ ንነሥእ እምእዴሁ ወይባርከነ። ወኢተፈልጠ እምኔነ እምአመ ዕለተ መጽአ እምካራን። እስከ ዛቲ ዕለት ወውእቱ ይነብር ምስሌነ ዘልፈ ውስተ ቤት እንዘ ያከብረነ። <sup>35:13</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤላ ይስሐቅ አነኒ አአምር ወእሬኢ ግብረ ያዕቆብ ዘምስሌነ ከመ በኵሉ ልቡ ውእቱ ያከብረነ። አፍቀርክዎ ለዔሳው ቀዲሙ እምነ ያዕቆብ እምዘተወልደ ወይእዜ አፈቅር ያዕቆብሃ እምነ ዔሳው እስመ አብዝኀ አእክዮ ምግባሪሁ ወአልቦ ጽድቀ ሎቱ እስመ ኵሉ ፍኖቱ ዐመፃ ወግፍዕ ወአልቦ ጽድቀ ሎቱ ዐውዶ። <sup>35:14</sup>&nbsp;ወይእዜኒ ልብየ ይትሀወክ በእንተ ምግባራቲሁ ወኢኮነ ውእቱ ወዘርኡ ለድኂን እስመ እለ ይትሐጐሉ እሙንቱ እምነ ምድር ወእለ ይሤረዉ እሙንቱ እምታሕተ ሰማይ። እስመ አምላከ አብርሃም ኀደገ ወሖረ ድኅረ አንስቲያሁ ድኅረ ርኵስ ወድኅረ ስሕተቶን ውእቱ ወውሉዱ <sup>35:15</sup>&nbsp;ወአንቲኒ ትብልኒ ከመ አምሕሎ ከመ ኢይቅትል እኅዋሁ ያዕቆብሃ። እመኒ መሐለ ኢይሄሉ ወኢይገብር ኂሩተ ዘእንበለ እከይ <sup>35:16</sup>&nbsp;ወእመኒ ፈቀደ ይቅትል ያዕቆብሃ እኅዋሁ ውስተ እደ ያዕቆብ ይትወሀብ ወኢያመሥጥ እምእዴሁ እስመ ውስተ እዴሁ ይወርድ። <sup>35:17</sup>&nbsp;ወአንተኒ ኢትፍርሂ በእንተ ያዕቆብ እስመ ዐቃቢሁ ለያዕቆብ ዐቢይ ወኀያል ወክቡር ወእኩት እምዐቃቢሁ ለዔሳው። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>35:9</sup>&nbsp;She went in to Isaac and said to him: 'I am making one request of you: make Esau swear that he will not harm Jacob and not pursue him in hatred. For you know the way Esau thinks — that he has been malicious since his youth and that he is devoid of virtue because he wishes to kill him after your death. <sup>35:10</sup>&nbsp;You know everything that he has done from the day his brother Jacob went to Haran until today — that he has wholeheartedly abandoned us. He has treated us badly; he has gathered your flocks and has taken all your possessions away from you by force. <sup>35:11</sup>&nbsp;When we would ask him in a pleading way for what belonged to us, he would act like someone who was being charitable to us. <sup>35:12</sup>&nbsp;He is behaving bitterly toward you due to the fact that you blessed your perfect and true son Jacob since he has virtue only, no evil. From the time he came from Haran until today he has not deprived us of anything but he always brings us everything in its season. He is wholeheartedly happy when we accept (anything) from him, and he blesses us. He has not separated from us from the day he came from Haran until today. He has continually been living with us at home (all the while) honoring us'. <sup>35:13</sup>&nbsp;Isaac said to her. 'I, too, know and see the actions of Jacob who is with us — that he wholeheartedly honors us. At first I did love Esau more than Jacob, after he was born; but now I love Jacob more than Esau because he has done so many bad things and lacks (the ability to do) what is right. For the entire way he acts is (characterized by) injustice and violence and there is no justice about him. <sup>35:14</sup>&nbsp;Now my mind is disturbed about his actions. Neither he nor his descendants are to be saved because they will be destroyed from the earth and be uprooted from beneath the sky. For he has abandoned the God of Abraham and has gone after his wives, after impurity, and after their errors — he and his sons. <sup>35:15</sup>&nbsp;You are saying to me that I should make him swear not to kill his brother Jacob. Even if he does swear, it will not happen. He will not do what is virtuous but rather what is evil. <sup>35:16</sup>&nbsp;If he wishes to kill his brother Jacob, he will be handed over to Jacob and will not escape from his control but will fall into his control. <sup>35:17</sup>&nbsp;Now you are not to be afraid for Jacob because Jacob's guardian is greater and more powerful, glorious, and praiseworthy than Esau's guardian'.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>35:18</sup>&nbsp;ወለአክት ርብቃ ወጸውዐቶ ለዔሳው ወመጽአ ኀቤሃ ወትቤሎ ስእለተ ብየ ወልድየ እንተ እስእል እምኀቤከ ወበል ከመ ትግበራ ወልድየ <sup>35:19</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤ አነ እገብር ኵሎ ዘትቤልኒ ወኢየአቢ ስእለተኪ። <sup>35:20</sup>&nbsp;ወትቤሎ አነ እስእል እምኀቤከ በዕለተ አመ ሞትኩ ከመ ታብአኒ ወትቅብረኒ ቅሩበ ሳራ እመ አቡከ ወከመ ትትፋቀሩ አንተ ወያዕቆብ በበይናቲክሙ ወኢይኅሥሥ እኩየ አሐዱ ለእኁሁ ዘእንበለ ተፋቅሮ ክመ ወትሴርሑ ውሉድየ ወትከብሩ በማእከለ ምድር ወኢይትፌሣሕ ላእሌክሙ ጸላኢ ወትከውኑ ለበረከት ወለምሕረት በቅድመ አዕይንቲሆሙ ለኵሎሙ እለ ያፈቅሩክሙ። <sup>35:21</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤ አነ እገብር ኵሎ ዘትቤልኒ ወእቀብረኪ አመ ዕለተ ሞትኪ ቅሩበ ሳራ እሙ ለአቡየ በከመ አፍቀርኪ አዕጽምቲሃ ከመ የሀሉ ቅሩበ አዕጽምቲኪ። <sup>35:22</sup>&nbsp;ወያዕቆብሃኒ እኅዋየ አነ አፈቅር እምኵሉ ዘሥጋ ወአልቦ ሊተ እኅወ በውስተ ኵሉ ምድር ዘእንበለ ውእቱ ባሕቲቱ። ወአኮ ዐቢይ ዝንቱ ሊተ እመ አፍቀርክዎ እስመ እኁየ ውእቱ ወኅቡረ ተዘራእነ በማእከለ ከርሥኪ ወኅቡረ ወፃእነ እምሕረትኪ ወእመ ኢያፍቀርኩ እኅዋየ መነ አፈቅር። <sup>35:23</sup>&nbsp;ወአነ ክመ አስተበቍዐኪ ከመ ትገሥጽዮ ለያዕቆብ በእንቲአየ ወበእንተ ውሉድየ እስመ አአምር ከመ ነጊሠ ይነግሥ ላዕሌየ ወላዕለ ውሉድየ። እስመ አመ ዕለተ ባረኮ አቡየ ኪያሁ ረሰየ ልዑለ ወኪያየ ትሑተ <sup>35:24</sup>&nbsp;ወአነ እምሕል ለኪ ከመ አፈቅሮ ወከመ ኢይትኀሠሥ ሎቱ እኩየ ኵሎ መዋዕል ሕይወትየ ዘእንበለ ሠናይ ክመ። ወመሐለ ላቲ በእንተዝ ኵሉ ነገር። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>35:18</sup>&nbsp;Then Rebecca sent and summoned Esau. When he had come to her, she said to him: 'I have a request that I will make of you, my son; say that you will do it, my son'. <sup>35:19</sup>&nbsp;He said: 'I will do anything you tell me; I will not refuse your request'. <sup>35:20</sup>&nbsp;She said to him: 'I ask of you that on the day I die you bring me and bury me near your father's mother Sarah; and that you and Jacob love one another, and that the one not aim at what is bad for his brother but only at loving one another. Then you will be prosperous, my sons, and be honored on the earth. Your enemy will not be happy over you. You will become a blessing and an object of kindness in the view of all who love you'. <sup>35:21</sup>&nbsp;He said: 'I will do everything that you say to me. I will bury you on the day of your death near my father's mother Sarah as you have desired that her bones may be near your bones. <sup>35:22</sup>&nbsp;My brother Jacob I will love more than all mankind. I have no brother on the entire earth but him alone. This is no great thing for me if I love him because he is my brother. We were conceived together in your belly and we emerged together from your womb. If I do not love my brother, whom shall I love? <sup>35:23</sup>&nbsp;I myself ask of you that you instruct Jacob about me and my sons because I know that he will indeed rule over me and my sons. For on the day when my father blessed him he made him the superior and me the inferior one. <sup>35:24</sup>&nbsp;I swear to you that I will love him and that throughout my entire lifetime I will not aim at what is bad for him but only at what is good'. He swore to her about this entire matter.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>35:25</sup>&nbsp;ወጸውዐቶ ለያዕቆብ በቅድመ አዕይንቲሁ ለዔሳው ወአዘዘቶ በከመ ነገር ዘተናገረት ምስለ ዔሳው። <sup>35:26</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤ አነ እገብር ሥምረተኪ ተሐበይኒ ከመ ኢይወፅእ እምኔየ ወእምነ ውሉድየ እኩይ ላዕለ ዔሳው ኢይቀድም ዘእንበለ ተፋቅሮ ክመ። <sup>35:27</sup>&nbsp;ወበልዑ ወሰትዩ ይእቲ ወውሉዳ በይእቲ ሌሊት። ወሞተት ወለተ ሠለስቱ ኢዮቤልዉ ወሱባዔ አሐዱ ወዓመት አሐዱ በዛቲ ሌሊት ወቀበርዋ ክልኤሆሙ ውሉዳ  ዔሳው ወያዕቆብ ውስተ በአት ዘእንተ ክልኤ ቅሩበ ሳራ እመ አቡሆሙ።
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>35:25</sup>&nbsp;She summoned Jacob in front of Esau and gave him orders in line with what she had discussed with Esau. <sup>35:26</sup>&nbsp;He said: 'I will do what pleases you. Trust me that nothing bad against Esau will come from me or my sons. I will not be first except in love only'. <sup>35:27</sup>&nbsp;She and her sons ate and drank that night. She died that night at the age of three jubilees, one week, and one year [= 155 years]. Her two sons Esau and Jacob buried her in the twofold cave near their father's mother Sarah.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>36:1</sup>&nbsp;ወበሳድስ ዓመት ዘዝ ሱበዔ ጸውዐ ይስሐቅ ክልዔሆሙ ውሉዶ ዔሳውሃ ወያዕቆብሃ ወመጽኡ ኀቤሁ ወይቤሎሙ አነ ደቂቅየ አሐውር ውስተ ፍኖተ አበዊየ ውስተ ቤት ዘለዓለም ኀበ ሀለዉ ህየ አበዊየ። <sup>36:2</sup>&nbsp;ወቅብሩኒ ቅሩበ አብርሃም አቡየ ውስተ በአት ዘካዕበት ውስተ ገራህተ ኤፍሮን ኬጣዊ ዘአጥረየ አብርሃም ለዝኅረ መቃብር ህየ ውስተ መቃብር ዘከረይኩ ለርእስየ ህየ ቅብሩኒ። <sup>36:3</sup>&nbsp;ወዘንተ እኤዝዘክሙ ውሉድየ ከመ ትግበሩ ጽድቀ ወርትዐ በዲበ ምድር ከመ ያምጽእ እግዚአብሔር ላዕሌክሙ ኵሎ ዘመጠነ ነገሮ እግዚአብሔር ይግበር ለአብርሃም ወለዘርኡ። <sup>36:4</sup>&nbsp;ወኩኑ ውሉድየ በበይናቲክሙ እንዘ ታፈቅሩ አኀዊክሙ ከመ ብእሲ ዘያፈቅር ነፍሶ ወእንዘ የኀሥሥ ብእሲ ለእኁሁ በዘያሤኒ ሎቱ ወበገቢር ኅቡረ በዲበ ምድር ወይትፋቀሩ በበይናቲሆሙ ከመ ነፍሶሙ። <sup>36:5</sup>&nbsp;ወበእንተ ነገረ ጣዖት አነ እጌሥጸክሙ ከመ ትመንንዎሙ ወትፃረርዎሙ ወከመ ኢታፍቅርዎሙ እስመ ስሕተት ምሉኣን እሙንቱ ለእለ ያመልክዎሙ ወለእለ ይሰግዱ ሎሙ። <sup>36:6</sup>&nbsp;ተዘከርዎ ውሉድየ ለእግዚአብሔር ለአምላከ አብርሃም አቡክሙ ወእምዝ አነኒ አምለክዎ ወተቀነይኩ ሎቱ ዘበ ጽድቅ ወበስፉሕ ከመ ያብዝኅክሙ ወያልህቅ ዘርእክሙ ከመ ከዋክብተ ሰማይ ለብዝኅ ወይትክልክሙ ውስተ ምድር ተክለ ጽድቅ ዘኢይሤረው ለኵሉ ትውልድ ዘለዓለም። <sup>36:7</sup>&nbsp;ወይእዜኒ አነ አምሕለክሙ በመሐላ ዐቢይ እስመ አልቦ መሐላ ዘእምኔሁ የዐቢ በስም ስቡሕ ወክቡር ወዐቢይ ስሩሕ ወመንክር ወኀያል ወዐቢይ ዘገብረ ሰማያተ ወምድረ ወኵሎ ኅቡረ። ከመ ትኩኑ እለ ትፈርህዎ ወእለ ታመልክዎ <sup>36:8</sup>&nbsp;ወእንዘ ያፈቅር አሐዱ አሐዱ እኅዋሁ በምሕረት ወበጽድቅ ወኢይፍቅድ ብእሲ እኩየ ለእኁሁ እምይእዜ ወእስከ ለዓለም ኵሎ መዋዕለ ሕይወትክሙ ከመ ትስርሑ በኵሉ ምግባሪክሙ ወኢትትሐጐሉ። <sup>36:9</sup>&nbsp;ወእመቦ ዘኀሠሠ እምኔክሙ እኩየ ለእኁሁ አእምሩ እምይእዜ ከመ ኵሉ ዘየኀሥሥ እኩየ ለእኁሁ ውስተ እዴሁ ይወድቅ ወይሤሮ እምድረ ሕያዋን ወዘርኡሂ ይትሐጐል እምታሕተ ሰማይ። <sup>36:10</sup>&nbsp;ወአመ ዕለተ ሀከክ ወመርገም ወመዓት ወቍጥዓ ወበእሳት በላዒ በከመ አውዐየ ሰዶምሃ ከማሁ ያውዒ ምድሮ ወሀገሮ ወኵሎ ዘይከውን ዚአሁ። ወይደመሰስ እመጽሐፈ ተግሣጸ ሰብእ ወኢየዐርግ ውስተ መጽሐፈ ሕይወት እስመ ውስተ ዘይትሐጐል ወየኀልፍ ለመርገም ዘለዓለም። ከመ ለኵሉ መዋዕል ይኩን ደይኖሙ እንዘ ትትሔደስ በጽእለት ወመርገም ወበመዓት ወበፃዕር ወበቍጥዓ ወበመቅሠፍት ወበደዌ ዘለዓለም። <sup>36:11</sup>&nbsp;አነ እነግር ወአሰምዕ ላዕሌክሙ ውሉድየ በከመ ኵነኔ ዘይመጽእ ዲበ ብእሲ ዘይፈቅድ ይግበር ሕሡመ ላዕለ እኁሁ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>36:1</sup>&nbsp;During the sixth year of this week [2162] Isaac summoned his two sons Esau and Jacob. When they had come to him, he said to them: 'My children, I am going on the way of my fathers, to the eternal home where my fathers are. <sup>36:2</sup>&nbsp;Bury me near my father Abraham in the double cave in the field of Ephron the Hittite which Abraham acquired to (have) a burial place there. There, in the grave that I dug for myself, bury me. <sup>36:3</sup>&nbsp;This is what I am ordering you, my sons: that you do what is right and just on the earth so that the Lord may bring on you everything which the Lord said that he would do for Abraham and his descendants. <sup>36:4</sup>&nbsp;Practice brotherly love among yourselves, my sons, like a man who loves himself, with each one aiming at doing what is good for his brother and at doing things together on the earth. May they love one another as themselves. <sup>36:5</sup>&nbsp;Regarding the matter of idols, I am instructing you to reject them, to be an enemy of them, and not to love them because they are full of errors for those who worship them and who bow to them. <sup>36:6</sup>&nbsp;My sons, remember the Lord, the God of your father Abraham (afterwards I, too, worshiped and served him properly and sincerely) so that he may make you numerous and increase your descendants in number like the stars of the sky and plant you in the earth as a righteous plant which will not be uprooted throughout all the history of eternity. <sup>36:7</sup>&nbsp;Now I will make you swear with the great oath — because there is no oath which is greater than it, by the praiseworthy, illustrious, and great, splendid, marvelous, powerful, and great name which made the heavens and the earth and everything together — that you will continue to fear and worship him, <sup>36:8</sup>&nbsp;as each loves his brother kindly and properly. One is not to desire what is bad for his brother now and forever, throughout your entire lifetime, so that you may be prosperous in everything that you do and not be destroyed. <sup>36:9</sup>&nbsp;If one of you aims at what is bad for his brother, be aware that from now on anyone who aims at what is bad for his brother will fall into his control and will be uprooted from the land of the living, while his descendants will be destroyed from beneath the sky. <sup>36:10</sup>&nbsp;On the day of turmoil and curse, of anger and wrath — with a blazing fire that devours — he will burn his land, his city, and everything that belongs to him just as he burned Sodom. He will be erased from the disciplinary book of mankind. He will not be entered in the book of life but in the one that will be destroyed. He will pass over to an eternal curse so that their punishment may always be renewed with denunciation and curse, with anger, pain, and wrath, and with blows and eternal sickness. <sup>36:11</sup>&nbsp;I am reporting and testifying to you, my sons, in accord with the punishment which will come on the man who wishes to do what is harmful to his brother'.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>36:12</sup>&nbsp;ወከፈለ ኵሎ ዘቦ ጥሪቶ ለክልኤሆሙ በይእቲ ዕለት ወወሀበ ዕበየ ለብእሲ ዘውእቱ ቀደመ ተወልዶ ወማኅፈደ ኵሎ ዘአውዳ። ወኵሎ ዘአጥረየ አብርሃም በኀበ ዐዘቅተ መሐላ <sup>36:13</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤ ዛተ አዐቢ ዕበየ ለብእሲ ዘውእቱ ቀደመ ተወልዶ። <sup>36:14</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤ ዔሳው ሤጥኩ ሎቱ ለያዕቆብ ወወሀብኩ ልህቃንየ ለያዕቆብ ይትወሀብ ሎቱ ወአልብየ ዘእብል በእንቲአሃ ምንተኒ ቃለ እስመ ኀቤሁ ሀለወት። <sup>36:15</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤ ይስሐቅ ታዕርፍ ዲቤክሙ ውሉድየ በረከት ወላዕለ ዘርእክሙ በዛቲ ዕለት እስመ አዕረፍክሙኒ ወኢሐዘነ ልብየ በእንተ ልህቃን ከመ ኢትግበር በእንቲአሃ ፁገ <sup>36:16</sup>&nbsp;ይባርኮ እግዚአብሔር ልዑል ለብእሲ ዘይገብር ጽድቀ ኪያሁ ወዘርኡ እስከ ለዓለም። <sup>36:17</sup>&nbsp;ወፈጸመ እንዘ ይኤዝዞሙ ወእንዘ ይባርኮሙ ወበልዑ ወሰትዩ በቅድሜሁ ኅቡረ ወተፈሥሐ እስመ ኮነ ዐርዮ በማእከሎሙ ወወፅኡ እምኀቤሁ ወአዕረፉ ይእተ ዕለተ ወኖሙ። <sup>36:18</sup>&nbsp;ወኖመ ይስሐቅ ውስተ ዐራቱ በዛቲ ዕለት እንዘ ይትፌሣሕ ወኖመ ንዋመ ዘለዓለም። ወሞተ ወልደ ምእት ወሰማንያ ዓመት ዕሥራ ወኀምስ ሱባዔ ፈጸመ ወኀምስተ ዓመተ። ወቀበርዎ ክልኤሆሙ ውሉዱ ዔሳው ወያዕቆብ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>36:12</sup>&nbsp;That day he divided all the property that he owned between the two of them. He gave the larger part to the man who was the first to be born along with the tower, everything around it, and everything that Abraham had acquired at the well of the oath. <sup>36:13</sup>&nbsp;He said: 'I am making this portion larger for the man who was the first to be born'. <sup>36:14</sup>&nbsp;But Esau said: 'I sold (it) to Jacob; I gave my birthright to Jacob. It is to be given to him. I will say absolutely nothing about it because it belongs to him'. <sup>36:15</sup>&nbsp;Isaac then said: 'May a blessing rest on you, my sons, and on your descendants today because you have given me rest. My mind is not saddened regarding the birthright — lest you do something perverse about it. <sup>36:16</sup>&nbsp;May the most high Lord bless the man who does what is right — him and his descendants forever'. <sup>36:17</sup>&nbsp;When he had finished giving them orders and blessing them, they ate and drank together in front of him. He was happy because there was agreement between them. They left him, rested that day, and fell asleep. <sup>36:18</sup>&nbsp;That day Isaac was happy as he fell asleep on his bed. He fell asleep forever and died at the age of 180 years. He had completed 25 weeks and five years. His two sons Esau and Jacob buried him. 
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>36:19</sup>&nbsp;ወሖረ ዔሳው ውስተ ምድረ ኤዶም ውስተ ደብረ ሲር ወነበረ ህየ። <sup>36:20</sup>&nbsp;ወያዕቆብ ኀደረ ውስተ ደብረ ኬብሮን ውስተ ማኅፈድ ዘምድረ ፍልሰተ አቡሁ አብርሃም። ወአምለኮ ለእግዚአብሔር በኵሉ ልቡ ወበከመ ትእዛዛት ዘያስተርኢ በከመ ፈለጠ ዘመዋዕለ ልደቱ። <sup>36:21</sup>&nbsp;ወሞተት ልያ ብእሲቱ በዓመት ራብዕ ዘሱባዔ ካልእ ዘአርብዓ ወኃምስ ኢዮቤልዉ ወቀበራ ውስተ በአት ዘእንተ ክልኤ ቅሩበ ርብቃ እሙ በፀጋሙ ለመቃብረ ሳራ እመ አቡሁ <sup>36:22</sup>&nbsp;ወመጽኡ ኵሎሙ ውሉዳ ወውሉዱ ከመ ይብክይዋ ልያሃ ብእሲቶ ምስሌሁ ወከመ ይናዝዝዎ በእንቲአሃ እስመ ሀሎ ይላሕዋ <sup>36:23</sup>&nbsp;እስመ ያፈቅራ ፈድፋደ ጥቀ እምአመ ሞተት ራሔል እኅታ እስመ ፍጽምት ወራትዕት ይእቲ በኵሉ ፍናዊሃ ወታከብሮ ለያዕቆብ። ወበኵሉ መዋዕል ዘሐይወት ምስሌሁ ኢሰምዐ እምአፉሃ ቃለ ድሩከ እስመ የዋሂት ወሰላመ ወርትዐ ወክብረ ባቲ <sup>36:24</sup>&nbsp;ወይዜከር ኵሎ ምግባራቲሃ ዘገብረት በሕይወታ ወይላሕዋ ጥቀ እስመ ያፈቅራ በኵሉ ልቡ ወበኵሉ ነፍሱ።
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>36:19</sup>&nbsp;Esau went to the land of Edom — to Mt. Seir — and lived there, <sup>36:20</sup>&nbsp;while Jacob lived on the mountain of Hebron, in the tower (which was located in) the land where his father Abraham had resided as a foreigner. He worshiped the Lord wholeheartedly and in line with the visible commands according to the division of the times of his generation. <sup>36:21</sup>&nbsp;His wife Leah died during the fourth year of the second week of the forty-fifth jubilee [2167]. He buried her in the twofold cave near his mother Rebecca, on the left of his grandmother Sarah's grave. <sup>36:22</sup>&nbsp;All her sons and his sons came to mourn with him for his wife Leah and to comfort him regarding her because he was lamenting her. <sup>36:23</sup>&nbsp;For he loved her very much from the time when her sister Rachel died because she was perfect and right in all her behavior and honored Jacob. In all the time that she lived with him he did not hear a harsh word from her mouth because she was gentle and possessed (the virtues of) peace, truthfulness, and honor. <sup>36:24</sup>&nbsp;As he recalled all the things that she had done in her lifetime, he greatly lamented her because he loved her with all his heart and with all his person.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>37:1</sup>&nbsp;ወበዕለተ ሞተ ይስሐቅ አቡሁ ለያዕቆብ ወለዔሳው ሰምዑ ውሉደ ዔሳው ከመ ወሀቦ ይስሐቅ ልህቃነ ለያዕቆብ ወልዱ ዘይንእስ። ወተምዑ ፈድፋደ <sup>37:2</sup>&nbsp;ወተጋአዙ ምስለ አቡሆሙ እንዘ ይብሉ በእንተ ምንት እንዘ ሀሎከ አንተ ዘትልህቅ ወእንዘ ይንእስ ለያዕቆብ ወሀቦ አቡከ ልህቃነ ወኪያከ ኀደገ። <sup>37:3</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤሎሙ እስመ አነ ሤጥኩ ቅድመተ ልደትየ ለያዕቆብ በኅዳጥ ጸብሐ ብርስን። ወበዕለተ ፈነወኒ አቡየ እንዐው ወአሥግር ወአምጽእ ሎቱ ከመ ይብላዕ ወይባርከኒ መጽአ በተጠብቦት። ወአብአ ለአቡየ መብልዐ ወመስቴ ወባረኮ አቡየ ወኪያየ ረሰየኒ ታሕተ እዴሁ። <sup>37:4</sup>&nbsp;ወይእዜኒ አምሐለነ አቡነ ኪያየ ወኪያሁ ከመ ኢንትኃሠሥ በእከይ አሐዱ ላዕለ እኁሁ ወከመ ነሀሉ በተፋቅሮ ወበሰላም ብእሲ ምስለ እኁሁ ወኢናማስን ፍናዊነ <sup>37:5</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤልዎ ኢንሰምዐከ ለገቢር ምስሌሁ ሰላመ እስመ ኀይለ ዚአነ ይጸንዕ እምኀይሉ ወንሕነ ንጸንዕ እምኔሁ ነሐውር ላዕሌሁ ወንቀትሎ ወናሐጕል ውሉዶ ወለእመ ኢተሐውር ምስሌነ ለከሂ ናሐስም። <sup>37:6</sup>&nbsp;ወይእዜኒ ስምዐነ ወንፈኑ ውስተ አራም ወውስተ ፍልስጥኤም ወውስተ ሞአብ ወውስተ አሞን ወንኅረይ ለርእስነ ኅሩያነ ሰብአ እለ ይዳለጉ ውስተ ቀትል ወንሖር ላዕሌሁ ወንትቃተል ምስሌሁ ወንሠርዎ እምድር እንበለ የአኀዝ ኀይለ። <sup>37:7</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤሎሙ አቡሆሙ ኢትሖሩ ወኢትግበሩ ምስሌሁ ፀብአ ከመ ኢትደቁ ቅድሜሁ። <sup>37:8</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤልዎ ዝኑ ክመ ግብርከ ዘእምውርዙትከ እስከ ዛቲ ዕለት ወአንተ ታበውእ ክሳደከ ታሕተ አርዑቱ ኢንሰምዕ ንሕነሰ ዘንተ ነገረ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
'Because I sold my right of the first-born to Jacob in exchange for a little lentil broth. The day my father sent me to hunt and trap and to bring (something) to him so that he could eat (it) and bless me, he came in a crafty way and brought in food and drink to my father. My father blessed him and put me under his control. <sup>37:4</sup>&nbsp;Now our father has made us — me and him — swear that we will not aim at what is bad, the one against his brother, and that we will continue in (a state of) mutual love and peace, each with his brother, so that we should not corrupt our behavior'. <sup>37:5</sup>&nbsp;They said to him: 'We will not listen to you by making peace with him because our strength is greater than his strength, and we are stronger than he is. We will go against him, kill him, and destroy his sons. If you do not go with us, we will harm you, too. <sup>37:6</sup>&nbsp;Now hsten to us; let us send to Aram, Philistia, Moab, and Ammon; and let us choose for ourselves select men who are brave in battle. Then let us go against him, fight with him, and uproot him from the earth before he gains strength'. <sup>37:7</sup>&nbsp;Their father said to them: 'Do not go and do not make war with him so that you may not fall before him'. <sup>37:8</sup>&nbsp;They said to him: 'Is this not the very way you have acted from your youth until today. You are putting your neck beneath his yoke. We will not listen to what you are saying'.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>37:9</sup>&nbsp;ወፈነዉ ውስተ አራም ወኀበ አዱራም ኀበ ዐርከ አቡሆሙ ወተዓሰቡ ምስሌሆሙ ዐሠርተ ምእተ መስተባእሳነ ዕደወ ወስተቃትላነ ኅሩያነ። <sup>37:10</sup>&nbsp;ወመጽኡ ኀቤሆሙ እምነ ሞአብ ወእምኀበ ውሉደ አሞን እለ ተዓሰቡ ዐሠርቱ ምእት ኅሩያን። ወእምነ ፍልስጥኤም ዐሠርቱ ምእት ኅሩያን መስተቃትላን ወእምኤዶም ወእምነ ኮሬውስ ዐሠርቱ ምእት ኅሩያን መስተባእሳን ወእምነ ኬጤዎን ዕደው ጽኑዓን መስተቃትላን። <sup>37:11</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤልዎ ለአቡሆሙ ፃእ ምርሖሙ ወእመአኮ ንቀትለከ። <sup>37:12</sup>&nbsp;ወመልአ መዓተ ወቍጥዓ በጊዜ ርእየ ውሉዶ ከመ ይትኤገልዎ ከመ ይሖር ቅድመ ይምርሖሙ ኀበ ያዕቆብ እኀሁ። <sup>37:13</sup>&nbsp;ወእምዝ ተዘከረ ኵሎ እከየ እንተ ሀሎት ውስተ ልቡ ኅብእት ላዕለ ያዕቆብ እኁሁ ወኢተዘከረ መሐላ ዘመሐለ ለአቡሁ ወለእሙ ከመ ኢይትኃሠሥ ኵሎ እከየ ኵሎ መዋዕሊሁ ላዕለ ያዕቆብ እኁሁ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>37:9</sup>&nbsp;So they sent to Aram and to their father's friend Aduram. Together with them they hired for themselves 1000 fighting men, select warriors. <sup>37:10</sup>&nbsp;There came to them from Moab and from the Ammonites 1000 select men who were hired; from the Philistines 1000 select warriors; from Edom and the Horites 1000 select fighters, and from the Kittim strong warriors. <sup>37:11</sup>&nbsp;They said to their father: 'Go out; lead them. Otherwise, we will kill you'. <sup>37:12</sup>&nbsp;He was filled with anger and wrath when he saw that his sons were forcing him to go in front in order to lead them to his brother Jacob. <sup>37:13</sup>&nbsp;But afterwards he remembered all the bad things that were hidden in his mind against his brother Jacob, and he did not remember the oath that he had sworn to his father and mother not to aim at anything bad against his brother Jacob throughout his entire lifetime.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>37:14</sup>&nbsp;ወበዝ ኵሉ ኢያእመረ ያዕቆብ ከመ እሙንቱ ይመጽኡ ኀቤሁ ለቀትል። ወውእቱሰ ይላሑ ልያሃ ብእሲቶ እስከ ሶበ ቀርቡ ኀቤሁ ጥቃ ማኅፈድ በአርብዓ ምእት ብእሲ መስተቃትላን መስተባእሳን ኅሩያን። <sup>37:15</sup>&nbsp;ወለአኩ ኀቤሁ ሰብአ ኬብሮን እንዘ ይብሉ ናሁአ እኁከአ መጽአአ ላዕሌከአ ይትቃተል ከአ በአርብዓ ምእት ብእሲ ቅኑታነ ሰይፍ ወይጸውሩ ወልታ ወንዋየ ሐቅል እስመ ያፈቅርዎ ለያዕቆብ እምዔሳው ነገርዎ እስመ ያዕቆብ ብእሲ ጸጋዊ ወመሓሪ ውእቱ እምነ ዔሳው። <sup>37:16</sup>&nbsp;ወኢአምነ ያዕቆብ እስከ ሶበ ቀርቡ ጥቃ ማኅፈድ <sup>37:17</sup>&nbsp;ወዐጸወ አናቅጸ ማኅፈድ። ወቆመ ውስተ ተድባብ ወተናገረ ምስለ እኁሁ ዔሳው ወይቤ ሠናየ ኑዛዜ መጻእከ ትናዝዘኒ በእንተ ብእሲትየ እንተ ሞተት። ዝኑ ውእቱ መሐላ ዘመሐልከ ለአቡከ ወለእምከ ካዕበ ዘእንበለ ይሙት አበስከ እመሐላ ወበሰዓት መሐልከ ለአቡከ ተኰነንከ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>37:14</sup>&nbsp;During all of this, Jacob was unaware that they were coming to him for battle. He, for his part, was mourning for his wife Leah until they approached him near the tower with 4000 warriors, select fighting men. <sup>37:15</sup>&nbsp;The people of Hebron sent word to him: 'Your brother has just now come against you to fight you with 4000 men who have swords buckled on and are carrying shields and weapons'. They told him because they loved Jacob more than Esau, since Jacob was a more generous and kind man than Esau. <sup>37:16</sup>&nbsp;But Jacob did not believe (it) until they came near the tower. <sup>37:17</sup>&nbsp;Then he closed the gates of the tower, stood on the top, and spoke with his brother Esau. He said: 'It is a fine consolation that you have come to give me for my wife who has died. Is this the oath that you swore to your father and your mother two times before he died? You have violated the oath and were condemned in the hour when you swore (it) to your father'.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>37:18</sup>&nbsp;ወውእቱ ጊዜ አውሥአ ዔሳው ወይቤሎ አልቦ ለውሉደ ሰብእ ወለአራዊተ ምድር መሐላ ጽድቅ ዘመሐሉ ምሒሎሙ እስከ ለዓለም። ወእንተ ጸብሐት የኀሥሡ ዝንቱ ለዝንቱ እኩየ ወከመ ይቅትል አሐዱ ጸላኢሁ ወፀረ። <sup>37:19</sup>&nbsp;ወትጸልአኒ አንተ ኪያየ ወውሉድየ እስከ ለዓለም ወአልቦ ገቢረ ምስሌከ ታእኃ። <sup>37:20</sup>&nbsp;ስማዕ ዘንተ ነገርየ ዘአነ እነግረከ እመ ይዌልጥ ሐራውያ ማእሶ ወጸጕሮሂ ከመ ፀምር ለእመ አድከመ ወእመ ወፅአ ዲበ ርእሱ አቅርንት ከመ አቅርንተ ሀየል ወአባግዕ አሜሃ እገብር ምስሌከ ታእኃ። ተፈልጣ አጥባት እምእሞን እስመ ኢኮንከኒ እኅወ። <sup>37:21</sup>&nbsp;ወእመ ገብሩ ተኵላት ሰላመ ምስለ መሐስዕ ከመ ኢይብልዕዎሙ። ወከመ ኢይትአገልዎሙ ወእመ ኮነ አልባቢሆሙ ወአሠንዮ አሜሃ ይከውን በውስተ ልብየ ላዕሌከ ሰላም <sup>37:22</sup>&nbsp;ወለእመ ኮነ አንበሳ ማኅፈሮ ለላህም። ወለእመ ተፀምደ ምስሌሁ በአርዑት ወሐረሰ ምስሌሁ ወገብረ ሰላመ ምስሌሁ አሜሃ እገብር ሰላመ ምስሌከ። <sup>37:23</sup>&nbsp;ወእመ ጻዕደወ ቋዓት ከመ ራዛ አሜሃ አእምር ከመ አፍቀርኩከ ወእገብር ምስሌከ ሰላመ። ተሠረው አንተ ወይሠረዉ ውሉድከ ወኢይኩን ለከ ሰላም። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>37:18</sup>&nbsp;Then Esau said in reply to him: 'Neither mankind nor animals have a true oath which they, once they have sworn, have sworn (it as valid) forever. Everyday they aim at what is bad for one another and at each one killing his enemy and opponent. <sup>37:19</sup>&nbsp;You will hate me and my sons forever. There is no observing of brotherly ties with you. <sup>37:20</sup>&nbsp;Listen to what I have to say to you. If a pig changes its hide and makes its bristles as limp as wool; and if horns like deer's and sheep's horns emerge from its head, then I will observe brotherly ties with you. Since we were separated at our mother's breasts, you have not been a brother to me.[foot]Noting the difficulty in the verse, VanderKam has "The breasts have been separated from their mother, for you have not been a brother to me." We have followed James Kugel's suggestion in <em>A Walk Through Jubilees: Studies in the Book of Jubilees and the World of Its Creation</em> (Brill 2012, p.178) that מאז נפרדנו משדי אמנו might fit better with the Jubilees Qumran fragment 4q223-224 unit 2 col. 4:8.[/foot] "We have followed  <sup>37:21</sup>&nbsp;If wolves make peace with lambs so that they do not eat them or injure them; and if they have resolved to treat them well, then there will be peace in my mind for you. <sup>37:22</sup>&nbsp;If the lion becomes the friend of a bull, and if it is harnessed together with it in a yoke and plows with it and makes peace with it, then I will make peace with you. <sup>37:23</sup>&nbsp;If the raven turns white like the raza-bird, then know that I love you and will make peace with you. (As for) you — be uprooted and may your children be uprooted. There is to be no peace for you'.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>37:24</sup>&nbsp;ወነጊዜ ርእየ ያዕቆብ ከመ አእከየ እምልቡ ላዕሌሁ ወእምኵሉ ነፍሱ ከመ ይቅትሎ። ወመጽአ እንዘ ያንፈርዕፅ ከመ መፍለስ ዘይመጽእ ውስተ ረምሕ ዘይረግዞ ወይቀትሎ ወኢይሴስል እምኔሁ። <sup>37:25</sup>&nbsp;ውእተ ጊዜ ይቤ ለእሊአሁ ወለአግብርቲሁ ከመ ይሩድዎ ወለኵሎሙ ካልአኒሁ።
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>37:24</sup>&nbsp;When Jacob saw that he was adversely inclined toward him from his mind and his entire self so that he could kill him and (that) he had come bounding along like a boar that comes upon the spear which pierces it and kills it but does not pull back from it, <sup>37:25</sup>&nbsp;then he told his own (people) and his servants to attack him and all his companions.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>38:1</sup>&nbsp;ወእምዝ ተናገሮ ይሁዳ ለያዕቆብ አቡሁ ወይቤሎ ምስክ አባ ቀሥተከ ወፈኑ ሐጸከ ወንድፍ ጸላኤ ወቅትል ፀራዌ ወይኩን ለከ ኀይል እስመ ኢንቀትል እኅዋከ ወኀቤከ ውእቱ ወመምስልከ ውእቱ በኀቤነ ለክብር። <sup>38:2</sup>&nbsp;ይእተ ሶቤ ወሰቀ ያዕቆብ ቀሥቶ ወፈነወ ሐጸ ወነደፎ ለዔሳው እኁሁ ወገደሎ <sup>38:3</sup>&nbsp;ወደገመ ፈነወ ሐጸ ወሄጶ አዱራንሃ አራማዌ ጥቦ ፀጋማዌ ወቀተሎ። <sup>38:4</sup>&nbsp;ወእምዝ ወፅኡ ውሉደ ያዕቆብ እሙንቱ ወአግብርቲሆሙ ተናፊቆሙ ውስተ መርብዕተ ማኅፈድ። <sup>38:5</sup>&nbsp;ወወፅአ ይሁዳ ፍጽመ ወንፍታሌም ወጋድ ምስሌሁ ወኀምሳ ደቅ ምስሌሁ እንተ ገጸ ደቡብ ለማኅፈድ ወቀተሉ ኵሎ ዘረከቡ በቅድሜሆሙ ወአልቦ ዘአምሠጠ እምኔሆሙ ወኢአሐዱ። <sup>38:6</sup>&nbsp;ወሌዊ ወዳን ወአሴር ወፅኡ እንተ ገጸ ጽባሑ ለማኅፈድ ወኀምሳ ምስሌሆሙ ወቀተሉ መስተቃትላኒሆሙ ለሞአብ ወለአሞን። <sup>38:7</sup>&nbsp;ወወፅኡ ሮቤል ወርሳኮር ወዛብሎን እንተ ገጸ ሰሜኑ ለማኅፈድ ወኀምሳ ምስሌሆሙ ወቀተሉ መስተባእሳኒሆሙ ለፍልስጥኤም። <sup>38:8</sup>&nbsp;ወወፅኡ ስምዖን ወብንያም ወኤኖክ ወልደ ሮቤል እንተ ገጸ ዐረቢሁ ለማኅፈድ ወኀምሳ ምስሌሆሙ ወቀተሉ እምነ ኤዶም ወእምነ ኮሬዎን አርባዕተ ምእተ ዕደ ጽኑዓነ መስተቃትላነ ወስድስቱ ምእት ጐዩ። ወአርባዕቲሆሙ ደቂቀ ዔሳው ጐዩ ምስሌሆሙ ወኀደጉ አባሆሙ ቅቱለ በከመ ወድቀ ውስተ ወግር ዘይእቲ ውስተ አዱራም። <sup>38:9</sup>&nbsp;ወሰደድዎሙ ውሉደ ያዕቆብ ድኅሬሆሙ እስከ ደብረ ሲኢር። ወያዕቆብሰ ቀበረ እኅዋሁ ውስተ ወግር እንተ ይእቲ ውስተ አዱራም ወገብአ ውስተ ቤቱ። <sup>38:10</sup>&nbsp;ወአመንደብዎሙ ውሉደ ያዕቆብ ለደቂቀ ዔሳው በደብረ ሰኢር ወአትሐቱ ክሳዶሙ ከመ ይከኩኑ አግብርተ ለደቂቀ ያዕቆብ። <sup>38:11</sup>&nbsp;ወለአኩ ኀበ አቡሆሙ እመ ይገብሩ ሰላም ምስሌሆሙ ወለእመ ይቀትልዎሙ። <sup>38:12</sup>&nbsp;ወለአከ ያዕቆብ ኀበ ውሉዱ ከመ ይግበሩ ሰላመ ወገብሩ ምስሌሆሙ ሰላመ ወአንበሩ አርዑተ ቅኔ ላዕሌሆሙ ከመ ይጸብሑ ለያዕቆብ ወለውሉዱ ኵሎ <sup>38:13</sup>&nbsp;ወነበሩ እንዘ ይጼብሑ ለያዕቆብ እስከ አመ ዕለተ ወረደ ያዕቆብ ውስተ ግብጽ። <sup>38:14</sup>&nbsp;ወኢነተጉ ውሉዱ ኤዶም እምአርዑተ ቅኔ ዘዐሠርቱ ወክልኤቱ ውሉደ ያዕቆብ ላዕሌሆሙ እስከ ዛቲ ዕለት 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>38:1</sup>&nbsp;After this Judah spoke to his father Jacob and said to him: 'Draw your bow, father; shoot your arrow; pierce the enemy; and kill the foe. May you have the strength because we will not kill your brother, since he is near to you and, in our estimation, he is equal to you in honor'. <sup>38:2</sup>&nbsp;Jacob then stretched his bow, shot an arrow, pierced his brother Esau [on his right breast], and struck him down. <sup>38:3</sup>&nbsp;He shot another arrow and hit Aduran the Aramean on his left breast; he drove him back and killed him. <sup>38:4</sup>&nbsp;After this Jacob's sons — they and their servants — went out, dividing themselves to the four sides of the tower. <sup>38:5</sup>&nbsp;Judah went out in front. Naphtali and Gad were with him, and 50 servants were with him on the south side of the tower. They killed everyone whom they found in front of them. No one at all escaped from them. <sup>38:6</sup>&nbsp;Levi, Dan, and Asher went out on the east side of the tower, and 50 were with them. They killed the Moabite and Ammonite warriors. <sup>38:7</sup>&nbsp;Reuben, Issachar, and Zebulun went out on the north side of the tower, and 50 were with them. They killed the Philistine fighting men. <sup>38:8</sup>&nbsp;Simeon, Benjamin, and Enoch — Reuben's son — went out on the west side of the tower, and 50 were with them. Of (the people of) Edom and the Horites they killed 400 strong warriors, and 600 ran away. Esau's four sons ran away with them. They left their slain father just as he had fallen on the hill that is in Aduram. <sup>38:9</sup>&nbsp;Jacob's sons pursued them as far as Mt. Seir, while Jacob buried his brother on the hill that is in Aduram and then returned to his house. <sup>38:10</sup>&nbsp;Jacob's sons pressed hard on Esau's sons in Mt. Seir. They bowed their necks to become servants for Jacob's sons. <sup>38:11</sup>&nbsp;They sent to their father (to ask) whether they should make peace with them or kill them. <sup>38:12</sup>&nbsp;Jacob sent word to his sons to make peace. So they made peace with them and placed the yoke of servitude on them so that they should pay tribute to Jacob and his sons for all time. <sup>38:13</sup>&nbsp;They continued paying tribute to Jacob until the day that Jacob went down to Egypt. <sup>38:14</sup>&nbsp;The Edomites have not extricated themselves from the yoke of servitude which Jacob's sons imposed on them until today.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>38:15</sup>&nbsp;ወእሉ ነገሥት እለ ነግሡ በኤዶም ዘእንበለ ይንግሥ ንጉሥ ለውሉደ እስራኤል እስከ ዛቲ ዕለት በምድረ ኤዶም። <sup>38:16</sup>&nbsp;ወነግሠ በኤዶም ባላቅ ወልደ ቦኤር ወስመ ሀገሩ ደናባ። <sup>38:17</sup>&nbsp;ወሞተ ባላቅ ወነግሠ ህየንቴሁ ዮባብ ወልደ ዛራ ዘእምነ ቦሲር። <sup>38:18</sup>&nbsp;ወሞተ ዮባብ ወነግሠ ህየንቴሁ አሳም ዘእምነ ደብረ ቴማን። <sup>38:19</sup>&nbsp;ወሞተ አሳም ወነግሠ ህየንቴሁ አዳት ወልደ ባርድ ዘቀተለ መዕድያምሃ በሐቅለ ሞአብ ወስመ ሀገሩ አውኡቱ። <sup>38:20</sup>&nbsp;ወሞተ አዳት ወነግሠ ህየንቴሁ ሰሎማን ዘእምነ እማሴቃ። <sup>38:21</sup>&nbsp;ወሞተ ሰሎማን ወነገሠ ህየንቴሁ ሳኡል ዘእምነ ራአቦት ፈለግ <sup>38:22</sup>&nbsp;ወሞተ ሳኡል ወነግሠ ህየንቴሁ ብኤሉናን ወልደ አክቡር <sup>38:23</sup>&nbsp;ወሞተ በኤሉናን ወልደ አክቡር ወነግሠ ህየንቴሁ አዳት ወስመ ብእሲቱ መይጠቢት ወለተ መጥሪት ወለተ ሜተቤድዛአብ። <sup>38:24</sup>&nbsp;እሉ ነገሥት እለ ነግሡ በምድረ ኤዶም።
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>38:15</sup>&nbsp;These are the kings who ruled in Edom — before a king ruled the Israelites — until today in the land of Edom. <sup>38:16</sup>&nbsp;Balak, son of Bo'er, became king in Edom. The name of his city was Danaba. <sup>38:17</sup>&nbsp;After Balak died, Yobab son of Zara who was from Bosir became king in his place. <sup>38:18</sup>&nbsp;After Yobab died, Asam who was from Mt. Teman became king in his place. <sup>38:19</sup>&nbsp;After Asam died, Adat son of Bared who slaughtered Midian in the field of Moab became king in his place. The name of his city was Awutu. <sup>38:20</sup>&nbsp;After Adat died, Saloman who was from Emaseqa became king in his place. <sup>38:21</sup>&nbsp;After Saloman died, Saul who was from the river Raabot became king in his place. <sup>38:22</sup>&nbsp;After Saul died, Beelunan son of Akbur became king in his place. <sup>38:23</sup>&nbsp;After Baelunan son of Akbur died, Adat became king in his place. His wife's name was Maytabit, daughter of Matrit, daughter of Metabedezaab. <sup>38:24</sup>&nbsp;These are the kings who ruled in the land of Edom.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>39:1</sup>&nbsp;ወኀደረ ያዕቆብ በምድረ ፍልሰተ አቡሁ ምድረ ከናአን <sup>39:2</sup>&nbsp;እለ ትዝምደ ያዕቆብ። ወዮሴፍሰ ወልደ ዐሠርቱ ወሰብዐቱ ዓመት አውረድዎ ውስተ ግብጽ ወተሣየጦ ፋጢፋራን ኅፅዉ ለፈርዖን ሊቀ መብስላን። <sup>39:3</sup>&nbsp;ወሤሞ ለዮሴፍ ዲበ ኵሉ ቤቱ። ወኮነት በረከተ እግዚአብሔር ውስተ ቤተ ግብጻዊ በእንተ ዮሴፍ ወኵሎ ዘገብረ እግዚአብሔር ይሴርሖ። <sup>39:4</sup>&nbsp;ወኀደገ ግብጻዊ ኵሎ ቅድሜሁ ለዮሴፍ እስመ ርእየ ከመ እግዚአብሔር ምስሌሁ ወኵሎ ዘገብረ እግዚአብሔር ይሴርሖ 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>39:1</sup>&nbsp;Jacob lived in the land where his father had wandered as a foreigner — the land of Canaan. <sup>39:2</sup>&nbsp;This is the history of Jacob. When Joseph was 17 years of age, they brought him down to Egypt, The pharaoh's eunuch Potiphar, the chief cook, bought him. <sup>39:3</sup>&nbsp;He put Joseph in charge of his entire house. The Lord's blessing was (present) in the Egyptian's house because of Joseph. The Lord made everything that he did succeed for him. <sup>39:4</sup>&nbsp;The Egyptian left everything to Joseph because he noticed that the Lord was with him and that the Lord made everything that he did succeed for him.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>39:5</sup>&nbsp;ወዮሴፍሰ ሠናይ ራእዩ ወላሕይ ጥቀ ራእዩ። ወአንሥአት አዕይንቲሃ ብእሲተ እግዚኡ ወርእየቶ ለዮሴፍ ወአፍቀረቶ ወአስተብቍዐቶ ከመ ይስክብ ምስሌሃ <sup>39:6</sup>&nbsp;ወኢመጠወ ነፍሶ። ወተዘከሮ ለእግዚአብሔር ወቃላተ ዘያነብብ ያዕቆብ አቡሁ ዘእምውስተ ቃላተ አብርሃም ከመ አልቦ መነሂ ሰብእ ዘይዜሙ በብእሲት እንተ ባቲ ምተ ከመቦ ኵነኔ ሞት ዘተሠርዐ ሎቱ በሰማያት ቅድመ እግዚአብሔር ልዑል። ወኀጢአት ተዐርግ በእንቲአሁ ውስተ መጻሕፍት ዘለዓለም በኵሉ መዋዕል ቅድመ እግዚአብሔር። <sup>39:7</sup>&nbsp;ወተዘከረ ዮሴፍ ዘንተ ንባበ ወኢፈቀደ ይስክብ ምስሌሃ <sup>39:8</sup>&nbsp;ወአስተብቍዐቶ ዓመተ አሐተ ወካልአ ወአበያ ሰሚዐ <sup>39:9</sup>&nbsp;ወለጠቀቶ ወአኀዘቶ በቤት ከመ ትትባአሶ ይስክብ ምስሌሃ። ወዐፀወት ኆኅተ ቤት ወአኀዘቶ ወኀደገ ልብሶ ውስተ እዴሃ ወሰበረ ማዕፆ ወጐየ አፍአ እምቅድመ ገጻ። <sup>39:10</sup>&nbsp;ወርእየት ይእቲ ብእሲት ከመ ኢይሰክብ ምስሌሃ ወጠቀለቶ ቅድመ እግዚኡ እንዘ ትብል ኪያየ ፈቀደ ገብርከ ዕብራዊ ዘታፈቅር ይትዐገለኒ ከመ ይስክብ ምስሌየ። ወኮነ ሶበ አልዐልኩ ቃልየ ጐየ ወኀደገ ልብሶ ውስተ እዴየ በጊዜ እንተ አኀዝክዎ ወሰበረ ማዕፆ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>39:5</sup>&nbsp;Now Joseph was well formed and very handsome. The wife of his master looked up, saw Joseph, loved him, and pleaded with him to lie with her. <sup>39:6</sup>&nbsp;But he did not surrender himself. He remembered the Lord and what his father Jacob would read to him from the words of Abraham — that no one is to commit adultery with a woman who has a husband; that there is a death penalty which has been ordained for him in heaven before the most high Lord. The sin will be entered regarding him in the eternal books forever before the Lord. <sup>39:7</sup>&nbsp;Joseph remembered what he had said and refused to lie with her. <sup>39:8</sup>&nbsp;She pleaded with him for one year and a second, but he refused to listen to her. <sup>39:9</sup>&nbsp;She drew him close and held on to him in the house in order to compel him to he with her. She closed the door of the house and held on to him. He left his clothes in her hands, broke the door, and ran away from her to the outside. <sup>39:10</sup>&nbsp;When that woman saw that he would not lie with her, she accused him falsely to his master: 'Your Hebrew slave whom you love wanted to force me so that he could lie with me. When I shouted, he ran away, left his clothes in my hands when I grabbed him, and broke the door'. <sup>39:11</sup>&nbsp;When the Egyptian saw Joseph's clothes and the broken door, he believed what his wife said. He put Joseph in prison in the place where the prisoners whom the king imprisoned would stay.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>39:11</sup>&nbsp;ወርእየ ግብጻዊ ልብሰ ዮሴፍ ወማዕፆ ስቡረ። ወሰምዐ ነገረ ብእሲቱ ወወደዮ ለዮሴፍ ቤተ ሞቅሕ ውስተ መካን ኀበ ይነብሩ ሙቁሓን እለ ሞቅሐ ንጉሥ <sup>39:12</sup>&nbsp;ወሀሎ ህየ ውስተ ሞቅሕ። ወወሀቦ እግዚአብሔር ሞገሰ ለዮሴፍ በቅድሜሁ ለሊቀ ዐቀብተ ሞቅሕ ወምሕረተ በቅድሜሁ እስመ ርእየ ከመ እግዚአብሔር ምስሌሁ ወኵሎ ዘገብረ እግዚአብሔር ይሴርሖ። <sup>39:13</sup>&nbsp;ወኀደገ ኵሎ ቅድሜሁ ወአልቦ ሊቀ ዐቀብተ ሞቅሕ ዘያአምር ምስሌሁ ምንተኒ እስመ ዮሴፍ ኵሎ ይገብር ወእግዚአብሔር ይፌጽም ወነበረ ህየ ክልኤተ ዓመተ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>39:12</sup>&nbsp;While he was there in the prison, the Lord gave Joseph a favorable reception before the chief of the prison guards and and a kind reception before him because he saw that the Lord was with him and that the Lord was making everything that he did succeed for him. <sup>39:13</sup>&nbsp;He left everything to him. The chief of the prison guards knew nothing at all about his affairs because Joseph would do everything and the Lord would bring (it) to completion. He remained there for two years.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>39:14</sup>&nbsp;ወበውእቱ መዋዕል ተምዕዐ ፈርዖን ንጉሠ ግብጽ ላዕለ ክልኤቱ ኅጽዋኒሁ ላዕለ ሊቀ መዘርት ወላዕለ ሊቀ ኀበዝት ወወደዮሙ ውስተ ሞቅሕ ውስተ ቤቱ ለሊቀ መበስላን ውስተ ሞቅሕ ኀበ ሀሎ ዮሴፍ እኁዝ ህየ። <sup>39:15</sup>&nbsp;ወሠርዖ ለዮሴፍ ሊቀ ዐቀብተ ሞቅሕ ከመ ይትለአኮሙ ወይትለአክ በቅድሜሁ <sup>39:16</sup>&nbsp;ወሐለሙ ክልኤሆሙ ሕልመ ሊቀ መዘርት ወሊቀ ሐበዝት ወነገርዎ ለዮሴፍ <sup>39:17</sup>&nbsp;ወበከመ ፈከረ ሎሙ ከማሁ ኮኖሙ። ወለሊቀ መዘርት አግብኦ ፈርዖን ውስተ ግብሩ ወለሐባዚሰ ሰቀሎ በከመ ፈከረ ሎቱ ዮሴፍ። <sup>39:18</sup>&nbsp;ወረስዖ ሊቀ መዘርት ለዮሴፍ በቤተ ሞቅሕ እስመ አይድዖ ዘይከውኖ ወኢተዘከረ ከመ ያይድዕ ለፈርዖን ዘከመ ነገሮ ዮሴፍ እስመ ረስዐ።
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>39:14</sup>&nbsp;At that time the pharaoh, the king of Egypt, became angry at two of his eunuchs — the chief butler and the chief baker. He put them in prison, in the house of the chief cook, in the prison where Joseph was held. <sup>39:15</sup>&nbsp;The chief of the prison guards appointed Joseph to serve them. So he would serve in his presence. <sup>39:16</sup>&nbsp;Both of them — the chief butler and the chief baker — had a dream and told it to Joseph. <sup>39:17</sup>&nbsp;Things turned out for them just as he interpreted for them. The pharaoh restored the chief butler to his job, but he hanged the baker as Joseph had interpreted for him. <sup>39:18</sup>&nbsp;The chief butler forgot Joseph in prison although he had informed him (about) what would happen to him. He did not remember to tell the pharaoh how Joseph had told him because he forgot.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>40:1</sup>&nbsp;ወበውእቱ መዋዕል ሐለመ ፈርዖን ሕልመ ክልኤተ በአሐቲ ሌሊት በእንተ ነገረ ዐባር ዘይከውን ዲበ ኵሉ ምድር ወነቅሀ እምንዋሙ ወጸውዖሙ ለኵሎሙ መፈክራነ ሕልም እለ ውስተ ግብጽ ወረቀይት ወነገሮሙ ክልኤሆሙ ሕልሞ ወኢክህሉ አእምሮ። <sup>40:2</sup>&nbsp;ወእምዝ ተዘከሮ ለዮሴፍ ሊቀ መዘርት ወነገረ በእንቲአሁ ለንጉሥ ወአውፅእዎ እምነ ቤተ ሞቅሕ ወነገረ በቅድሜሁ ክልኤሆሙ ሕለሚሁ። <sup>40:3</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤ በቅድሜሁ ለፈርዖን ከመ ክልኤሆሙ ሕለሚሁ አሐዱ እሙንቱ። ወይቤሎ ሰብዐቱ ዓመት ይመጽእ ጽጋብ ውስተ ኵሉ ምድረ ግብጽ ወእምድኅረዝ ሰብዐቱ ዓመተ ዐባር ዘኢኮነ ከማሁ ዐባር ውስተ ኵሉ ምድር። <sup>40:4</sup>&nbsp;ወይእዜኒ ይሥራዕ ፈርዖን ውስተ ኵሉ ምድረ ግብጽ ከያደ ወይዝግቡ ሲሲተ ለሀገር ውስተ ሀገር በመዋዕለ ዓመታት ዘጽጋብ ወይከውን ሲሲተ ለሰብዐቱ ዓመታተ ዐባር ወኢትትሐጐል ምድር እምቅድመ ገጸ ዐባር እስመ ኀያል ይከውን ጥቀ። <sup>40:5</sup>&nbsp;ወወሀቦ እግዚአብሔር ለዮሴፍ ሞገሰ ወምሕረተ በቅድመ አዕይንቲሁ ለፈርዖን ወይቤ ፈርዖን ለላእካኒሁ ኢንረክብ ብእሴ ጠቢበ ወማእምረ ዘከመዝ ብእሲ እስመ መንፈሰ እግዚአብሔር ምስሌሁ። <sup>40:6</sup>&nbsp;ወሤሞ ዳግመ ውስተ ኵሉ መንግሥቱ ወአኰነኖ ውስተ ኵሉ ግብጽ ወአጽዐኖ ዲበ ሰረገላሁ ካዕብ ዘፈርዖን <sup>40:7</sup>&nbsp;ወአልበሶ ልብሰ ቢሶስ ወአዕነቆ ባዝግና ወርቅ ውስተ ክሳዱ። ወሰበከ በቅድሜሁ ወይቤ ኢል ኢል ወአቢርር ወወሀቦ ማዕተበ ውስተ እዴሁ ወአመበሎ ዲበ ኵሉ ቤቱ ወአዕበዮ። ወይቤሎ ኢየዐቢ እምኔከ ዘእንበለ መንበር ባሕቲቶ 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>40:1</sup>&nbsp;At that time the pharaoh had two dreams in one night about the subject of the famine which would come on the whole land. When he awakened, he summoned all the dream interpreters who were in Egypt and the enchanters. He told them his two dreams, but they were unable to understand (them). <sup>40:2</sup>&nbsp;Then the chief butler remembered Joseph. After he had told the king about him, he was brought from prison and he related his two dreams in his presence. <sup>40:3</sup>&nbsp;He said in the pharaoh's presence that his two dreams were one. He said to him: 'Seven years are coming (in which there will be) abundance in the entire land of Egypt, but afterwards there will be a seven-year famine, the like of which famine has never been in the entire land. <sup>40:4</sup>&nbsp;Now let the pharaoh appoint overseers throughout the entire land of Egypt and let them store each city's food in the city during the period of the years of abundance. Then there will be food for the seven years of famine, and the land will not be destroyed because of the famine, since it will be very severe'. <sup>40:5</sup>&nbsp;The Lord gave Joseph a favorable and kind reception in the view of the pharaoh. The pharaoh said to his servants: 'We will not find a man as wise and knowledgeable as this man, for the spirit of the Lord is with him'. <sup>40:6</sup>&nbsp;He appointed him as the second (in command) in his entire kingdom, gave him authority over all Egypt, and allowed him to ride on his second chariot which was the pharaoh's. <sup>40:7</sup>&nbsp;He dressed him with clothing made of hnen and hung a gold chain on his neck. He made a proclamation before him and said: 'El, El the Mighty One of El'.[foot]from "Il il and abirer." Cf. VanderKam, footnote p. 265: RONSCH (<em>Das Buch der Jubilaen</em>, 158- 59) and Charles (1902, p. 226, n.): “אל אל ואביר אל.” They also noted the parallel in Joseph and Aseneth 3:4; 18:1-2; 21:21, where Joseph is called ό δυνατὸς τοῦ θεοῦ (see also Berger, 519, n. b to v 7).[/foot] He put a signet ring on his hand and made him ruler over his entire household. He made him great and said to him: 'I will not be greater than you except with regard to the throne only'.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>40:8</sup>&nbsp;ወመበለ ዮሴፍ ውስተ ኵሉ ምድረ ግብጽ ወአፍቅርዎ ኵሎሙ መኳንንቲሁ ለፈርዖን ወኵሎሙ ላእካኒሁ ወኵሎሙ እለ ይገብሩ ግብረ ንጉሥ። እስመ በርትዕ የሐውር ወአልቦ ትዕቢተ ወአዕብዮ ልብ ወነሢአ ገጽ ወአልቦ ነሢአ ሕልያን እስመ በርትዕ ይኴንን ለኵሉ አሕዛበ ምድር። <sup>40:9</sup>&nbsp;ወተሰናአወት ምድረ ግብድ በቅድሜሁ ለፈርዖን በእንተ ዮሴፍ እስመ እግዚአብሔር ምስሌሁ ወወሀቦ ሞገሰ ወምሕረተ ላዕለ ኵሎሙ ዘመዱ በቅድመ ኵሎሙ እለ ያአምርዎ ወለእለ ይሰምዑ ስምዐ ምስሌሁ ወረትዐት መንግሥተ ፈርዖን ወአልቦ ሰይጣነ ወአልቦ እኩየ <sup>40:10</sup>&nbsp;ወጸውዐ ንጉሥ ስሞ ለዮሴፍ ስፋንጢፋንስ። ወወሀቦ ወለተ ፉጢፋራን ብእሲተ ለዮሴፍ ወለተ ሳውዕ ዘኢሊዮጰሊስ ሊቀ መብስላን <sup>40:11</sup>&nbsp;ወበዕለተ ቆመ ዮሴፍ ኀበ ፈርዖን ወልደ ሠላሳ ክረምት አመ ቆመ ቅድመ ፈርዖን። <sup>40:12</sup>&nbsp;ወበውእቱ ዓመት ሞተ ይስሐቅ ወበጽሐ በከመ ነገረ ዮሴፍ በእንተ ፍካሬ ክልኤቱ ሕልሙ ዘከመ ነገሮ ወኮነ ሰብዐቱ ክረምት ዘጽጋብ ውስተ ኵሉ ምድረ ግብጽ ወፈርየት ምድረ ብዙኀ አሐቲ መስፈርት ዐሠርተ ወሰማኒተ ምእተ መሳፍረ። <sup>40:13</sup>&nbsp;ወአስተጋብአ ዮሴፍ ሲሲተ ለሀገር ውስተ ሀገር እስከ መልአ ሥርናይ እስከ ሶበ ይስእኑ ኆልቆቶ ወሰፊረ እምነ ብዝኁ።
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>40:8</sup>&nbsp;So Joseph became ruler over the entire land of Egypt. All of the pharaoh's princes, all of his servants, and all who were doing the king's work loved him because he conducted himself in a just way. He was not arrogant, proud, or partial, nor did he accept bribes because he was ruling all the people of the land in a just way. <sup>40:9</sup>&nbsp;The land of Egypt lived in harmony before the pharaoh because of Joseph for the Lord was with him. He gave him a favorable and kind reception for all his family before all who knew him and who heard reports about him.
