The pharaoh's rule was just, and there was no satan or any evil one. <sup>40:10</sup>&nbsp;The king named Joseph Sefantifanes[foot]i.e., צפנותת פענח (Genesis 41:45)[/foot] and gave Joseph as a wife the daughter of Potiphar, the daughter of the priest of Heliopolis — the chief cook. <sup>40:11</sup>&nbsp;On the day when Joseph took up his position with the pharaoh he was 30 years of age when he took up his position with the pharaoh. <sup>40:12</sup>&nbsp;(Isaac died that year). Things turned out just as Joseph had reported about the interpretation of his two dreams, just as he had reported to him. There were seven years of abundance in the whole land of Egypt. The land of Egypt was most productive: one measure (would produce) 1800 measures. <sup>40:13</sup>&nbsp;Joseph collected (each) city's food in the city until it was so full of wheat that it was impossible to count or measure it because of its quantity.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>41:1</sup>&nbsp;ወበአርብ ወኀምስቱ ኢዮቤልዉ ወዳግም ሱባዔ በዓመት ካልእ ነሥአ ይሁዳ ለዔር በኵሩ ብእሲተ እምነ አዋልደ አራም ወስማ ትዕማር። <sup>41:2</sup>&nbsp;ወጸልአ ወኢሰከበ ምስሌሃ እስመ እምአዋልደ ከናአን እሙ ወፈቀደ ይንሣእ ሎቱ ብእሲተ እምነገደ እሙ ወኢአብሖ ይሁዳ አቡሁ። <sup>41:3</sup>&nbsp;ወውእቱ ዔር በኵሩ ለይሁዳ እኩይ ወቀተሎ እግዚአብሔር። <sup>41:4</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤ ይሁዳ ለአውናን እኁሁ ባእ ኀበ ብእሲተ እኁሁ ወረስያ ኑዕልተ ወአንሥእ ዘርአ ለእኁከ። <sup>41:5</sup>&nbsp;ወአእመረ አውናን ከመ ኢኮነ ዘዚአሁ ዘርእ ክመ ዘእኁሁ። ወቦአ ቤተ ብእሲተ እኁሁ ወከዐወ ዘርአ ውስተ ምድር። ወእኩየ ኮነ በቅድመ አዕይንተ እግዚአብሔር ወቀተሎ። <sup>41:6</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤ ይሁዳ ለትዕማር መርዓቱ ንበሪ ቤተ አቡኪ እንዘ ትመዐስቢ እስከ አመ ይልህቅ ሴሎም ወልድየ ወእሁበኪ ሎቱ ብእሲተ። <sup>41:7</sup>&nbsp;ወልህቀ ወኢኀደገት ቤድሱኤል ብእሲተ ይሁዳ ሴሎምሃ ወልዳ ከመ ያውስብ። ወሞተት ቤድሱኤል ብእሲተ ይሁዳ በዓመት ኃምስ ዘዝ ሱባዔ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>41:1</sup>&nbsp;In the forty-fifth jubilee, the second week during the second year [2165], Judah took as a wife for his first-born Er one of the Aramean women whose name was Tamar. <sup>41:2</sup>&nbsp;He hated (her) and did not lie with her because his mother was a Canaanite woman and he wanted to marry someone from his mother's tribe. But his father Judah did not allow him. <sup>41:3</sup>&nbsp;That Er, Judah's first-born, was evil, and the Lord killed him. <sup>41:4</sup>&nbsp;Then Judah said to his brother Onan: 'Go in to your brother's wife, perform the levirate duty for her, and produce descendants for your brother'. <sup>41:5</sup>&nbsp;Onan knew that the descendants would not be his but his brother's, so he entered the house of his brother's wife and poured out the semen on the ground. In the Lord's estimation it was an evil act, and he killed him. <sup>41:6</sup>&nbsp;So Judah said to his daughter-in-law Tamar: 'Remain in your father's house as a widow until my son Selom grows up. Then I will give you to him as a wife'. <sup>41:7</sup>&nbsp;He grew up, but Judah's wife Bedsuel did not allow her son Selom to marry (her). Judah's wife Bedsuel died during the fifth year of this week [2168].
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>41:8</sup>&nbsp;ወበሳድስ ዓመቱ ዐርገ ይሁዳ ይቅርጽ አባግዒሁ በቴምናታ። ወነገርዋ ለትዕማር ናሁ ሐሙኪ የዐርግ ይቅርጽ አባግዒሁ በቴምናታ። <sup>41:9</sup>&nbsp;ወአንበረት አልባሰ ምዕስብናሃ ወለብሰት ግልባቤ ወተሠነየት ወነበረት ውስተ አንቀጽ እንተ መንገለ ፍኖተ ቴምናታ። <sup>41:10</sup>&nbsp;ወእንዘ የሐውር ይሁዳ ረከባ ወተሐዘባ ከመ ዘማዊት ወይቤላ እባእ ኀቤኪ ወትቤሎ ባእ ወቦአ። <sup>41:11</sup>&nbsp;ወትቤሎ ሀበኒ ደነስየ ወይቤላ አልብየ ውስተ እዴየ ዘእንበለ ሕልቀት ዘአጽባዕትየ ወድጕልማየ ወበትርየ ዘውስተ እዴየ <sup>41:12</sup>&nbsp;ወትቤሎ ሀበኒ ኪያሆሙ እስከ ሶበ ትፌኑ ሊተ ደነስየ። ወይቤላ አነ እፌኑ ለኪ መሕስአ ጠሊ ወወሀባ ኪያሆሙ ላቲ [ወሀሎ ምስሌሃ] ወጸንሰት ሎቱ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>41:8</sup>&nbsp;In its sixth year [2169] Judah went up to shear his sheep in Timnah. Tamar was told: 'Your father-in-law is now going up to shear his sheep in Timnah'. <sup>41:9</sup>&nbsp;Then she put aside her widow's clothing, put on a veil, made herself up, and sat down at the gate near the road to Timnah. <sup>41:10</sup>&nbsp;As Judah was going along, he found her and supposed that she was a prostitute. He said to her: 'Let me come in to you'. She said to him: 'Come in'. So he came in. <sup>41:11</sup>&nbsp;She said to him: 'Give me my fee'. He said to her: 'I have nothing with me except the ring on my finger, my neck chain, and my staff which is in my hand'. <sup>41:12</sup>&nbsp;She said to him: 'Give them to me until you send me my fee'. He said to her: 'I will send you a kid'. He gave them to her. [After he was with her], she became pregnant by him.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>41:13</sup>&nbsp;ወሖረ ይሁዳ ውስተ አባግዒሁ ወይእቲኒ ሖረት ቤተ አቡሃ። <sup>41:14</sup>&nbsp;ወፈነወ ይሁዳ መሕስአ በእደ ኖላዊሁ አዶላማዊ ወኀጥአ ወተስእሎሙ ለሰብአ ብሔር እንዘ ይብል አይቴ ሀለወት ዘማዊት እንተ ዝየ ወይቤልዎ አልቦ ዝየስ ዘማዊት ወአልብነ ኀቤነ ዘማዊተ <sup>41:15</sup>&nbsp;ወገብአ ወአይድዖ ከመ ኀጥአ ወይቤሎ ተስእልኩ ሰብአ ብሔርኒ ወይቤሉኒ አልቦ ዝየስ ዘማዊተ። ወይቤ ተንሥእ ከመ ኢንኩን ለስላቅ 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>41:13</sup>&nbsp;Then Judah went to his sheep, but she went to her father's house. <sup>41:14</sup>&nbsp;Judah sent the kid through his Adullamite shepherd, but he failed to find (her). He asked the men of the area: 'Where is the prostitute who was here'? They said to him: 'There is no prostitute here, nor do we have any prostitute with us'. <sup>41:15</sup>&nbsp;When he returned and told him that he had failed to find (her), he said to him: 'I asked the men of the area and they said to me: «There is no prostitute here»'. He said: 'Let her keep (them) so that we may not become the object of mockery'.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>41:16</sup>&nbsp;ወእንዘ አእከለት ሠለስተ አውራኀ ተዐውቀት ከመ ፀንሰት ይእቲ። ወነገርዎ ለይሁዳ እንዘ ይብሉ ናሁ ትዕማር መርዐትከ ፀንሰት በዝሙት። <sup>41:17</sup>&nbsp;ወሖረ ይሁዳ ቤተ አቡሃ ወይቤሎሙ ለአቡሃ ወለአኀዊሃ አውፅእዋ ወያውዕይዋ እስመ ገብረት ርኵሰ በውስተ እስራኤል። <sup>41:18</sup>&nbsp;ወኮነ ሶበ አውፅእዋ ከመ ያውዕይዋ ፈነወት ለሐሙሃ ሕልቀተ ወድጕልማ ወበትረ ወትቤ አእምርአ ዘመኑአ ዝንቱአ እስመአ ሎቱአ ፀነስኩአ። <sup>41:19</sup>&nbsp;ወአእመረ ይሁዳ ወይቤ ጸድቀት ትዕማር እምኔየ ወኢያውዕይዋ እንከ <sup>41:20</sup>&nbsp;ወበእንተዝ ኢተውህበት ለሴሎም ወኢደገመ እንከ ቀሪቦታ። <sup>41:21</sup>&nbsp;ወእምዝ ፀንሰት ወወለደት ክልኤተ ደቀ ፋሬስሃ ወዛራሃ በዓመት ሳብዕ ዘዝንቱ ሱባዔ ዘዳግም <sup>41:22</sup>&nbsp;ወእምዝ ተፈጸመ ሰብዐቱ ዓመት ዘሰምር ዘይቤሎ ዮሴፍ ለፈርዖን። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>41:16</sup>&nbsp;When she reached three months, she was visibly pregnant. Judah was told: 'Your daughter-in-law Tamar has now become pregnant through prostitution'. <sup>41:17</sup>&nbsp;Judah went to her father's house and said to her father and brothers: 'Bring her out and let her be burned because she has done something impure in Israel'. <sup>41:18</sup>&nbsp;When she was brought out to be burned, she sent the ring, the neck chain, and the staff to her father-in-law and said: 'Recognize whose these are because I am pregnant by him'. <sup>41:19</sup>&nbsp;Judah recognized (them) and said: 'Tamar has been more just than I; therefore, do not burn her'. <sup>41:20</sup>&nbsp;For this reason she was not given to Selom, and he did not approach her again. <sup>41:21</sup>&nbsp;Afterwards she was pregnant and gave birth to two boys — Perez and Zerah — during the seventh year of this second week [2170]. <sup>41:22</sup>&nbsp;Following this the seven years of copious harvest (about) which Joseph had told the pharaoh were completed.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>41:23</sup>&nbsp;ወአእመረ ይሁዳ ከመ እኩይ ግብር ዘገብረ እስመ ሰከበ ምስለ መርዓቱ ወአስተሐሠመ በቅድመ አዕይንቲሁ ወአእመረ ከመ አበሰ ወስሕተ እስመ ከሠተ ክድነተ ወልዱ ወአኀዘ ይላሑ ወይትመሐለል ቅድመ እግዚአብሔር በእንተ አበሳሁ። <sup>41:24</sup>&nbsp;ወነገርናሁ በሕልም ከመ ይሰረይ ሎቱ እስመ ተማሕለለ ጥቀ ወእስመ ላሐወ ወኢገብረ እንከ <sup>41:25</sup>&nbsp;ወኮነ ሎቱ ስርየት እስመ ተመይጠ እምኀጢአቱ ወእምኢያእምሮቱ እስመ ዐቢይ አበሳ አምላክነ። ወኵሉ ዘይገብር ከመዝ ኵሉ ዘይሰክብ ምስለ ሐማቱ ያውዕይዎ በእሳት ከመ የዐይ ቦቱ እስመ ርኵስ ወግማኔ ኮነ ላዕሌሆሙ በእሳት ያውዕይዎሙ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>41:23</sup>&nbsp;Judah knew that what he had done was evil because he had lain with his daughter-in-law. In his own view he considered it evil, and he knew that he had done wrong and erred, for he had uncovered his son's covering. He began to lament and plead before the Lord because of his sin. <sup>41:24</sup>&nbsp;We told him in a dream that it would be forgiven for him because he had pleaded very much and because he had lamented and did not do (it) again. <sup>41:25</sup>&nbsp;He had forgiveness because he turned from his sin and from his ignorance, for the sin was a great one before our God. Anyone who acts in this way — anyone who lies with his mother-in-law — is to be burned in fire so that he burns in it because impurity and contamination have come on them. They are to be burned.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>41:26</sup>&nbsp;ወአንተኒ አዝዞሙ ለውሉደ እስራኤል ወኢይኩን ርኵስ በማእከሎሙ እስመ ኵሉ ዘይሰክብ ምስለ መርዓቱ ወምስለ ሐማቱ ርኵሰ ገብረ በእሳት ያውዕዩ ብእሴ ዘሰከበ ምስሌሃ ወብእሲተኒ ወየኀድግ መዓተ ወመቅሠፍተ እምእስራኤል። <sup>41:27</sup>&nbsp;ወለይሁዳኒ ነገርናሁ ከመ ኢሰከቡ ምስሌሃ ክልኤሆሙ ደቂቁ። በእንተዝ ቆመ ዘርኡ ለካልእ ነገድ። ወኢይሤረዉ <sup>41:28</sup>&nbsp;እስመ በየውሀተ አዕይንቲሁ ሖረ ወኀሠሠ ኵነኔ እስመ እምፍትሐ አብርሃም ዘአዘዞሙ ለውሉዱ ፈቀደ ይሁዳ ያውዕያ በእሳት።
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>41:26</sup>&nbsp;Now you order the Israelites that there is to be no impurity among them, for anyone who lies with his daughter-in-law or his mother-in-law has done something that is impure. They are to burn the man who lay with her and the woman. Then he will make anger and punishment desist from Israel. <sup>41:27</sup>&nbsp;We told Judah that his two sons had not lain with her. For this reason his descendants were established for another generation and would not be uprooted. <sup>41:28</sup>&nbsp;For in his integrity he had gone and demanded punishment because Judah had wanted to burn her on the basis of the law which Abraham had commanded his children.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>42:1</sup>&nbsp;ወበቀዳሚ ዓመት ዘሱባዔ ሣልስ ዘአርብዓ ወኀምስቱ ኢዮቤልው አኀዘ ዐባር ይምጻእ ውስተ ምድር ወአበየ ዝናም ተውህቦ ለምድር እስመ አልቦ ምንተኒ ዘይወርድ <sup>42:2</sup>&nbsp;ወዐብረት ምድር። ወበምድረ ግብጽ ባሕቱ ቦቱ ሲሲተ እስመ አስተጋብአ ዮሴፍ ዘርአ በምድር በሰብዐቱ ዓመት ዘሠምር ወዐቀቦ <sup>42:3</sup>&nbsp;ወመጽኡ ግብጽ ኀበ ዮሴፍ ከመ የሀቦሙ ሲሲተ ወከሠተ መዛግብተ ኀበ ሀሎ ሥርናይ ዘቀዳሚ ዓመት ወሤጠ ለአሕዛበ ምድር በወርቅ። <sup>42:4</sup>&nbsp;ወሰምዐ ያዕቆብ ከመ ቦቱ ሲሲተ ውስተ ግብጽ ወፈነወ ዐሠርተ ደቆ ከመ ይንሥኡ ሎቱ ሲሲተ በግብጽ ወብንያምሃሰ ኢፈነወ። ወበጽሑ ምስለ ዘየሐውር <sup>42:5</sup>&nbsp;ወአእመሮ ዮሴፍ ወእሙንቱሰ ኢያእመርዎ። ወተናገረ ምስሌሆሙ ወተስእሎሙ ወይቤሎሙ አኮኑ ሰብአ ዐይን አንትሙ ወመጻእክሙ ታስተሐይጹ አሰረ ምድር ወዐጸዎሙ። <sup>42:6</sup>&nbsp;ወእምዝ ፈትሖሙ ወአቀመ ስምዖንሃ ባሕቲቶ ወተስዐተ አኀዊሁ ፈነወ <sup>42:7</sup>&nbsp;ወመልአ አሕስሊሆሙ ሥርናየ ወወርቆሙሂ ወደየ ሎሙ ውስተ አሕስሊሆሙ ወኢያእመሩ። <sup>42:8</sup>&nbsp;ወአዘዞሙ ከመ ያምጽኡ እኅዋሆሙ ዘይንእስ እስመ ነገርዎ ከመ ሀሎ አቡሆሙ ሕያው ወእኁሆሙ ዘይንእስ። <sup>42:9</sup>&nbsp;ወዐርጉ እምድረ ግብጽ ወበጽሑ ምድረ ከናአን ወነገሩ ለአቡሆሙ ኵሎ ዘከመ ረከቦሙ ወእፎ ተናገረ ምስሌሆሙ መኰንነ ብሔር ዐጸብጺበ ወአኀዞ ለስምዖን እስከ ሶበ ያመጽእዎ ለብንያም። <sup>42:10</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤ ያዕቆብ አምከንክሙኒኬ ወዮሴፍኒ ኢሀሎ ወስምዖንሂ ኢሀሎ ወብንያምሃኒ ትነሥእዎ ላዕሌየኬ ኮነ እከይክሙ። <sup>42:11</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤ ኢየሐውር ወልድየ ምስሌክሙ እመቦ ከመ ደወየ። እስመ ክልኤተ ወለደት እሞሙ ወአሐዱ ተሐጕለ ወዘንተኒ ትነሥኡኒ እመቦ ከመ ፈፀነ በፍኖት ወታወርዱ ሊተ ርስእየ በሐዘን ውስተ ሞት። <sup>42:12</sup>&nbsp;እስመ ርእየ ከመ ገብአ ወርቆሙ ኵሉ በዕቈሪሁ ወበዝ ፈርሀ ፈንዎቶ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>42:1</sup>&nbsp;During the first year of the third week of the forty-fifth jubilee [2171], the famine began to come to the land. The rain refused to be given to the earth because there was nothing which was coming down. <sup>42:2</sup>&nbsp;The earth became unproductive, but in the land of Egypt there was food because Joseph had gathered the seed in the land during the seven years of copious harvest and kept it. <sup>42:3</sup>&nbsp;When the Egyptians came to Joseph so that he would give them food, he opened the storehouses where the grain of the first year was and sold (it) to the people of the land in exchange for money. <sup>42:4</sup>&nbsp;Jacob heard that there was food in Egypt, so he sent his ten sons to get food for him in Egypt. But he did not send Benjamin. They arrived with those who were going (there). <sup>42:5</sup>&nbsp;Joseph recognized them, but they did not recognize him. He spoke with them, asked them questions, and said to them: 'Are you not spies? You have come to investigate the paths of the land'. He then imprisoned them. <sup>42:6</sup>&nbsp;Afterwards he released them. He detained only Simeon and sent his nine brothers away. <sup>42:7</sup>&nbsp;He filled their sacks with grain and put their money in their sacks. But they did not know (this). <sup>42:8</sup>&nbsp;He ordered them to bring their youngest brother because they had told him that their father was alive and their youngest brother (also). <sup>42:9</sup>&nbsp;They went up from the land of Egypt and came to the land of Canaan. They told their father everything that had happened to them and how the ruler of the area had spoken harshly with them and was holding Simeon until they should bring Benjamin. <sup>42:10</sup>&nbsp;Jacob said: 'Me you have deprived of children. Joseph does not exist nor does Simeon exist, and you are going to take Benjamin. Your wickedness has come upon me'. <sup>42:11</sup>&nbsp;He said: 'My son will not go with you. Perhaps he would become ill. For their mother gave birth to two; one has died and this one, too, you will take from me. Perhaps he would catch a fever on the way. Then you would bring down my old age in sorrow to death'. <sup>42:12</sup>&nbsp;For he saw that their money was returned — each one in his purse, and he was afraid to send him for this reason.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>42:13</sup>&nbsp;ወዐባርኒ በዝኀ ወኀየለ በምድረ ከናአን ወበኵሉ ምድር ዘእንበለ ምድረ ግብጽ። እስመ ብዙኃን እምውሉደ ግብጽ ዘገቡ ዘርኦሙ ለሲሲት እምዘ ርእይዎ ለዮሴፍ ከመ ያስተጋብእ ዘርአ ወይሠይም ውስተ መዛግብት ወየዐቅብ ለዓመተ ዐባር። <sup>42:14</sup>&nbsp;ወተሴሰይዎ ሰብአ ግብጽ በቀዳሚ ዓመት ዘዐባር 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>42:13</sup>&nbsp;Now the famine grew increasingly severe in the land of Canaan and in every land except the land of Egypt because many Egyptians had stored their seed for food after they saw Joseph collecting seed, placing (it) in storehouses, and keeping (it) for the years of the famine. <sup>42:14</sup>&nbsp;The Egyptians fed themselves with it during the first year of the famine.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>42:15</sup>&nbsp;ወሶበ ርእየ እስራኤል ከመ ኀየለ ጥቀ ዐባር ውስተ ምድር ወአልቦ ድኂነ ወይቤ ለውሉዱ ሖሩ ግብኡ ወንሥኡ ለነ ሲሲተ ኢንሙት <sup>42:16</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤሉ ኢነሐውር እመ ኢመጽአ እኁነ ዘይንእስ ምስሌነ ኢነሐውር <sup>42:17</sup>&nbsp;ወርእየ እስራኤል ከመ እመ ኢፈነዎ ምስሌሆሙ ይትሐጐሉ ኵሎሙ እምቅድመ ዐባር። <sup>42:18</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤ ሮቤል ሀበንዮ ውስተ እዴየ ወለእመ ኢያግባእክዎ ለከ ቅትል ክልኤተ ውሉድየ ህየንተ ነፍሰ ዚአሁ። ወይቤሎ ኢየሐውር ምስሌከ <sup>42:19</sup>&nbsp;ወቀርበ ይሁዳ ወይቤ ፈንዎ ምስሌነ ወለእመ ኢያግባእክዎ ለከ እቡሰ እኩን በቅድሜከ ኵሎ መዋዕለ ሕይወትየ። <sup>42:20</sup>&nbsp;ወፈነዎ ምስሌሆሙ በካልእ ዓመት ዘዝ ሱባዔ በሠርቀ ወርኅ ወበጽሑ ብሔረ ግብጽ ምስለ ኵሎሙ እለ የሐውሩ ወአምኃሆሙ ውስተ እደዊሆሙ ማየ ልብን ወከርካዕ ወጤሬቤንቶስ ወጸቃውዐ መዓር 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>42:15</sup>&nbsp;When Israel saw that the famine was very severe in the land and (that) there was no relief, he said to his sons: 'Go, return, and get us (some) food so that we may not die'. <sup>42:16</sup>&nbsp;But they said: 'We will not go. If our youngest brother does not come with us, we will not go'. <sup>42:17</sup>&nbsp;Israel saw that if he did not send him with them they would all die because of the famine. <sup>42:18</sup>&nbsp;Then Reuben said: 'Put him under my control. If I do not bring him back to you, kill my two sons for his life'. But he said to him: 'He will not go with you'. <sup>42:19</sup>&nbsp;Then Judah approached and said: 'Send him with us. If I do not bring him back to you, then let me be guilty before you throughout my entire lifetime'. <sup>42:20</sup>&nbsp;So he sent him with them during the second year of this week [2172], on the first of the month. They arrived in the territory of Egypt with all who were going (there) and (had) their gifts in their hands: stacte, almonds, terebinth nuts, and pure honey.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>42:21</sup>&nbsp;ወበጽሑ ወቆሙ ቅድመ ዮሴፍ ወርእየ ብንያምሃ እኅዋሁ ወአእመሮ ወይቤሎሙ ዝኑ እኁክሙ ዘይንእስ ወይቤልዎ ውእቱ። ወይቤ እግዚአብሔር ይሣሀልከ ወልድየ <sup>42:22</sup>&nbsp;ወፈነዎ ውስተ ቤቱ ወስምዖንሃኒ አውጽአ ሎሙ። ወገብረ ሎሙ ምሳሐ ወአቅረቡ ሎቱ አመኃሁ ዘአምጽኡ በእደዊሆሙ። <sup>42:23</sup>&nbsp;ወበልዑ በቅድሜሁ ወወሀቦሙ ክፍለ ለኵሎሙ ወበዝኀ መክፈልተ ብንያም እመክፈልተ ኵሎሙ ትስብዕተ። <sup>42:24</sup>&nbsp;ወበልዑ ወሰትዩ ወተንሥኡ ወኀደሩ ኀበ አእዱጊሆሙ። <sup>42:25</sup>&nbsp;ወኀለየ ዮሴፍ ኅሊና በዘ ያአምር ኅሊናሆሙ እመቦ ኅሊና ሰላም በበይናቲሆሙ። ወይቤሎ ለብእሲ ዘላዕለ ቤቱ ምላእ ሎሙ ኵሎ አሕስሊሆሙ እክለ ወወርቆሙኒ አግብእ ሎሙ ማእከለ መዋዲቶሙ ወኮራ በዘ እሰቲ ደይ ውስተ ዘይንእስ ብሩር ወፈንዎሙ።
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>42:21</sup>&nbsp;They arrived and stood in front of Joseph. When he saw his brother Benjamin, he recognized him and said to them: 'Is this your youngest brother'? They said to him: 'He is'. He said: 'May the Lord be gracious to you, my son'. <sup>42:22</sup>&nbsp;He sent him into his house and brought Simeon out to them. He prepared a dinner for them. They presented him with his gifts which they had brought in their hands. <sup>42:23</sup>&nbsp;They ate in front of him. He gave portions to all of them, but Benjamin's share was seven times larger than the share of any of them. <sup>42:24</sup>&nbsp;They ate and drank. Then they got up and stayed with their donkeys. <sup>42:25</sup>&nbsp;Joseph conceived of a plan by which he would know their thoughts — whether there were peaceful thoughts between them. He said to the man who was in charge of his house: 'Fill all their sacks with food for them and return their money to them in their containers; put the cup with which I drink in the sack of the youngest — the silver cup — and send them away'.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>43:1</sup>&nbsp;ወገብረ በከመ ይቤሎ ዮሴፍ ወመልአ ሎሙ አሕስሊሆሙ ኵሎ ሲሲተ ወወርቆሙኒ ወደየ ውስተ አሕስሊሆሙ ወኮራ ወደየ ውስተ ሐስለ ብንያም። <sup>43:2</sup>&nbsp;ወነግሀ በጽባሕ ሖሩ ወኮነ ሶበ ወፅኡ እምህየ ይቤሎ ዮሴፍ ለብእሴ ቤቱ ዴግኖሙ ሩጽ ወተጋአዞሙ እንዘ ትብል ህየንተ ሠናይት ዐሰይክሙኒ እኩየ ሰረቅሙኒ ጽዋዐ ብሩር በዘይሰቲ እግዚእየ ወአግብኦ ሊተ ለእኁሆሙ ዘይንእስ ወፍጡነ አምጽኦ ዘእንበለ እፃእ ውስተ ምኵናንየ <sup>43:3</sup>&nbsp;ወሮጸ ድኅሬሆሙ። ወይቤሎሙ በከመ ዝንቱ ነገር <sup>43:4</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤልዎ ሐሰ ሎሙ ለአግብርቲከ ኢይገብሩ ዘንተሰ ነገረ ወኢይሰርቁ እምቤተ እግዚእከ ምንተኒ ንዋየ። ወወርቀኒ ዘረከብነ ቀዲሙ ውስተ አሕስሊነ አሶጥነ ደቅከ እምድረ ከናአን <sup>43:5</sup>&nbsp;እፎ እንከ ንሰርቅ ምንተኒ ንዋየ። ናሁ ንሕነሂ ወአሕስሊነሂ ፍትን ወበኀበ ረከብከ ጽዋዐ ውስተ ሐስለ አሐዱ ብእሲ እምኔነ ይትቀተል ወንሕነሂ ወአእዱጊነሂ ንትቀነይ ለእግዚእከ <sup>43:6</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤሎሙ አኮ ከማሁ በኀበ ብእሲ ዘረከብክዎ ባሕቲቶ እነሥእ ገብረ ወአንትሙሰ ተአትዉ በሰላም ቤተክሙ <sup>43:7</sup>&nbsp;ወእንዘ ይፈትን ውስተ ንዋዮሙ እምዘ ይልህቅ ቀደመ ወፈጸመ በኀበ ዘይንእስ ወተረክበ ውስተ ሐስለ ብንያም <sup>43:8</sup>&nbsp;ወሠጠጡ አልባሲሆሙ ወጸዐኑ ዲበ አእዱጊሆሙ ወተመይጡ ሀገረ ወበጽሑ ቤቶ ለዮሴፍ ወሰገዱ ሎቱ ኵሎሙ በገጾሙ ውስተ ምድር። <sup>43:9</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤሎሙ ዮሴፍ እኩየ ገበርክሙ ወይቤሉ ምንተ ንበል ወምንተ ንትዋቀሥ እግዚእነ ረከበ አበሳሆሙ ለአግብርቲሁ ነየነ ንሕነ አግብርቱ ለእግዚእነ ወአእዱጊነሂ። <sup>43:10</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤሎሙ ዮሴፍ እግዚአብሔር አንሰ እፈርህ አንትሙሰ ሖሩ አብያቲክሙ ወእኁክሙ ከመ ይኩን ቅኑየ እስመ እኩየ ገበርክሙ ኢታአምሩኑ ከመ ያስተአድም ብእሲ ጽዋዖ በከመ አነ በዝ ጽዋዕ ወኪያሁ ሰረቅሙኒ። <sup>43:11</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤ ይሁዳ ላዕሌየ እግዚኦ እትናገር ገብርከ ቃለ ውስተ እዝነ እግዚእየ። ክልኤተ አኀወ ወለደት እሙ ለገብርከ ለአቡነ ለነ አሐዱ ወፅአ ወተገድፈ ወአልቦ ዘረከቦ ወውእቱ ባሕቲቱ ተረፈ ለእሙ። ወገብርከኒ አቡነ ያፈቅሮ ወነፍሱኒ እስርት እምነፍዝ <sup>43:12</sup>&nbsp;ወይከውን እምከመ ሖርነ ኀበ ገብርከ አቡነ ወእምከመ ኢሀሎ ምስሌነ ወሬዛ ይመውት ወንቀጽዕ አባነ በሐዘን እስከ ለመዊት <sup>43:13</sup>&nbsp;ወእገብር አነ ባሕቱ ገብርከ ህየንቴሁ ለሕፃን ገብረ ለእግዚእየ። ወይሖር ወሬዛ ምስለ አኀዊሁ እስመ ተሐበይክዎ እምእዴሁ ለገብርከ አቡነ ለነ ወለእመ ኢያግባእክዎ ይኤብስ ገበርከ ለአቡነ ኵሎን መዋዕለ <sup>43:14</sup>&nbsp;ወርእየ ዮሴፍ ከመ ልበ ኵሎሙ ዕሩይ ብእሲ ምስለ ካልኡ ለሠናይ ወስእነ ተዐግሦ ወነገሮሙ ከመ ውእቱ ዮሴፍ <sup>43:15</sup>&nbsp;ወተናገረ ምስሌሆሙ በከመ ልሳነ ዕብራይስጥ። ወሐቀፈ ክሳውዲሆሙ ወበከየ ወእሙንቱሰ ኢያእመርዎ ወአኀዙ ይብክዩ። <sup>43:16</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤሎሙ ኢትብክዩ ላዕሌየ አፍጥኑ ወአምጽእዎ ለአቡየ ኀቤየ ወእርአዮ ዘእንበለ እሙት ወአዕይንቲሁኒ ለእኁየ ብንያም እንዘ ይሬእያ። <sup>43:17</sup>&nbsp;እስመ ናሁ ዝንቱ ካልእ ዓም ዘዐባር ወዓዲ ኀምስቱ ዓመት ሀሎ ወአልቦ ማእረረ ወአልቦ ፍሬ ዕፅ ወአልቦ ሐሪሰ <sup>43:18</sup>&nbsp;ፍጡነ ረዱ አንትሙ ወአብያቲክሙ ወኢትትሐጐሉ በዐባር ወኢትተክዙ በእንተ ጥሪትክሙ እስመ ለሠሪዕ አቅደመ ፈንዎትየ እግዚአብሔር ቅድሜክሙ ከመ ይሕየዉ ሕዝብ ብዙኃን። <sup>43:19</sup>&nbsp;ወዜንውዎ ለአቡየ ከመ ዓዲ ሕያው አነ ወአንትሙኒ ናሁ ትሬእዩ ከመ ሠርዐኒ እግዚአብሔር ከመ እንተ አቡሁ ለፈርዖን ወከመ እመብል ውስተ ቤቱ ወዲበ ኵሉ ምድረ ግብጽ <sup>43:20</sup>&nbsp;ወዜንውዎ ለአቡየ ኵሎ ክብርየ ወኵሎ ዘመጠነ ወሀበኒ እግዚአብሔር ብዕለ ወክብረ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>43:1</sup>&nbsp;He did as Joseph told him. He filled all their sacks with food for them and placed their money in their sacks. He put the cup in Benjamin's sack. <sup>43:2</sup>&nbsp;Early in the morning they went (off). But when they had left that place, Joseph said to the man of his house: 'Pursue them. Run and reprimand them as follows: «You have repaid me with evil instead of good. You have stolen from me the silver cup with which my master drinks». Bring their youngest brother back to me and bring him quickly, before I go out to the place where I rule'. <sup>43:3</sup>&nbsp;He ran after them and spoke to them in line with this message. <sup>43:4</sup>&nbsp;They said to him: 'Heaven forbid that your servants should do such a thing and should steal any container from the house of your master. Your servants have brought back from the land of Canaan the money that we found in our sacks the first time. <sup>43:5</sup>&nbsp;How, then, should we steal any container? Here we and our sacks are. Make a search, and anyone of us in whose sack you find the cup is to be killed, while we and our donkeys are to serve your master'. <sup>43:6</sup>&nbsp;He said to them: '(That) is not the way it will be. I will take only the man with whom I find it as a servant, and you may go safely to your home'. <sup>43:7</sup>&nbsp;As he was searching among their containers, he began with the oldest and ended with the youngest. It was found in Benjamin's sack. <sup>43:8</sup>&nbsp;They tore their clothing, loaded their donkeys, and returned to the city. When they arrived at Joseph's house, all of them bowed to him with their faces to the ground. <sup>43:9</sup>&nbsp;Joseph said to them: 'You have done an evil thing'. They said: 'What are we to say and what shall we say in our defense. Our master has discovered the crime of his servants. We ourselves and our donkeys, too, are our master's servants'. <sup>43:10</sup>&nbsp;Joseph said to them: 'As for me, I fear the Lord. As for you, go to your houses, but your brother is to be enslaved because you have done something evil. Do you not know that a man takes pleasure in his cup as I do in this cup? And you stole it from me'. <sup>43:11</sup>&nbsp;Then Judah said: 'Please, master, allow me, your servant, to say something in my master's hearing. His mother gave birth to two brothers for your servant our father. One has gone away and been lost; no one has found him. He alone is left of his mother('s children). And your servant our father loves him and his life is tied together with the life of this one. <sup>43:12</sup>&nbsp;If we go to your servant our father and if the young man is not with us, then he would die and we would bring our father down in sorrow to death. <sup>43:13</sup>&nbsp;Rather, I your servant will remain in place of the child as a servant of my master. Let the young man go with his brothers because I took responsibility for him from your servant our father. If I do not bring him back, your servant will be guilty to our father forever. <sup>43:14</sup>&nbsp;When Joseph saw that the minds of all of them were in harmony one with the other for good (ends), he was unable to control himself, and he told them that he was Joseph. <sup>43:15</sup>&nbsp;He spoke with them in the Hebrew language. He wrapped his arms around their necks and cried. But they did not recognize him and began to cry. <sup>43:16</sup>&nbsp;Then he said to them: 'Do not cry about me. Quickly bring my father to me and let me see him before I die, while my brother Benjamin also looks on. <sup>43:17</sup>&nbsp;For this is now the second year of the famine and there are still five more years without harvest, without fruit (growing on) trees, and without plowing. <sup>43:18</sup>&nbsp;You and your households come down quickly so that you may not die in the famine. Do not worry about your property because the Lord sent me first before you to arrange matters so that many people may remain alive. <sup>43:19</sup>&nbsp;Tell my father that I am still alive. You now see that the Lord has made me like a father to the pharaoh and to rule in his household and over the entire land of Egypt. <sup>43:20</sup>&nbsp;Tell my father about all my splendor and all the wealth and splendor which the Lord has given me'.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>43:21</sup>&nbsp;ወወሀቦሙ በቃለ አፈ ፈርዖን ሰረገላተ ወሥንቀ ለፍኖት ወወሀቦሙ ለኵሎሙ አልባሰ ሕብር ወብሩረ። <sup>43:22</sup>&nbsp;ወለአቡሆሙኒ ፈነወ አልባሰ ወብሩረ ወዐሠርተ አእዱገ ዘይወስዱ ስርናየ ወፈነዎሙ <sup>43:23</sup>&nbsp;ወዐርጉ ወዜነዉ ለአቡሆሙ። ከመ ዮሴፍ ሕያው ወከመ ውእቱ ያሰፍር ስርናየ ለኵሉ አሕዛበ ምድር ወይሜብል ዲበ ኵሉ ምድረ ግብጽ። <sup>43:24</sup>&nbsp;ወኢአምነ አቡሆሙ እስመ ደንገፀ በኅሊናሁ። ወእምዝ ርእየ ሰረገላተ ዘፈነወ ዮሴፍ ወተሐደሰት ወሐይወት መንፈሱ ወይቤ ዐቢይ ውእቱ ሊተ እስመ ዮሴፍ ሕያው እረድ ወእርአዮ ዘእንበለ እሙት።
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>43:21</sup>&nbsp;By personal command of the pharaoh he gave them wagons and provisions for the trip, and he gave all of them colored clothing and silver. <sup>43:22</sup>&nbsp;To their father he sent clothing, silver, and ten donkeys which were carrying grain. Then he sent them away. <sup>43:23</sup>&nbsp;They went up and told their father that Joseph was alive and that he was having grain distributed to all the peoples of the earth and ruling over the entire land of Egypt. <sup>43:24</sup>&nbsp;Their father did not believe (it) because he was disturbed in his thoughts. But after he saw the wagons which Joseph had sent, his spirit revived and he said: 'It is enough for me that Joseph is alive. Let me go down and see him before I die'.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>44:1</sup>&nbsp;ወተንሥአ እስራኤል እምካራን እምቤቱ በሠርቀ ሣልስ ወርኅ ወሖረ እንተ ፍኖተ ዐዘቅተ መሐላ ወሦዐ መሥዋዕተ ለአምላከ አቡሁ ይስሐቅ አመ ሰቡዑ ለዝ ወርኅ። <sup>44:2</sup>&nbsp;ወተዘከረ ያዕቆብ ሕልመ ዘርእየ በቤቴል ወፈርሀ ወሪደ ውስተ ግብጽ <sup>44:3</sup>&nbsp;ወእንዘ ይኄሊ ይልአክ ለዮሴፍ ከመ ይምጻእ ኀቤሁ ወኢይረድ ውእቱ። ወነበረ ህየ ሰቡዐ ዕለተ እመቦ ከመ ይርአይ ራእየ እመ ይነብር ወለእመ ይወርድ። <sup>44:4</sup>&nbsp;ወገብረ በዓለ ማእረር ቀዳሜ ፍሬ ስርናይ እምስርናይ ብሉይ እስመ አልቦ ውስተ ኵሉ ምድረ ከናአን ምልአ እድ ምንተሂ ዘርአ ውስተ ምድር እስመ ዐባር ውእቱ ኮነ ለኵሉ አራዊት ወለእንስሳ ወለአዕዋፍ ወለሰብእኒ 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>44:1</sup>&nbsp;Israel set out from Hebron, from his house, on the first of the third month. He went by way of the well of the oath and offered a sacrifice to the God of his father Isaac on the seventh of this month. <sup>44:2</sup>&nbsp;When Jacob remembered the dream that he had seen in Bethel, he was afraid to go down to Egypt. <sup>44:3</sup>&nbsp;But as he was thinking about sending word to Joseph that he should come to him and that he would not go down, he remained there for seven days on the chance that he would see a vision (about) whether he should remain or go down. <sup>44:4</sup>&nbsp;He celebrated the harvest festival — the firstfruits of grain — with old grain because in all the land of Canaan there was not even a handful of seed in the land since the famine affected all the animals, the cattle, the birds, and mankind as well.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>44:5</sup>&nbsp;ወአመ ዐሡሩ ወሰዱሱ አስተርአዮ እግዚአብሔር ወይቤሎ ያዕቆብ ያዕቆብ ወይቤ ነየ አነ። ወይቤሎ አነኬ አምላከ አበዊከ አምላከ አብርሃም ወይስሐቅ ኢትፍራህ ወሪደ ግብጽ እስመ ውስተ ዐቢይ ሕዝብ እሠርዐከ በህየ። <sup>44:6</sup>&nbsp;አነ እወርድ ምስሌከ ወአነ እወስደከ ወበዛቲ ምድር ትትቀበር ወዮሴፍ ያነብር እዴሁ ዲበ አዕይንቲከ ኢትፍራህ ረድ ውስተ ግብጽ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>44:5</sup>&nbsp;On the sixteenth the Lord appeared to him and said to him: 'Jacob, Jacob'. He said: 'Yes'? He said to him: 'I am the God of your fathers — the God of Abraham and Isaac. Do not be afraid to go down to Egypt because I will make you into a great nation there. <sup>44:6</sup>&nbsp;I will go down with you and I will lead you (back). You will be buried in this land, and Joseph will place his hands on your eyes. Do not be afraid; go down to Egypt'.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>44:7</sup>&nbsp;ወተንሥኡ ውሉዱ ወውሉደ ውሉዱ ወአጽዐኑ አባሆሙ ወንዋዮሙ ዲበ ሰረገላት <sup>44:8</sup>&nbsp;ወተንሥአ እስራኤል እምዐዘቅተ መሐላ አመ ዐሡር ወሰዱስ ዕለት ዘዝ ወርኅ ሣልስ ወሖረ ብሔረ ግብጽ። <sup>44:9</sup>&nbsp;ወፈነወ እስራኤል ቅድሜሁ ኀበ ዮሴፍ ወልዶ ይሁዳሃ ከመ ያስተሐይጽ ምድረ ጌሤም እስመ ህየ ይቤሎሙ ዮሴፍ ለአኀዊሁ ይምጽኡ ከመ ይኅድሩ ህየ ከመ ይኩኑ ቅሩባነ ዚአሁ። <sup>44:10</sup>&nbsp;ወይእቲኒ ሠናይት በምድረ ግብጽ ወቅርብት ኀቤሁ ለኵሉ ወለእለሂ እንስሳ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>44:7</sup>&nbsp;His sons and grandsons set about loading their father and their property on the wagons. <sup>44:8</sup>&nbsp;Israel set out from the well of the oath on the sixteenth day of this third month and went to the territory of Egypt. <sup>44:9</sup>&nbsp;Israel sent his son Judah in front of him to Joseph to check the land of Goshen because Joseph had told his brothers to come there in order to live there so that they would be his neighbors. <sup>44:10</sup>&nbsp;It was the best (place) in the land of Egypt and (it was) near him for each one and also all the cattle.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>44:11</sup>&nbsp;ወዝ አስማቲሆሙ ለውሉደ ያዕቆብ እለ ሖሩ ውስተ ግብጽ ምስለ ያዕቆብ አቡሆሙ <sup>44:12</sup>&nbsp;ሮቤል በኵሩ ለእስራኤል ወዝ አስማቲሆሙ ለውሉዱ ኤኖክ ወፋሉስ ወኤስሮም ወከራሚ ኀምስቱ። <sup>44:13</sup>&nbsp;ስምዖን ወውሉዱ ወዝ አስማቲሆሙ ለውሉዱ ኢያሙኤል ወኢያሚን ወአዎት ወኢያኪም ወሳአር ወሳውል ወልዳ ለፍኒሰወት ሰብዓቱ። <sup>44:14</sup>&nbsp;ሌዊ ወውሉዱ ወዝ አስማቲሆሙ ለውሉዱ ጌድሶን ወቃዓድ ወሚራሪ አርባዕቱ። <sup>44:15</sup>&nbsp;ይሁዳ ወውሉዱ ወዝ አስማቲሆሙ ለውሉዱ ሴሎም ወፋሬስ ወዛራ አርባዕቱ። <sup>44:16</sup>&nbsp;ይሳኮር ወውሉዱ ወዝ አስማቲሆሙ ለውሉዱ ቶላ ወፉአ ወኢያሱብ ወሳምሮም ኀምስቱ። <sup>44:17</sup>&nbsp;ዛብሎን ወውሉዱ ወዝ አስማቲሆሙ ለውሉዱ ሳአር ወኤሎን ወኢያሊኤል አርባዕቱ። <sup>44:18</sup>&nbsp;ወእሉ ውሉደ ያዕቆብ ወውሉዶሙ እለ ወለደት ልያ ለያዕቆብ በመስጴጦምያ ስድስቱ ወአሐቲ ዲና እኅቶሙ። ወኵሉ ነፍስ ዘውሉደ ልያ ወውሉዶሙ እለ ቦኡ ምስለ ያዕቆብ አቡሆሙ ውስተ ግብጽ ዕሥራ ወተስዐቱ ወያዕቆብ አቡሆሙ ምስሌሆሙ። ወኮኑ ሠላሳ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>44:11</sup>&nbsp;These are the names of Jacob's children who went to Egypt with their father Jacob. <sup>44:12</sup>&nbsp;Reuben, Israel's first-born, and these are the names of his sons: Enoch, Pallu, Hezron, and Carmi — five; <sup>44:13</sup>&nbsp;Simeon and his sons, and these are the names of his sons: Jemuel, Jamin, Ohad, Jachin, Zohar, and Shaul, the son of the Phoenician woman — seven; <sup>44:14</sup>&nbsp;Levi and his sons, and these are the names of his sons: Gershon, Kohath, and Merari — four; <sup>44:15</sup>&nbsp;Judah and his sons, and these are the names of his sons: Shelah, Perez, and Zerah — four; <sup>44:16</sup>&nbsp;Issachar and his sons, and these are the names of his sons: Tola, Puvah, lob, and Shimron — five; <sup>44:17</sup>&nbsp;Zebulun and his sons, and these are the names of his sons: Sered, Elon, and Jahleel — four; <sup>44:18</sup>&nbsp;These are Jacob's sons and their sons to whom Leah gave birth for Jacob in Mesopotamia — six and their one sister Dinah. All of the persons of Leah's sons and their sons who went with their father Jacob to Egypt were 29. And, as their father Jacob was with them, they were 30.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>44:19</sup>&nbsp;ወውሉደ ዘለፋ ለአኪታ ለልያ ብእሲተ ያዕቆብ ዘወለደት ለያዕቆብ ጋድሃ ወአሴርሃ። <sup>44:20</sup>&nbsp;ወዝ አስማተ ውሉዶሙ እለ ቦኡ ምስሌሁ ውስተ ግብጽ ውሉደ ጋድ ሴፍዮን ወአጋቲ ወሱኒ ወአሲቦን [ወዔዲስ] ወአሪሊ ወአሩዲ ሰማኒቱ። <sup>44:21</sup>&nbsp;ወውሉደ አሴር ኢዮምና ወይሱአ [ወይኡኤል] ወቤርያ ወሳራ እኅቶሙ አሐቲ ኀምስቱ። <sup>44:22</sup>&nbsp;ኵሉ ነፍስ ዐሠርቱ ወአርባዕቱ ወኮነ ኵሉ ዘልያ አርባዓ ወአርባዕቱ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>44:19</sup>&nbsp;The sons of Zilpah, the maid of Jacob's wife Leah, to whom she gave birth for Jacob were Gad and Asher. <sup>44:20</sup>&nbsp;These are the names of their sons who went with him into Egypt. Gad's sons: Ziphion, Haggi, Shuni, Ezbon, [Eri], Areli, and Arodi — eight. <sup>44:21</sup>&nbsp;The children of Asher: Imnah, Ishvah, [Ishvi], Beriah, and their one sister Serah — six. <sup>44:22</sup>&nbsp;All the persons were 14, and all those of Leah were 44.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>44:23</sup>&nbsp;ወውሉደ ራሔል ዘብእሲተ ያዕቆብ ዮሴፍ ወብንያም። <sup>44:24</sup>&nbsp;ወተወልዱ ለዮሴፍ በግብጽ ዘእንበለ ይባእ አቡሁ ውስተ ግብጽ ዘወለደት ሎቱ አስኔት ወለተ ፉጢራዕ ሣውዕ ዘኢሊዮጳሊስ ምነሴሃ ወኤፍሬምሃ። ሠለስቱ። <sup>44:25</sup>&nbsp;ወውሉደ ብንያም ባላ ወባኮር ወአስቢል ጉአድ ወንኤማን ወአብዮድ ወራኤ ወሰናኒም ወአፊም ወጋአም ዐሠርቱ ወአሐዱ። <sup>44:26</sup>&nbsp;ወኮነ ኵሉ ነፍስ ዘራሔል ዐሠርቱ ወአርባዕቱ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>44:23</sup>&nbsp;The sons of Rachel who was Jacob's wife were Joseph and Benjamin. <sup>44:24</sup>&nbsp;Before his father came to Egypt children, to whom Asenath — the daughter of Potiphar, the priest of Heliopohs — gave birth for him, were born to Joseph in Egypt: Manasseh and Ephraim — three. <sup>44:25</sup>&nbsp;The sons of Benjamin were: Bela, Becher, Ashbel, Gera, Naaman, Ehi, Rosh, Muppim, Huppim, and Ard — eleven. <sup>44:26</sup>&nbsp;All the persons of Rachel were 14.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>44:27</sup>&nbsp;ወውሉደ ባላ ለአኪታ ለራሔል ብእሲቱ ለያዕቆብ ዘወለደት ለያዕቆብ ዳንሃ ወንፍታሌም። <sup>44:28</sup>&nbsp;ወዝ አስማተ ውሉዶሙ እለ ቦኡ ምስሌሆሙ ውስተ ግብጽ ውሉደ ዳን ኩሲም ወሳሞን ወአሱዲ ወኢያከ ወሰሎሞን ስድስቱ <sup>44:29</sup>&nbsp;ወሞቱ በግብጽ በዓመተ ቦኡ ወተረፎ ለዳን ኩሲም ባሕቲቱ። <sup>44:30</sup>&nbsp;ወዝ አስማቲሆሙ ለውሉደ ንፍታሌም ኢያሲኤል ወጋሂኒ ወአሰአር ወሰሉም ወኤው <sup>44:31</sup>&nbsp;ወሞተ ኤው በግብጽ ዘተወልደ እምድኅረ ዓመተ ዐባር <sup>44:32</sup>&nbsp;ወኮኑ ኵሎሙ ዘራሔል ዕሥራ ወስድስቱ 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>44:27</sup>&nbsp;The sons of Bilhah, the maid of Jacob's wife Rachel, to whom she gave birth for Jacob were Dan and Naphtali. <sup>44:28</sup>&nbsp;These are the names of their sons who went with them to Egypt. The sons of Dan were: Hushim, Samon, Asudi, Iyaka, and Salomon — six. <sup>44:29</sup>&nbsp;They died in Egypt during the year in which they came (there). Only Hushim was left to Dan. <sup>44:30</sup>&nbsp;These are the names of Naphtali's sons: Jahzeel, Guni, Jezer, Shillem, and Ev. <sup>44:31</sup>&nbsp;Ev, who was born after the years of the famine, died in Egypt. <sup>44:32</sup>&nbsp;All those of Rachel were 26.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>44:33</sup>&nbsp;ወኵሉ መንፈስ ዘያዕቆብ ዘቦአ ውስተ ግብጽ ሰብዓ መንፈስ። እሉ እንከ ውሉዱ ወውሉደ ውሉዱ ኵሎሙ ሰብዓ ወኀምስቱ እለ ሞቱ በግብጽ ዘእንበለ ያውስቡ ወውሉድኒ አልቦሙ። <sup>44:34</sup>&nbsp;ወበምድረ ከናአን ሞትዎ ለይሁዳ ክልኤቱ ደቁ ኤር ወኣውናን ወአልቦሙ ውሉደ ወቀበርዎሙ ደቂቀ እስራኤል ለእለ ተሐጕሉ ወተሠይሙ ውስተ ሰብዓ ሕዝብ።
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>44:33</sup>&nbsp;All the persons of Jacob who entered Egypt were 70 persons. So all of these sons and grandsons of his were 70, and five who died in Egypt before they married. They had no children. <sup>44:34</sup>&nbsp;Judah's two sons Er and Onan had died in the land of Canaan. They had no children. The sons of Israel buried those who died, and they were placed among the 70 nations.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>45:1</sup>&nbsp;ወቦአ እስራኤል ውስተ ብሔረ ግብጽ ውስተ ምድረ ጌሤም አመ ሠርቀ ወርኅ ራብዕ በካልእ ዓመት ዘሱባዔ ሣልስ ዘአርብዓ ወኀምስቱ ኢዮቤልው። <sup>45:2</sup>&nbsp;ወመጽአ ዮሴፍ ይትቀበል አባሁ ያዕቆብሃ ውስተ ምድረ ጌሤም ወሐቀፈ ክሳደ አቡሁ ወበከየ። <sup>45:3</sup>&nbsp;ወይቤሎ እስራኤል ለዮሴፍ እሙት ይእዜሰ እምዘ ርኢኩከ ወይእዜኒ ይትባረክ እግዚአብሔር አምላከ እስራኤል ወአምላከ አብርሃም ወአምላከ ይስሐቅ ዘኢከልአ ምሕረቶ ወሣህሎ እምገብሩ ያዕቆብ። <sup>45:4</sup>&nbsp;ዐቢይ ሊተ ዘርኢኩ ገጸከ እንዘ ሕያው አነ እስመ አማን ህልው ራእይ ዘርኢኩ በቤቴል ይትባረክ እግዚአብሔር አምላኪየ ለዓለመ ዓለም ወቡሩክ ስሙ። <sup>45:5</sup>&nbsp;ወበልዑ ዮሴፍ ወአኀዊሁ በቅድመ አቡሆሙ ኅብስተ ወሰትዩ ወይነ ወተፈሥሐ ያዕቆብ ፍሥሓ ዐቢየ ጥቀ። እስመ ርእዮ ለዮሴፍ እንዘ ይበልዕ ምስለ አኀዊሁ ወይሰቲ በቅድሜሁ። ወባረኮ ለፈጣሬ ኵሉ ዘዐቀቦ ወዐቀበ ሎቱ ዐሠርተ ወክልኤተ ውሉዶ። <sup>45:6</sup>&nbsp;ወወሀቦ ዮሴፍ ለአቡሁ ወለአኀዊሁ ሀብተ ከመ ይኅድሩ ምድረ ጌሤም ወውስተ ራሜሲኖ ወኵሎ አድያሚሃ ሎሙ ዘይኴንኑ በቅድሜሁ ለፈርዖን። ወኀደረ እስራኤል ወውሉዱ ምድረ ጌሤም ምሥናዪሃ ለምድረ ግብጽ ወእስራኤልሰ ወልደ ምእት ወሠላሳ ዓመት አመ ቦአ ውስተ ግብጽ <sup>45:7</sup>&nbsp;ወሴሰዮሙ ዮሴፍ ለአቡሁ ወለአኀዊሁ ወጥሪቶሙሂ ኀባውዘ በከመ የአክሎሙ ለሰብዐቱ ዓመታተ ዐባር 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>45:1</sup>&nbsp;Israel went into the territory of Egypt, into the land of Goshen, on the first of the fourth month during the second year of the third week of the forty-fifth jubilee [2172]. <sup>45:2</sup>&nbsp;When Joseph came to meet his father Jacob in the land of Goshen, he wrapped his arms around his father's neck and cried. <sup>45:3</sup>&nbsp;Israel said to Joseph: 'Now let me die after I have seen you. Now may the Lord, the God of Israel, the God of Abraham, and the God of Isaac — who has not withheld his kindness and his mercy from his servant Jacob — be blessed. <sup>45:4</sup>&nbsp;It is enough for me that I have seen your face while I am alive, because the vision that I saw in Bethel was certainly true. May the Lord my God be blessed forever and ever and may his name be blessed'. <sup>45:5</sup>&nbsp;Joseph and his brothers ate food and drank wine in front of their father. Jacob was extremely happy because in front of him he saw Joseph eating and drinking with his brothers. He blessed the creator of all who had preserved him and preserved his twelve sons for him. <sup>45:6</sup>&nbsp;As a gift Joseph gave his father and his brothers (the right) to live in the land of Goshen and in Ramses; and (he gave) them all its districts which they would rule in the pharaoh's presence. Israel and his sons lived in the land of Goshen, the best part of the land of Egypt. Israel was 130 years of age when he came into Egypt. <sup>45:7</sup>&nbsp;Joseph provided as much food for his father, his brothers, and also for their livestock as would be sufficient for them for the seven years of famine.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>45:8</sup>&nbsp;ወሐመት ምድረ ግብጽ እምቅድመ ገጸ ዐባር። ወአስተጋብአ ዮሴፍ ኵለንታሃ ምድረ ግብጽ ለፈርዖን በእክል ወሰብአኒ ወእንስሳሆሙኒ ወኵሎ አጥረየ ፈርዖን <sup>45:9</sup>&nbsp;ወተፈጸመ ዓመታተ ዐባር። ወወሀበ ዮሴፍ ለአሕዛብ ዘውስተ ምድር ዘርአ ወሲሲተ ከመ ይዝርኡ በሳምን ዓመት እስመ መልአ ፈለግ ዲበ ኵላ ምድረ ግብጽ <sup>45:10</sup>&nbsp;እስመ በሰብዓቱ ዓመታተ ዐባር። ኢሰቀየ ዘእንበለ ውኁዳት መካን ኀበ ድንጋገ ፈለግ ወይእዜሰ መልአ። ወዘርኡ ግብጽ ምድረ ወፈርየት ብዙኀ ሠናየ በውእቱ ዓመት <sup>45:11</sup>&nbsp;ወውእቱ ዓመት ቀዳሚ ዘሱባዔ ራብዕ ዘአርብዓ ወኀምስቱ ኢዮቤሌው። <sup>45:12</sup>&nbsp;ወነሥአ ዮሴፍ እምእክል ዘዘርኡ ኀምስቶ ለንጉሥ ወራብዕተ እደ ኀደገ ሎሙ ለሲሲት ወለዘርእ ወረሰዮ ዮሴፍ ሥርዐተ ለምድረ ግብጽ እስከ ዛቲ ዕለት። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>45:8</sup>&nbsp;As the land of Egypt suffered from the famine, Joseph gained the whole land of Egypt for the pharaoh in exchange for food. He acquired the people, their cattle, and everything for the pharaoh. <sup>45:9</sup>&nbsp;When the years of the famine were completed, Joseph gave seed and food to the people who were in the land so that they could sow seed in the eighth year because the river had overflowed the entire land of Egypt. <sup>45:10</sup>&nbsp;For during the seven years of the famine it had irrigated only a few places at the river bank, but now it overflowed. The Egyptians seeded the land, and it yielded good produce that year. <sup>45:11</sup>&nbsp;That was the first year of the fourth week of the forty-fifth jubilee [2178]. <sup>45:12</sup>&nbsp;Joseph took the king's fifth of the food which had been sown, and he left four parts for them for food and seed. Joseph made it a law for the land of Egypt until today.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>45:13</sup>&nbsp;ወሐይወ እስራኤል በምድረ ግብጽ ዐሠርተ ወሰብዓተ ዓመተ። ወኮና ኵሎን መዋዕል እለ ሐይወ ሠለስቱ ኢዩቤልውስ ምእት ወአርብዓ ወሰብዓቱ ዓመት ወሞተ በዓመት ራብዕ ዘሱባዔ ኃምስ ዘአርብዓ ወኀምስቱ ኢዩቤልውስ። <sup>45:14</sup>&nbsp;ወባረኮሙ እስራኤል ለውሉዱ ዘእንበለ ይሙት ወነገሮሙ ኵሎ ዘኮነ ይረክቦሙ በምድረ ግብጽ ወበደኃሪ መዋዕል ዘከመ ይመጽእ ላዕሌሆሙ አይድዖሙ ወባረኮሙ። ወወሀቦ ለዮሴፍ ክልኤተ መክፈልተ በዲበ ምድር <sup>45:15</sup>&nbsp;ወኖመ ምስለ አበዊሁ ወተቀብረ ውስተ በአት ዘካዕበት በምድረ ከናአን ቅሩበ አብርሃም አቡሁ ውስተ መቃብር ዘከረየ ለርእሱ ውስተ በአተ ካዕበት በምድረ ኬብሮን። <sup>45:16</sup>&nbsp;ወወሀቦ ኵሎ መጻሕፍቲሁ ወመጻሕፍተ አበዊሁ ለሌዊ ወልዱ ከመ ይዕቀቦን ወከመ የሐድሶን ለውሉዱ እስከ ዛቲ ዕለት። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>45:13</sup>&nbsp;Israel lived for 17 years in the land of Egypt. All of the time that he lived was three jubilees — 147 years. He died during the fourth year of the fifth week of the forty-fifth jubilee [2188]. <sup>45:14</sup>&nbsp;Israel blessed his sons before he died. He told them everything that would happen to them in the land of Egypt; and he informed them (about) what would happen to them at the end of time. He blessed them and gave Joseph two shares in the land. <sup>45:15</sup>&nbsp;He slept with his fathers and was buried near his father Abraham in the double cave in the land of Canaan — in the grave which he had dug for himself in the double cave in the land of Hebron. <sup>45:16</sup>&nbsp;He gave all his books and the books of his fathers to his son Levi so that he could preserve them and renew them for his sons until today.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>46:1</sup>&nbsp;ወኮነ እምድኅረ ሞተ ያዕቆብ በዝኁ ውሉደ እስራኤል በምድረ ግብጽ ወኮኑ ሕዝበ ብዙኀ ወኮኑ ኵሎሙ ዕሩያነ በልቦሙ ከመ ያፍቅር እኅው እኅዋሁ ወከመ ይትራዳእ ብእሲ ምስለ እኁሁ ወበዝኁ ወፈድፋዱ ጥቀ። ወዐሠርተ ሱባዔ ዓመታት ኵሎ መዋዕለ ሕይወቱ ለዮሴፍ። <sup>46:2</sup>&nbsp;ወአልቦ ሰይጣነ ወአልቦ ምንተኒ እኩየ ኵሎ መዋዕለ ሕይወቱ ለዮሴፍ እለ ሐይወ እምድኅረ አቡሁ ያዕቆብ። እስመ ኵሎሙ ግብጽ ያከብርዎሙ ለውሉደ እስራኤል ኵሎ መዋዕለ ሕይወቱ ለዮሴፍ <sup>46:3</sup>&nbsp;ወሞተ ዮሴፍ ወልደ ምእት ወዐሠርቱ ዓመት ወዐሠርተ ወሰብዐተ ዓመተ ነበረ ምድረ ከናአን ወዐሠርተ ዓመተ ነበረ እንዘ ይትቀነይ። ወሠለስተ ዓመተ ውስተ ቤተ ሞቅሕ ወሰማንያ ዓመተ እምታሕተ ንጉሥ እንዘ ይኴንን ኵላ ምድረ ግብጽ <sup>46:4</sup>&nbsp;ወሞተ ወኵሎሙ አኀዊሁ ወኵላ ይእቲ ትውልድ <sup>46:5</sup>&nbsp;ወአዘዞሙ ለውሉደ እስራኤል ዘእንበለ ይሙት ከመ ይሰዱ አዕጽምቲሁ በመዋዕል አመ ይወፅኡ እምድረ ግብጽ። <sup>46:6</sup>&nbsp;ወአምሐሎሙ በእንተ አዕጽምቲሁ እስመ አእመረ ከመ ኢይደግሙ ግብጽ አውፅኦቶ ወቀቢሮቶ በዕለት በምድረ ከናአን። እስመ ማከማሮን ንጉሠ ከናአን እንዘ የኀድር ምድረ አሱር ተቃተለ በቈላ ምስለ ንጉሠ ግብጽ ወቀተሎ በህየ። ወዴገኖሙ ድኅሬሆሙ ለግብጽ እስከ አንቀጸ ኤርሞን <sup>46:7</sup>&nbsp;ወስእነ በዊአ እስመ ነግሠ ካልእ ሐዲስ ንጉሥ ለግብጽ ወኀየለ እምኔሁ ወገብአ ምድረ ከናአን ወተዐጽወ አናቅጸ ግብጽ ወአልቦ ዘይወፅእ ወአልቦ ዘይበውእ ውስተ ግብጽ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>46:1</sup>&nbsp;After the death of Jacob, the children of Israel became numerous in the land of Egypt. They became a populous nation, and all of them were of the same mind so that each one loved the other and each one helped the other. They became numerous and increased very much — even for ten weeks of years [= 70 years] — for all of Joseph's lifetime. <sup>46:2</sup>&nbsp;There was no satan or any evil one throughout all of Joseph's lifetime that he lived after his father Jacob because all the Egyptians were honoring the children of Israel for all of Joseph's lifetime. <sup>46:3</sup>&nbsp;Joseph died when he was 110 years of age. He had lived for 17 years in the land of Canaan; for ten years he remained enslaved; he was in prison for three years; and for 80 years he was ruhng the entire land of Egypt under the pharaoh. <sup>46:4</sup>&nbsp;He died and all his brothers and all of that generation. <sup>46:5</sup>&nbsp;Before he died he ordered the Israelites to take his bones along at the time when they would leave the land of Egypt. <sup>46:6</sup>&nbsp;He made them swear about his bones because he knew that the Egyptians would not again bring him out and bury him on the day in the land of Canaan, since Makamaron, the king of Canaan, — while he was living in the land of Asur — fought in the valley with the king of Egypt and killed him there. He pursued the Egyptians as far as the gates of Ermon. <sup>46:7</sup>&nbsp;He was unable to enter because another new king ruled Egypt. He was stronger than he, so he returned to the land of Canaan and the gates of Egypt were closed with no one leaving or entering Egypt.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>46:8</sup>&nbsp;ወሞተ ዮሴፍ በዘ አርብዓ ወስድስቱ ኢዮቤልዉ በሱባዔ ሳድስ በካልእ ዓመቱ ወቀበርዎ ውስተ ምድረ ግብጽ ወሞቱ ኵሎሙ አኀዊሁ እምድኅሬሁ። <sup>46:9</sup>&nbsp;ወወፅአ ንጉሠ ግብጽ ከመ ይትቃተል ምስለ ንጉሠ ከናአን በዘ አርብዓ ወሰብዐቱ ኢዮቤልዉ በዳግም ሱባዔ በካልእ ዓመቱ። ወአውፅኡ ውሉደ እስራኤል አዕጽምቲሆሙ ለውሉደ ያዕቆብ ኵሎ ዘእንበለ አዕጽምተ ዮሴፍ ወቀበርዎ ውስተ ገዳም ውስተ በአት ዘካዕበት ውስተ ደብር። <sup>46:10</sup>&nbsp;ወገብኡ ብዙኃን ውስተ ግብጽ ወኅዳጣን ተርፉ እምኔሆሙ ውስተ ደብረ ኬብሮን ወተረፈ አብራም አቡከ ምስሌሆሙ። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>46:8</sup>&nbsp;Joseph died in the forty-sixth jubilee, in the sixth week, during its second year [2242]. He was buried in the land of Egypt, and all his brothers died after him. <sup>46:9</sup>&nbsp;Then the king of Egypt went out to fight with the king of Canaan in the forty-seventh jubilee, in the second week, during its second year [2263]. The Israelites brought out all the bones of Jacob's sons except Joseph's bones. They buried them in the field, in the double cave in the mountain. <sup>46:10</sup>&nbsp;Many returned to Egypt but a few of them remained on the mountain of Hebron. Your father Amram remained with them. 
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>46:11</sup>&nbsp;ወሞአ ንጉሠ ከናአን ለንጉሠ ግብጽ ወዐጸወ አናቅጸ ግብጽ <sup>46:12</sup>&nbsp;ወኀለየ ኅሊና እኩየ ላዕለ ውሉደ እስራኤል ከመ ያሕምሞሙ ወይቤሎሙ ለሰብአ ግብጽ <sup>46:13</sup>&nbsp;ናሁ ሕዝበ ውሉደ እስራኤል ልህቁ ወበዝኁ እምኔነ ንዑ ንጠበብ ላዕሌሆሙ ዘእንበለ ይብዝኁ ወናሕምሞሙ በቅኔ ዘእንበለ ይምጽአነ ቀትል ወእሙንቱኒ ዘእንበለ ይፅብኡነ ወእመ አኮሰ እሙንቱኒ ይዴመሩ ምስለ ፀር ወይወፅኡ እምድርነ እስመ ልቦሙ ወገጾሙ ውስተ ምድረ ከናአን <sup>46:14</sup>&nbsp;ወሠርዐ ላዕሌሆሙ ሊቃነ ገባር ከመ ያሕምምዎሙ በቅኔ። ወሐነጹ አህጉረ ጽኑዓተ ለፈርዖን ጲቶሃ ወራምሴሃ ወሐነጹ ኵሎ ጥቅመ ወኵሎ አረፋተ ዘወድቀ በሀገረ ግብጽ <sup>46:15</sup>&nbsp;ወይቀንይዎሙ ግፉዐ ወመጠነ ያሐስሙ ላዕሌሆሙ ከማሁ ይበዝኁ ወከማሁ ይፈደፍዱ <sup>46:16</sup>&nbsp;ወያስተራኵስዎሙ ሰብአ ግብጽ ለውሉደ እስራኤል።
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>46:11</sup>&nbsp;The king of Canaan conquered the king of Egypt and closed the gates of Egypt. <sup>46:12</sup>&nbsp;He conceived an evil plan against the Israelites in order to make them suffer. He said to the Egyptians: <sup>46:13</sup>&nbsp;'The nation of the Israelites has now increased and become more numerous than we are. Come on, let us outwit them before they multiply. Let us make them suffer in slavery before war comes our way and they, too, fight against us. Otherwise they will unite with the enemy and leave our land because their mind(s) and face(s look) toward the land of Canaan'. <sup>46:14</sup>&nbsp;He appointed taskmasters over them to make them suffer in slavery. They built fortified cities for the pharaoh — Pithom and Ramses. They built every wall and all the fortifications which had fallen down in the cities of Egypt. <sup>46:15</sup>&nbsp;They were enslaving them by force, but however much they would make them suffer the more they would multiply and the more they would increase. <sup>46:16</sup>&nbsp;The Egyptians considered the Israelites detestable.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>47:1</sup>&nbsp;ወበሱባዔ ሳብዕ በሳብዕ ዓመት በዘ አርብዓ ወሰብዓቱ ኢዩቤልዉ መጽአ አቡከ እምድረ ከናአን ወተወለድከ በራብዕ ሱባዔ በሳድስ ዓመቱ በዘ አርብዓ ወሰማኒቱ ኢዮቤሌዎን ዘውእቱ መዋዕለ ምንዳቤ ላዕለ ውሉደ እስራኤል። <sup>47:2</sup>&nbsp;ወአዘዘ ንጉሠ ግብጽ ፈርዖን ትእዛዘ ላዕሌሆሙ ከመ ይግድፉ ውሉዶሙ ኵሎ ሮሰ ዘተወልደ ውስተ ፈለግ <sup>47:3</sup>&nbsp;ወነበሩ እንዘ ይገድፉ ሰብዐተ ወርኀ እስከ አመ ዕለተ ተወለድከ። ወኀብአተከ እምከ ሠለስተ አውራኀ ወነገሩ በእንቲሃ። <sup>47:4</sup>&nbsp;ወገብረት ለከ ነፍቀ ወለበጠታ ፒሳ ወአስፋሊጦ ወአንበረቶ ውስተ ሣዕር ኀበ ድንጋገ ፈለግ ወአንበረተከ ውስቴታ ሰቡዐ መዋዕለ። ወእምከ ትመጽእ በሌሊት ወታጠብወከ ወመዓልተ ተዐቅበከ ማርያ እኅትከ እምነ አዕዋፍ <sup>47:5</sup>&nbsp;ወበውእቱ መዋዕል ወፅአት ተርሙት ወለተ ፈርዖን ከመ ትትኀፀብ በውስተ ፈለግ ወሰምዐት ቃለከ እንዘ ትበኪ ወትቤ ለዕብራዊያቲሃ ከመ ያምጽአከ ወአምጽአከ ኀቤሃ <sup>47:6</sup>&nbsp;ወአውፅአተከ እምነፍቅ ወምሕረተከ። <sup>47:7</sup>&nbsp;ወትቤላ እኅርከ እሖርኑ ወእጸውዕ ለኪ አሐተ እምዕብራዊያት እንተ ተሐፅኖ ወታጠብዎ ለኪ ለዝ ሕፃን። [ወትቤላ ሑሪ።] <sup>47:8</sup>&nbsp;ወሖረት ወጸውዐታ ለእምከ ለኢዮክቤት ወወሀበታ ዐስበ ወሐፀነተከ 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>47:1</sup>&nbsp;During the seventh week, in the seventh year, in the forty-seventh jubilee [2303], your father came from the land of Canaan. You were born during the fourth week, in its sixth year, in the forty-eighth jubilee [2330], which was the time of distress for the Israelites. <sup>47:2</sup>&nbsp;The pharaoh, the king of Egypt, had given orders regarding them that they were to throw their sons — every male who was born — into the river. <sup>47:3</sup>&nbsp;They continued throwing (them in) for seven months until the time when you were born. Your mother hid you for three months. Then they told about her. <sup>47:4</sup>&nbsp;She made a box for you, covered it with pitch and asphalt, and put it in the grass at the riverbank. She put you in it for seven days. Your mother would come at night and nurse you, and during the day your sister Miriam would protect you from the birds. <sup>47:5</sup>&nbsp;At that time Tarmuth, the pharaoh's daughter, went out to bathe in the river and heard you crying. She told her slaves to bring you, so they brought you to her. <sup>47:6</sup>&nbsp;She took you out of the box and pitied you. <sup>47:7</sup>&nbsp;Then your sister said to her: 'Should I go and summon for you one of the Hebrew women who will care for and nurse this infant for you'? [She said to her: 'Go'.] <sup>47:8</sup>&nbsp;She went and summoned your mother Jochebed. She gave her wages and she took care of you.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>47:9</sup>&nbsp;ወእምዝ ልሂቀከ ወሰዱከ ቤተ ፈርዖን ወኮንከ ውሉዳ ወመሀረከ ዕብራን አቡከ መጽሐፈ ወእምዘ ፈጸምከ ሠለስተ ሱባዔ አብአከ ውስተ ዐጸደ መንግሥት። <sup>47:10</sup>&nbsp;ወሀለውከ ውስተ ዐጸድ ሠለስተ ሱባዔ ዓመት እስከ መዋዕል አመ ወፃእከ እምዐጸደ መንግሥት። ወርኢኮ ለግብጻዊ እንዘ ይዘብጦ ለካልእከ ዘእምነ ውሉደ እስራኤል ወቀተልኮ ወኀባእኮ ውስተ ኆጻ። <sup>47:11</sup>&nbsp;ወበሳኒታ ዕለት ረከብከ ክልኤተ እንዘ ይትባአሱ እምውሉደ እስራኤል ወትቤሎ ለዘይትዔገል ለምንት ትዘብጥ እኅዋከ <sup>47:12</sup>&nbsp;ወተምዕዐ ወተቈጥዐ ወይቤ መኑ ሤመከ ላዕሌነ መልአከ ወመኰንነ ትቅትለኒኑ ትፈቅድ በከመ ቀተልኮ ለግብጻዊ ወፈራህከ ወጐየይከ እምቅድመ ዝንቱ ነገር።
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>47:9</sup>&nbsp;Afterwards, when you had grown up, you were brought to the pharaoh's daughter and became her child. Your father Amram taught you (the art of) writing. After you had completed three weeks [ = 21 years], he brought you into the royal court. <sup>47:10</sup>&nbsp;You remained in the court for three weeks of years [ = 21 years] until the time when you went from the royal court and saw the Egyptian beating your companion who was one of the Israelites. You killed him and hid him in the sand. <sup>47:11</sup>&nbsp;On the next day you found two of the Israelites fighting. You said to the one who was acting unjustly: 'Why are you beating your brother'? <sup>47:12</sup>&nbsp;He became angry and indignant and said: 'Who appointed you as ruler and judge over us? Do you want to kill me as you killed the Egyptian'? Then you were afraid and ran away because of this matter.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>48:1</sup>&nbsp;ወበሳድስ ዓመት ዘሱባዔ ሣልስ ዘአርብዓ ወተስዐቱ ኢዮቤልዉሳት ሖርከ ወነበርከ ህየ ኀምስተ ሱባዔ ወዓመተ አሐደ ወገባእከ ውስተ ግብጽ በሱባዔ ዳግም በዓመት ካልእ በውእቱ ኀምሳ ኢዮቤልው። <sup>48:2</sup>&nbsp;ወአንተ ተአምር ዘተናገረ ለከ በደብረ ሲና ወምንተ ፈቀደ ይግበር ምስሌከ መኰንነ መስቴማ አመ ትገብእ ግብጽ በፍኖት በአላቴ ምጽላል <sup>48:3</sup>&nbsp;አኮሁ በኵሉ ኀይሉ ፈቀደ ይቅትልከ ወያድኅኖሙ ለግብጻዊያን እምእዴከ እስመ ርእየከ ከመ ተፈነውከ ትግበር ኵነኔ ወበቀለ ላዕለ ግብጻዊያን <sup>48:4</sup>&nbsp;ወባላሕኩከ እምእዴሁ። ወገብርከ ተአምረ ወመንክረ በዘ ተፈኖከ ትግበር በግብጽ ላዕለ ፈርዖን ወላዕለ ኵሉ ቤቱ ወላዕለ አግብርቱ ወላዕለ ሕዝቡ። <sup>48:5</sup>&nbsp;ወገብረ እግዚአብሔር ላዕሌሆሙ በቀለ ዐቢየ በእንተ እስራኤል ወመሐጾሙ ወቀተሎሙ በደም ወበቈርነነዓት ወበትንንያ ወበጽንጽያ ከልብ ወበእኩይ ቍስል ዘውእቱ ይፈልሕ ዕንጰዕንጴ ወእንስሳሆሙ በሞት ወበአእባነ በረድ። በዝንቱ አጥፍአ ኵሎ ዘይሠርጽ ሎሙ ወበአንበጣ እንተ በልዐት ተረፈ ዘተረፎሙ እምበረድ ወበጽልመት በኵሮሙ ዘሰብእ ወዘእንስሳ። ወበኵሉ አማልክቲሆሙ ገብረ እግዚአብሔር በቀለ ወአውዐዮሙ በእሳት <sup>48:6</sup>&nbsp;ወኵሉ ተፈነወ ወእዴከ ከመ ትግበር ዘእንበለ ይትገበር ወሀለውከ ትትናገሮ ለንጉሠ ግብጽ ወበቅድመ ኵሎሙ ላእካኒሁ ወበቅድመ ሕዝቡ <sup>48:7</sup>&nbsp;ወኵሉ ኮነ በቃልከ ዐሥሩ ኵነኔ ዐቢያት ወፀዋጋት መጽአ ውስተ ምድረ ግብድ ከመ ትግበር ቦቱ በቀለ እስራኤል። <sup>48:8</sup>&nbsp;ወኵሎ ገብረ እግዚአብሔር በእንተ እስራኤል። ወበከመ ሥርዐቱ ዘተካየደ ምስለ አብርሃም ከመ ይትበቀል ላዕሌሆሙ በከመ ይቀንይዎሙ በግፍዕ። <sup>48:9</sup>&nbsp;ወመኰንነ መስቴማ ይትቀወመከ ቅድሜከ ወይፈቅድ ያውድቀ ውስተ እደ ፈርዖን ወይረድእ ሥራያቲሆሙ ለግብጽ ወይትቃወሙ ወይገብሩ በቅድሜከ። <sup>48:10</sup>&nbsp;እከየሰኬ ኀደግናሆሙ ይግበሩ ወፈውሰ ኢናበውሖሙ ከመ ይትገበር በእደዊሆሙ። <sup>48:11</sup>&nbsp;መሐጾሙ እግዚአብሔር በቍስል እኩይ ወስእኑ ተቃውሞ እስመ አሕጐልናሆሙ እምገቢረ ምንተሂ አሐደ ትእምርተ። <sup>48:12</sup>&nbsp;ወበኵሉ ተአምር ወመንክር ኢኀፈረ መኰንነ መስቴማ እስከ ሶበ ኀየለ ወጸርኀ ሎሙ ለግብጽ ከመ ይዴግኑ ድኅሬከ በኵሉ ኀይሎሙ ለግብጽ በሰረገላቲሆሙ ወአፍራሲሆሙ ወበኵሉ ብዝኆሙ ለአሕዛበ ግብጽ 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>48:1</sup>&nbsp;During the sixth year of the third week of the forty-ninth jubilee [2372], you went and lived there for five weeks and one year [= 36 years]. Then you returned to Egypt in the second week, during the second year in the fiftieth jubilee [2410]. <sup>48:2</sup>&nbsp;You know who spoke to you at Mt. Sinai and what the prince of Mastema wanted to do to you while you were returning to Egypt — on the way at the shady fir tree. <sup>48:3</sup>&nbsp;Did he not wish with all his strength to kill you and to save the Egyptians from your power because he saw that you were sent to carry out punishment and revenge on the Egyptians? <sup>48:4</sup> I rescued you from his power. You performed the signs and miracles which you were sent to perform in Egypt against the pharaoh, all his house, his servants, and his nation. <sup>48:5</sup>&nbsp;The Lord effected a great revenge against them on account of Israel. He struck them and killed them with blood, frogs, gnats, dog flies, bad sores which break out in blisters; (and he struck) their cattle with death; and with hailstones — with these he annihilated everything that was growing for them; with locusts which ate whatever was left for them from the hail; with darkness; (and with the death of) their first-born of men and cattle. The Lord took revenge on all their gods and burned them up. <sup>48:6</sup>&nbsp;Everything was sent through you, before it was done, so that you should do (it). You were speaking with the king of Egypt and in front of all his servants and his people. <sup>48:7</sup>&nbsp;Everything happened by your word. Ten great and severe punishments came to the land of Egypt so that you could take revenge on it for Israel. <sup>48:8</sup>&nbsp;The Lord did everything for the sake of Israel and in accord with his covenant which he made with Abraham to take revenge on them just as they were enslaving them with force. <sup>48:9</sup>&nbsp;The prince of Mastema would stand up against you and wish to make you fall into the pharaoh's power. He would help the Egyptian magicians and they would oppose (you) and perform in front of you. <sup>48:10</sup>&nbsp;We permitted them to do evil things, but we would not allow healings to be performed by them. <sup>48:11</sup>&nbsp;When the Lord struck them with bad sores, they were unable to oppose (you) because we deprived them of (their ability) to perform a single sign. <sup>48:12</sup>&nbsp;Despite all the signs and miracles, the prince of Mastema was not put to shame until he gained strength and cried out to the Egyptians to pursue you with all the Egyptian army — with their chariots, their horses — and with all the throng of the Egyptian people.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>48:13</sup>&nbsp;ወቆምኩ ማእከሌከ ወማእከሎሙ ለግብጽ ወማእከሎሙ ለእስራኤል ወባላሕናሆሙ ለእስራኤል እምእዴሁ ወእምእደ ሕዝብ። ወአውፅኦሙ እግዚአብሔር እንተ ማእከለ ባሕር ከመ እንተ የብስ <sup>48:14</sup>&nbsp;ወኵሎሙ ሕዝብ ዘአውፅአ ይዴግኑ ድኅሬሆሙ ለእስራኤል ወወረዎሙ እግዚአብሔር አምላክነ ማእከለ ባሕር ውስተ መዓምቅቲሃ ለቀላይ በታሕቴሆሙ ለውሉደ እስራኤል በከመ ወረዉ ውሉዶሙ ሰብአ ግብጽ ውስተ ፈለግ ምእተ እልፈ ተበቀሎሙ። ወዐሠርቱ ምእት ዕደው ኀያላን ወእለሂ ሠለስተ ይዳለጉ ጠፍኡ በእንተ አሐዱ ጠባዊት ዘገደፉ ማእከለ ፈለግ እምውሉደ ሕዝብከ 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>48:13</sup>&nbsp;I stood between you, the Egyptians, and the Israelites. We rescued the Israelites from his power and from the power of the people. The Lord brought them out through the middle of the sea as if on dry ground. <sup>48:14</sup>&nbsp;All of the people whom he brought out to pursue the Israelites the Lord our God threw into the sea — to the depths of the abyss — in place of the Israelites, just as the Egyptians had thrown their sons into the river. He took revenge on 1,000,000 of them. 1000 men (who were) strong and also very brave perished for one infant of your people whom they had thrown into the river.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>48:15</sup>&nbsp;ወአመ ዐሡር ወረቡዕ ዕለት ወአመ ዐሡር ወኀሙስ ወአመ ዐሡር ወሰዱስ ወአመ ዐሡር ወሰቡዕ ወአመ ዐሡር ወሰሙን ሀሎ መኰንነ መስቴማ እሱር ወዕፅው እምድኅሬሆሙ ለውሉደ እስራኤል ከመ ኢያስተዋድዮሙ። <sup>48:16</sup>&nbsp;ወአመ ዕለተ ዐሡር ወተሱዕ ፈታሕናሆሙ ከመ ይርድእዎሙ ለግብጽ ወከመ ይዴግኑ ድኅሬሆሙ ለውሉደ እስራኤል <sup>48:17</sup>&nbsp;ወአጽንዐ አልባሲሆሙ ወአኀየሎሙ ወተኀየሉ እምኀበ እግዚአብሔር አምላክነ ከመ ይምሐጾሙ ለግብጽ ወይወርዎሙ ማእከለ ባሕር። <sup>48:18</sup>&nbsp;ወአመ ዐሡር ወረቡዕ ዕለት አሰርናሁ ከመ ኢያስተዋድዮሙ ለደቂቀ እስራኤል በዕለት አመ ሀለዉ ይስእሉ ንዋየ ወአልባሰ እምኀበ ሰብአ ግብጽ ንዋየ ብሩር ወንዋየ ወርቅ ወንዋየ ብርት ወከመ ይማህርክዎሙ ለግብጽ ህየንተ ተቀንዩ እንተ ቀነይዎሙ በግፍዕ። <sup>48:19</sup>&nbsp;ወኢያውፃእናሆሙ ለውሉደ እስራኤል እምግብጽ ዕራቆሙ።
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>48:15</sup>&nbsp;On the fourteenth day, the fifteenth, the sixteenth, the seventeenth, and the eighteenth the prince of Mastema was bound and locked up behind the Israelites so that he could not accuse them. <sup>48:16</sup>&nbsp;On the nineteenth day we released them so that they could help the Egyptians and pursue the Israelites. <sup>48:17</sup>&nbsp;He stiffened their resolve and made them stubborn. They were made stubborn by the Lord our God so that he could strike the Egyptians and throw them into the sea. <sup>48:18</sup>&nbsp;On the fourteenth day we bound him so that he could not accuse the Israelites on the day when they were requesting utensils and clothing from the Egyptians — utensils of silver, utensils of gold, and utensils of bronze; and so that they could plunder the Egyptians in return for the fact that they were made to work when they enslaved them by force. <sup>48:19</sup>&nbsp;We did not bring the Israelites out of Egypt empty-handed.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>49:1</sup>&nbsp;ተዘከር ትእዛዘ ዘአዘዘከ እግዚአብሔር በእንተ ፋሲካ ከመ ትግበር በጊዜሁ አመ ዐሡር ወረቡዑ ለወርኅ ቀዳማዊ ከመ ትጥብሖ ዘእንበለ ይምሰይ ወከመ ይብልዕዎ በሌሊት አመ ምሴት ዘዐሡር ወኀሙስ እምጊዜ ዕርበተ ፀሐይ <sup>49:2</sup>&nbsp;እስመ በዛቲ ሌሊት ቀዳሜ በዓል ይእቲ ወቀዳሜ ፍሥሐ ይእቲ አንትሙ ትነብሩ ትብልዑ ጳስካ በግብጽ። ወኵሎን ኀይላቲሁ ለመስቴማ ተፈነወ ከመ ይቅትል ኵሎ በኵረ በምድረ ግብጽ እምበኵሩ ለፈርዖን እስከ በኵረ ላእኪት ፄዋዊት እንተ ማሕረፅ ወላዕለ እንስሳኒ <sup>49:3</sup>&nbsp;ወዛቲ ዘወሀበ እግዚአብሔር ሎሙ ውስተ ኵሉ ቤት ዘርእዩ ውስተ አንቀጹ ደመ በግዕ ዘዓመት ኢይባኡ ውስተ ቤቱ ለቀቲል አላ ይትዓደዉ ከመ ይድኀኑ ኵሎሙ እለ ውስተ ቤት እስመ ትእምርተ ደም ውስተ አንቀጹ <sup>49:4</sup>&nbsp;ወገብሩ ኀይላቲሁ ለእግዚአብሔር ኵሎ ዘመጠነ አዘዞሙ እግዚአብሔር ወተዐደዉ እምኵሉ ደቂቀ እስራኤል ወኢቦአ ላዕሌሆሙ መቅሠፍት ለአማስኖ እምኔሆሙ ኵሎ ነፍሰ እምእንስሳ እስከ ሰብእ ወእስከ ከልብ። <sup>49:5</sup>&nbsp;ወኮነ መቅሠፍት በግብጽ ጥቀ ዐቢይ ወአልቦ ቤተ በግብጽ ዘአልቦ በድነ ውስቴታ ወብካየ ወዐውያተ <sup>49:6</sup>&nbsp;ወኵሉ እስራኤል ይነብር እንዘ ይበልዕ ሥጋ ጳስካ ወእንዘ ይሰቲ ወይነ ወይሴብሕ ወይባርክ ወያአኵት እግዚአብሔር አምላከ አበዊሁ ወድልወ ይከውን ለወፂእ እምአርዑተ ግብጽ ወእምቅኔ እኪት 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>49:1</sup>&nbsp;Remember the commandments which the Lord gave you regarding the passover so that you may celebrate it at its time on the fourteenth of the first month, that you may sacrifice it before evening, and so that they may eat it at night on the evening of the fifteenth from the time of sunset. <sup>49:2</sup>&nbsp;For on this night — it was the beginning of the festival and the beginning of joy — you were eating the passover in Egypt when all the forces of Mastema were sent to kill every first-born in the land of Egypt — from the pharaoh's first-born to the first-born of the captive slave-girl at the millstone and to the cattle as well. <sup>49:3</sup>&nbsp;This is that which the Lord gave them: into each house on whose door they saw the blood of a year-old lamb, they were not to enter that house to kill but were to pass over (it) in order to save all who were in the house because the sign of the blood was on its door. <sup>49:4</sup>&nbsp;The Lord's forces did everything that the Lord ordered them. They passed over all the Israelites. The plague did not come on them to destroy any of them — from cattle to mankind to dogs. <sup>49:5</sup>&nbsp;The plague on Egypt was very great. There was no house in Egypt in which there was no corpse, crying, and mourning. <sup>49:6</sup>&nbsp;All Israel was eating the paschal meat, drinking the wine, and glorifying, blessing, and praising the Lord God of their fathers. They were ready to leave the Egyptian yoke and evil slavery.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>49:7</sup>&nbsp;ወአንተኒ ተዘከር ዛተ ዕለተ ኵሎ መዋዕለ ሕይወትከ ወግበራ እምዓም ለዓም ኵሎ መዋዕለ ሕይወትከ ምዕረ ለዓመት በዕለቱ በከመ ኵሉ ሕጉ ወኢታስተኃልፍ ዕለተ እምዕለት ወእምወርኅ ለወርኅ <sup>49:8</sup>&nbsp;እስመ ሥርዐት ዘለዓለም ውእቱ ወቍሩጽ ውስተ ጽላተ ሰማይ ላዕለ ውሉደ እስራኤል ከመ ይግበርዎ በኵሉ ዓመት ወዓመት በዕለቱ ምዕረ በዓመት ውስተ ኵሉ ትውልዶሙ ወአልቦ ወሰነ መዋዕል እስመ ለዓለም ውእቱ ሥሩዕ <sup>49:9</sup>&nbsp;ወብእሲ እንዘ ንጹሕ ውእቱ ወኢመጽአ ይግበሮ በጊዜ ዕለቱ ለአብኦ ቍርባን ዘይሠምር ቅድመ እግዚአብሔር ወለበሊዕ ወለሰቲይ በቅድመ እግዚአብሔር በዕለተ በዓሉ ወይሠረዉ ውእቱ ብእሲ ዘንጹሕ ወቅሩብ እስመ ቍርባነ እግዚአብሔር ኢያብአ በጊዜሁ ወኀጢአተ ይነሥእ ውእቱ ብእሲ ለርእሱ <sup>49:10</sup>&nbsp;ከመ ይኩኑ ውሉደ እስራኤል እለ ይመጽኡ ወይገብሩ ጰስከ በዕለተ ጊዜሁ አመ ዐሡሩ ወረቡዑ ለወርኅ ቀዳማዊ በማእከለ ምስያታት እምሣልስታ ለዕለት እስከ ሣልስታ ለሌሊት እስመ ክልኤ መክፈልታ ለዕለት ተውህበ ለብርሃን ወሣልስታ ለምሴት <sup>49:11</sup>&nbsp;ዝውእቱ ዘአዘዘከ እግዚአብሔር ከመ ትግበሮ በማእከለ ምሴታት። <sup>49:12</sup>&nbsp;ወኢይከውን ጠቢሖቱ በኵሉ ጊዜ ብርሃን ዘእንበለ ጊዜ ወሰነ ምሴት ወይበልዕዎ በጊዜ ምሴት እስከ ሣልስተ ሌሊት ወዘተርፈ እምኵሉ ሥጋሁ እምሣልስተ ሌሊት ወከሐ በእሳት ያውዕይዎ። <sup>49:13</sup>&nbsp;ወኢይከውን ያብስልዎ በማይ ወኢይብልዕዎ ጥራየ አላ ጥቡሰ በእሳት ብሱለ በእሳት በአስተሐምሞ ርእስ ምስለ ንዋየ ውስጡ ወምስለ እገሪሁ። ይጥብስዎ በእሳት ወአልቦ ሰቢረ ዐጽም እምውስቴቱ ምንተኒ እስመ ኢይትቀጠቀጥ እምውሉደ እስራኤል ምንተሂ ዐጽም 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>49:7</sup>&nbsp;Now you remember this day throughout all your lifetime. Celebrate it from year to year throughout all your lifetime, once a year on its day in accord with all of its law. Then you will not change a day from the day or from month to month. <sup>49:8</sup>&nbsp;For it is an eternal statute and it is engraved on the heavenly tablets regarding the Israelites that they are to celebrate it each and every year on its day, once a year, throughout their entire history. There is no temporal limit because it is ordained forever. <sup>49:9</sup>&nbsp;The man who is pure but does not come to celebrate it on its prescribed day — to bring a sacrifice that is pleasing before the Lord and to eat and drink before the Lord on the day of his festival — that man who is pure and nearby is to be uprooted because he did not bring the Lord's sacrifice at its time. That man will bear responsibility for his own sin. <sup>49:10</sup>&nbsp;The Israelites are to come and celebrate the passover on its specific day — on the fourteenth of the first month — between the evenings, from the third part of the day until the third part of the night. For two parts of the day have been given for light and its third part for the evening. <sup>49:11</sup>&nbsp;This is what the Lord commanded you — to celebrate it between the evenings. <sup>49:12</sup>&nbsp;It is not to be sacrificed at any hour of the daylight but in the hour of the boundary of the evening. They will eat it during the evening hour(s) until the third part of the night. Any of its meat that is left over from the third part of the night and beyond is to be burned. <sup>49:13</sup>&nbsp;They are not to boil it in water nor eat it raw but roasted on a fire, cooked with care on a fire — the head with its internal parts and its feet. They are to roast it on a fire. There will be no breaking of any bone in it because no bone of the Israelites will be broken.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>49:14</sup>&nbsp;በእንተዝ አዘዞሙ እግዚአብሔር ለውሉደ እስራኤል ከመ ይግበሩ ጳስካ በዕለተ ጊዜሁ። ወኢይከውን ሰቢረ ዐጽም ምንተሂ እምኔሁ እስመ ዕለተ በዓል ይእቲ ወዕለት እዝዝት ይእቲ ወአልቦ ተዐድዎ እምውስቴቱ ዕለተ እምዕለት ወእምወርኅ ወርኅ እስመ አመ ዕለተ በዓሉ ይትገበር። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>49:14</sup>&nbsp;Therefore the Lord ordered the Israelites to celebrate the passover on its specific day. No bone of it is to be broken because it is a festal day and a day which has been commanded. From it there is to be no passing over a day from the day or a month from the month because it is to be celebrated on its festal day.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>49:15</sup>&nbsp;ወአንተሂ አዝዞሙ ለውሉደ እስራኤል ከመ ይግበሩ ጳስካ በመዋዕሊሆሙ በኵሉ ዓመት ምዕረ ለዓመት በዕለተ ጊዜሁ ወይመጽእ ተዝካር እምቅድመ እግዚአብሔር ዘይሠምር ወኢይመጽኦሙ መቅሠፍት ለቀቲል ወለማኅፀት በውእቱ ዓመት አመ ገብሩ ጳስካ በጊዜሁ በኵሉ በከመ ተአዘዘ። <sup>49:16</sup>&nbsp;ወኢይከውን እንከ ለበሊዖቱ በአፍአ እምቤተ መቅደሱ ለእግዚአብሔር ወበአንጸረ ቤተ መቅደሱ ለእግዚአብሔር ወኵሉ ሕዝበ ማኅበሮሙ ለእስራኤል ይግበርዎ በጊዜሁ። <sup>49:17</sup>&nbsp;ኵሉ ሰብእ ዘመጽአ በዕለቱ ይብልዖ በቤተ መቅደሱ ለአምላክክሙ በቅድመ እግዚአብሔር ዘእምዕሥራ ዓመት ወላዕለ እስመ ከመዝ ተጽሕፈ ወተሠርዐ ከመ ይብልዕዎ በቤተ መቅደሱ ለእግዚአብሔር። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>49:15</sup>&nbsp;Now you order the Israelites to celebrate the passover each year during their times, once a year on its specific day. Then a pleasing memorial will come before the Lord and no plague will come upon them to kill and to strike (them) during that year when they have celebrated the passover at its time in every respect as it was commanded. <sup>49:16</sup>&nbsp;It is no longer to be eaten outside of the Lord's sanctuary but before the Lord's sanctuary. All the people of the Israelite congregation are to celebrate it at its time. <sup>49:17</sup>&nbsp;Every man who has come on its day, who is 20 years of age and above, is to eat it in the sanctuary of your God before the Lord, because this is the way it has been written and ordained — that they are to eat it in the Lord's sanctuary.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>49:18</sup>&nbsp;ወእምከመ ቦኡ ውሉደ እስራኤል ውስተ ምድር እንተ ይእኅዙ ውስተ ምድረ ከናአን ወይተክሉ ደብተራ እግዚአብሔር ማእከለ ምድር ውስተ አሐዱ እምነ ሠራዊቶሙ እስከ አመ ይትሐነጽ መቅደሱ ለእግዚአብሔር በዲበ ምድር። ወይኩኑ እንዘ ይመጽኡ ወይገብሩ ጳስከ በማእከለ ደብተራሁ ለእግዚአብሔር ወይጠብሕዎ በቅድመ እግዚአብሔር እምዓመት በዓመት። <sup>49:19</sup>&nbsp;ወበመዋዕል አመ ተሐንጸ ቤት በስመ እግዚአብሔር በምድረ ርስቶሙ ህየ ይሖሩ ወይጥብሑ ጳስካ ምሴተ እንዘ የዐርብ ፀሐይ በትሥልስታ ለዕለት <sup>49:20</sup>&nbsp;ወያዐርጉ ደሞ ውስተ ምክያዳ ለምሥዋዕ ወሥብሐ ያንብሩ ዲበ እሳት ዘላዕለ ምሥዋዕ ወሥጋሁ ይብልዑ ጥቡሰ በእሳት በውስተ ዐጸደ ቤተ መቅደስ በስመ እግዚአብሔር። <sup>49:21</sup>&nbsp;ወኢይክሉ ገቢረ ጳስካ በአህጉሪሆሙ ወበኵሉ በሓውርት ዘእንበለ በቅድመ ደብተራ እግዚአብሔር ወእመ አኮ በቅድመ ቤት ኀበ ኀደረ ስመ ዚአሁ ወስቴቱ ወኢይስሕቱ ድኅረ እግዚአብሔር። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>49:18</sup>&nbsp;When the Israelites enter the land which they will possess — the land of Canaan — and set up the Lord's tabernacle in the middle of the land in one of their tribal groups (until the time when the Lord's temple will be built in the land), they are to come and celebrate the passover in the Lord's tabernacle and sacrifice it before the Lord from year to year. <sup>49:19</sup>&nbsp;At the time when the house is built in the Lord's name in the land which they will possess, they are to go there and sacrifice the passover in the evening when the sun sets, in the third part of the day. <sup>49:20</sup>&nbsp;They will offer its blood on the base of the altar. They are to place the fat on the fire which is above the altar and are to eat its meat roasted on a fire in the courtyard of the sanctuary in the name of the Lord. <sup>49:21</sup>&nbsp;They will not be able to celebrate the passover in their cities or in any places except before the Lord's tabernacle or otherwise before the house in which his name has resided. Then they will not go astray from the Lord. 
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>49:22</sup>&nbsp;ወአንተኒ ሙሴ አዝዞሙ ለውሉደ እስራኤል ወይዕቀቡ ሥርዐተ ጳስካ በከመ ተአዘዘ ለከ ከመ ትንግሮሙ ዓመቶ ለለ ዓመት ወዕለቶ ለዕለታት ወበዓለ ናእት ከመ ይብልዑ ናእተ ሰቡዐ ዕለተ ከመ ይግበሩ በዓሎ ከመ ያብኡ ቍርባኖ ዕለተ እምዕለት በእላ ሰቡዕ መዋዕለ ፍሥሐ ቅድመ እግዚአብሔር ዲበ ምሥዋዐ አምላክክሙ <sup>49:23</sup>&nbsp;እስመ ዛተ በዓለ በውልዋሌ ገበርክምዋ አመ ትወፅኡ እምግብጽ እስከ አመ ተዐድዉ ባሕረ ውስተ ገዳመ ሱር እስመ በኀበ ድንጋገ ባሕር ሰለጥክምዋ።
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>49:22</sup>&nbsp;Now you, Moses, order the Israelites to keep the statute of the passover as it was commanded to you so that you may tell them its year each year, the time of the days, and the festival of unleavened bread so that they may eat unleavened bread for seven days to celebrate its festival, to bring its sacrifice before the Lord on the altar of your God each day during those seven joyful days. <sup>49:23</sup>&nbsp;For you celebrated this festival hastily when you were leaving Egypt until the time you crossed the sea into the wilderness of Sur, because you completed it on the seashore.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>50:1</sup>&nbsp;ወእምድኅረዝ ሕግ አይዳዕኩከ መዋዕለ ሰንበታት በገዳመ ሲና እንተ ይእቲ ማእከለ ኤሊም ወሲና <sup>50:2</sup>&nbsp;ወሰንበታተ ምድርኒ ነገርኩከ በደብረ ሲና ወዓመታተ ኢዮቤሌዎኒ ውስተ ሰንበታተ ዓመታት ወዓመቶሰ ኢነገርናከ እስከ አመ ትበውኡ ውስተ ምድር እንተ ትእኅዙ <sup>50:3</sup>&nbsp;ወታሰነብት ምድርኒ ሰንበታቲሃ በነቢሮቶሙ ዲቤሃ ወዓመቶ ለኢዮቤል ያእምሩ። <sup>50:4</sup>&nbsp;በእንተዝ ሠራዕኩ ለከ ሱባዔ ዓመታት ወኢዮቤሌዎታተ አርብዓ ወተስዐቱ ኢዮቤሌዎታት እምነ መዋዕሊሁ ለአዳም እስከ ዛቲ ዕለት ወሱባዔ አሐዱ ወክልኤ ዓመታት ወዓዲ አርብዓ ዓመት ርሑቅ ለአእምሮ ትእዛዛተ እግዚአብሔር እስከ አመ ያዐድው ማዕዶተ ምድረ ከናአን ዐዲዎሙ ዮርዳኖስ ገጸ ዐረቢሁ <sup>50:5</sup>&nbsp;ወኢዮቤሌዎታት የኀልፉ እስከ አመ ይነጽሕ እስራኤል እምኵሉ አበሳ ዝሙት ወርኵስ ወግማኔ ወኀጢአት ወጌጋይ ወየኀድር ውስተ ኵሉ ምድር እንዘ ይትአመን ወአልቦ እንከ ሎቱ መነሂ ሰይጣነ ወአልቦ መነሂ እኩየ ወትነጽሕ ምድር እምውእቱ ጊዜ እስከ ኵሉ መዋዕል። 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>50:1</sup>&nbsp;After this law I informed you about the sabbath days in the wilderness of Sin which is between Elim and Sinai. <sup>50:2</sup>&nbsp;On Mt. Sinai I told you about the sabbaths of the land and the years of jubilees in the sabbaths of the years, but its year we have not told you until the time when you enter the land which you will possess. <sup>50:3</sup>&nbsp;The land will observe its sabbaths when they live on it, and they are to know the year of the jubilee. <sup>50:4</sup>&nbsp;For this reason I have arranged for you the weeks of years and the jubilees — 49 jubilees from the time of Adam until today, and one week and two years. It is still 40 years off (for learning the Lord's commandments) until the time when he leads (them) across to the land of Canaan, after they have crossed the Jordan to the west of it. <sup>50:5</sup>&nbsp;The jubilees will pass by until Israel is pure of every sexual evil, impurity, contamination, sin, and error. Then they will live confidently in the entire land. They will no longer have any satan or any evil person. The land will be pure from that time until eternity.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>50:6</sup>&nbsp;ወናሁ ትእዛዘ ሰንበታትኒ ጸሐፍኩ ለከ ወኵሉ ፍትሐተ ሕገጊሁ <sup>50:7</sup>&nbsp;ሰዱሰ ዕለተ ትገብር ግብረ ወአመ ሳብዕት ዕለት ሰንበት ዘእግዚአብሔር አምላክክሙ ኢትግበሩ ባቲ ኵሎ ግብረ አንትሙ ወውሉድክሙ ወአግብርቲክሙ ወአእማቲክሙ ወኵሉ እንስሳክሙ ወነኪርኒ ዘኀቤክሙ። <sup>50:8</sup>&nbsp;ወሰብእ ዘይገብር ምንተሂ ግብረ ባቲ ይሙት ኵሉ ብእሲ ዘይጌምና ለዛ ዕለት ዘይሰክብ ምስለ ብእሲት ወዘሂ ይትናገር ነገረ ምግባር ባቲ ከመ ይግበር ባቲ ገዪሶ ወበእንተኒ ኵሉ ሠዪጥ ወተሣይጦ ወዘሂ ማየ ይቀድሕ ባቲ ዘኢያስተዳለወ ሎቱ በዕለተ ሳድስት ወዘኒ አንሥአ ዘይጸውር ኵሎ ከመ ያውፅእ እምደብተራሁ ወእመኒ እምቤቱ ይሙት። <sup>50:9</sup>&nbsp;ኢትግበሩ ሰንበት ምንተሂ ግብረ ዘኢያስተዳለውክምዎ ለክሙ በዕለተ ሳድስት ለበሊዕ ወለሰቲይ ወለአዕርፎ ወለአሰንብቶ እምኵሉ ግብር በዛቲ ዕለት ወለባርኮ እግዚአብሔር አምላክክሙ። ዘወሀበክሙ ዕለት በዓል ወዕለተ ቅድስተ ወዕለተ መንግሥት ቅድስት ለኵሉ እስራኤል ዛቲ ዕለት በመዋዕሊሆሙ በኵሉ መዋዕል <sup>50:10</sup>&nbsp;እስመ ዐባይ ክብር እንተ ወሀበ እግዚአብሔር ለእስራኤል ለበሊዕ ወለሰቲይ ወለጸጊብ በዛቲ ዕለተ በዓል ወለአዕርፎ ባቲ እምኵሉ ግብር ዘእምግብረ እጓለ እመሕያው ዘእንበለ ዐጢነ ዕጣን ወለአብኦ ቍርባን ወመሥዋዕት ቅድመ እግዚአብሔር ለመዋዕል ወለሰንበታት <sup>50:11</sup>&nbsp;ዝግብር ባሕቲቱ ይትገበር በመዋዕለ ሰንበታት በቤተ መቅደሱ ለእግዚአብሔር አምላክክሙ ከመ ያስተስርዩ ዲበ እስራኤል መባአ ወትረ ዕለተ እምዕለት ለተዝካር ዘይሠጠው ቅድመ እግዚአብሔር ወይትወከፎሙ ለዓለም ዕለተ እምዕለት በከመ ተአዘዝከ 
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>50:6</sup>&nbsp;I have now written for you the sabbath commandments and all the statutes of its laws. <sup>50:7</sup>&nbsp;You will work for six days, but on the seventh day is the sabbath of the Lord your God. Do not do any work on it — you, your children, your male and female servants, all your cattle, or the foreigner who is with you. <sup>50:8</sup>&nbsp;The man who does any work on it is to die. Any man who desecrates this day; who lies with a woman; who says anything about work on it — that he is to set out on a trip on it, or about any selling or buying; who on it draws water which he had not prepared for himself on the sixth day; or who lifts any load to bring (it) outside his tent or his house is to die. <sup>50:9</sup>&nbsp;On the sabbath day do not do any work which you have not prepared for yourself on the sixth day so that you may eat, drink, rest, keep sabbath on this day from all work, and bless the Lord your God who has given you a festal day and a holy day. This day among their days is to be the day of the holy kingdom for all Israel throughout all time. <sup>50:10</sup>&nbsp;For great is the honor which the Lord has given Israel to eat, drink, and be filled on this festal day; and to rest on it from any work that belongs to the work of mankind except to burn incense and to bring before the Lord offerings and sacrifices for the days and the sabbaths. <sup>50:11</sup>&nbsp;Only this (kind of) work is to be done on the sabbath days in the sanctuary of the Lord your God in order that they may atone continuously for Israel with offerings from day to day as a memorial that is acceptable before the Lord; and in order that he may receive them forever, day by day, as you were ordered.
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
<sup>50:12</sup>&nbsp;ወኵሉ ሰብእ ዘይገብር ግብረ ወዘሂ የሐውር መንገደ ወዘሂ ይትቀነይ ወፍረ ወእመሂ በቤቱ ወእመሂ በኵሉ መካን። ወዘሂ ያነድድ እሳተ ወዘሂ ይጼዐን ዲበ ኵሉ እንስሳ። ወዘሂ ይነግድ በሐመር ባሕረ ወኵሉ ሰብእ ዘይዘብጥ ወይቀትል ምንተሂ ወዘሂ የሐርድ እንስሳ ወዖፈ ወዘሂ አሥገረ እመሂ አርዌ ወዖፈ ወእመኒ ዓሣ ወዘሂ ይጸውም ወይገብር ፀብአ በዕለተ ሰንበት <sup>50:13</sup>&nbsp;ወሰብእ ዘይገብር ኵሎ ዘእምዝ በዕለተ ሰንበት ይሙት። ከመ ይኩኑ ውሉደ እስራኤል እንዘ ያሰነብቱ በከመ ትእዛዛተ ሰንበታተ ምድር በከመ ተጽሕፈ እምውስተ ጽላት ዘወሀበኒ ውስተ እደዊየ ከመ እጽሐፍ ለከ ሕገገ ጊዜ ወጊዜ በበ ኩፋሌ መዋዕሊሁ።
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
<sup>50:12</sup>&nbsp;Any man who does work; who goes on a trip; who works farmland whether at his home or in any (other) place; who hghts a fire; who rides any animal; who travels the sea by ship; any man who beats or kills anything; who shts the throat of an animal or bird; who catches either a wild animal, a bird, or a fish; who fasts and makes war on the sabbath day — <sup>50:13</sup>&nbsp;a man who does any of these things on the sabbath day is to die, so that the Israelites may continue observing the sabbath in accord with the commandments for the sabbaths of the land as it was written in the tablets which he placed in my hands so that I could write for you the laws of each specific time in every division of its times».
</div></td></tr>


<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;" width="46%">
<div class="ethiopic"><span lang="am">
ተፈጸመ በዝየ ነገር ዘኩፋሌ መዋዕል።
</span></div></td>
 
<td style="vertical-align:top;" width="53%">
<div class="english">
Here the words regarding the divisions of the times are completed.
</div></td></tr>
</tbody></table>

<hr />

We are grateful to Dr. <a href="http://web.archive.org/web/20160415140645/http://theology.nd.edu:80/people/faculty/james-c-vanderkam/">James VanderKam</a> for preparing this critical text of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Book_of_Jubilees">Book of Jubilees</a> (<em>Sefer haYovelim</em>) in its <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ge'ez_language">Ge'ez</a> translation in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ge'ez_script">Ethiopic script</a>. 

The book of Jubilees is an early Jewish deuterocanonical text composed in Hebrew during the Second Temple period sometime before the Maccabean struggle (ca. 167 BCE). In the introduction to his translation of Jubilees, Dr. VanderKam writes:

<blockquote>The present writer has argued at length that Jubilees was written between 161 and 152, while George Nickelsburg and Jonathan Goldstein have defended a date just before 167 B.C.[E.] on the grounds that the author betrays his knowledge of events that occurred in the first part of Antiochus IV's reign but is not aware of his religious edict which was promulgated in 167....[foot]NICKELSBURG, Jewish Literature Between the Bible and the Mishnah (Philadelphia: Fortress, 1981) 78-79; GOLDSTEIN, «The Date of the Book of Jubilees», PAAJR 50 (1983) 63-86. The apocalypse in Jubilees 23 plays a large part in these two attempts at dating.[/foot] 

Today students of the book agree that it was composed in Hebrew and that from Hebrew it was translated into Greek. It has been suggested...that a Hebrew text also served as the base for a Syriac translation, but it is not certain that there was a full Syriac translation and that, if there was one, it rendered a Hebrew rather than a Greek model. Copies of the Greek version of Jubilees then became the Vorlagen of translations into Latin and Ethiopic.

....The only version which preserves the complete text of Jubilees is the Ethiopic. The book was apparently translated from Greek at an early stage in the development of Ethiopic literature and enjoyed canonical status in the Abyssinian Church.</blockquote>

The English translation here was made by Dr. VanderKam and published in <em>The Book of Jubilees. A Translation</em> (Corpus Scriptorum Christianorum Orientalium 511 Scriptores Aethiopici 88) 1989.[foot]© 1989 by Corpus Scriptorum Christianorum Orientalium.[/foot] For the complete work including textual apparatus and annotation, please consult your local academic library.

Through the frame of a mytho-historical chronicle narrated by an angel, Jubilees (Sefer Yovalim) provides more than a gloss on most of Genesis through the giving of the Torah in Exodus. The unknown author presents a raison d'etre for the giving of the Torah itself in the context of world history, the human condition, and the existence of predation in Nature. It is one of the earliest pedagogical works (if not the earliest) explaining the purpose of Jewish teaching and practice to Jewish readers, in circumscribing the predatory passions that entered the world during the generation of the Flood. It is the earliest Jewish work providing a connection between the celebration of the festival of Shavuot (Pentecost) and the celebration of the giving of the Torah on Mt. Sinai. 

Finally, we are grateful to the Abyssinian Church and its generations of monks for preserving the book of Jubilees until this day.
</body>
